benchmarkData = null; let benchmarkComparison = null; // ?? ?숈뒿 DB ?????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? const LEARNING_DB_KEY = 'storyframe_learning_v1'; const LEARNING_THRESHOLD = 0.92; const MAX_ENTRIES_PER_FIELD = 200; function loadLearningDB() { try { const raw = localStorage.getItem(LEARNING_DB_KEY); if (!raw) return { version: 1, entries: [] }; const parsed = JSON.parse(raw); if (!Array.isArray(parsed.entries)) return { version: 1, entries: [] }; return parsed; } catch { return { version: 1, entries: [] }; } } function saveLearningDB(db) { try { localStorage.setItem(LEARNING_DB_KEY, JSON.stringify(db)); } catch { const trimmed = { version: 1, entries: db.entries.slice(-300) }; try { localStorage.setItem(LEARNING_DB_KEY, JSON.stringify(trimmed)); } catch {} } } function extractFeatureVector(composition, edgeMap, focusAnalysis, colorAnalysis) { const v = []; // 3횞3 ?곸뿭蹂?諛앷린 (0~1), 梨꾨룄 (0~1) = 18李⑥썝 for (let i = 0; i < 9; i++) v.push(composition.regions[i].brightness / 255); for (let i = 0; i < 9; i++) v.push(composition.regions[i].saturation); // 怨듦컙 遺꾪룷 = 5李⑥썝 v.push(composition.centerWeight); v.push(composition.leftWeightRatio); v.push(composition.rightWeightRatio); v.push(Math.min(composition.skinToneRatio * 10, 1)); v.push(composition.avgBrightness); // 珥덉젏 = 3李⑥썝 v.push(Math.min(focusAnalysis.sharpnessRatio / 4, 1)); v.push(Math.min(focusAnalysis.overallSharpness / 40, 1)); v.push(Math.min(focusAnalysis.centerSharpness / 40, 1)); // ?됱긽/?몄텧 = 6李⑥썝 v.push(colorAnalysis.avgBrightness); v.push(colorAnalysis.shadowRatio); v.push(colorAnalysis.highlightRatio); v.push(Math.min(colorAnalysis.vignetting / 3, 1)); v.push(colorAnalysis.warmRatio); v.push(colorAnalysis.coolRatio); v.push(colorAnalysis.avgSaturation || 0); v.push(Math.min((colorAnalysis.lumaStd || 0) * 6, 1)); v.push(Math.min((colorAnalysis.clippedHighlightRatio || 0) * 8, 1)); v.push(Math.min((colorAnalysis.clippedShadowRatio || 0) * 8, 1)); v.push(Math.min(Math.abs((colorAnalysis.leftWarmRatio || 0) - (colorAnalysis.rightWarmRatio || 0)) * 4, 1)); v.push(Math.min(Math.abs((colorAnalysis.leftCoolRatio || 0) - (colorAnalysis.rightCoolRatio || 0)) * 4, 1)); // ?ｌ? = 4李⑥썝 v.push(Math.min(edgeMap.avgEdge / 30, 1)); v.push(edgeMap.axisEnergyRatio); v.push(edgeMap.diagonalEnergyRatio); v.push(edgeMap.axisTilt / 45); // 援щ룄 蹂닿컯 吏??= 10李⑥썝 v.push(composition.visualCentroidX); v.push(composition.visualCentroidY); v.push(composition.centerHotspotWeight); v.push(composition.thirdsHotspotWeight); v.push(composition.goldenHotspotWeight); v.push(composition.verticalSymmetry); v.push(composition.horizontalSymmetry); v.push(composition.emptyRegionRatio); v.push(composition.leftOpenness); v.push(composition.rightOpenness); return v; } function cosineSimilarity(a, b) { if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b)) return 0; const len = Math.min(a.length, b.length); if (!len) return 0; let dot = 0, normA = 0, normB = 0; for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) { dot += a[i] * b[i]; normA += a[i] * a[i]; normB += b[i] * b[i]; } const denom = Math.sqrt(normA) * Math.sqrt(normB); if (!(denom > 0)) return 0; const lengthPenalty = len / Math.max(a.length, b.length, 1); return (dot / denom) * lengthPenalty; } function findLearningMatch(features, field) { const db = loadLearningDB(); const candidates = db.entries.filter(e => e.field === field); if (!candidates.length) return null; let best = null, bestSim = 0; for (const entry of candidates) { const sim = cosineSimilarity(features, entry.features); if (sim > bestSim) { bestSim = sim; best = entry; } } return best && bestSim >= LEARNING_THRESHOLD ? { label: best.label, similarity: bestSim } : null; } function addLearningEntry(field, label, features, videoName) { const db = loadLearningDB(); // ?대? 媛숈? ?꾨뱶??嫄곗쓽 ?숈씪???뱀쭠踰≫꽣媛 ?덉쑝硫???뼱?곌린 const deduped = db.entries.filter(e => { if (e.field !== field) return true; return cosineSimilarity(e.features, features) < 0.98; }); deduped.push({ id: `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`, ts: Date.now(), videoName: videoName || '', field, label, features }); // ?꾨뱶蹂?理쒕? MAX_ENTRIES_PER_FIELD 媛??좎? const perField = {}; for (const e of deduped) { if (!perField[e.field]) perField[e.field] = []; perField[e.field].push(e); } const trimmed = []; for (const f of Object.keys(perField)) { const sorted = perField[f].sort((a, b) => a.ts - b.ts); trimmed.push(...sorted.slice(-MAX_ENTRIES_PER_FIELD)); } db.entries = trimmed; saveLearningDB(db); } function learnFromBenchmarkComparison(rows) { const LEARNABLE = [ { rowKey: 'shotHit', benchKey: 'shotSize', camKey: 'shotSize' }, { rowKey: 'framingHit', benchKey: 'framing', camKey: 'framing' }, { rowKey: 'movementHit', benchKey: 'movement', camKey: 'movement' }, { rowKey: 'lensHit', benchKey: 'lensType', camKey: 'lensType' }, { rowKey: 'angleHit', benchKey: 'angle', camKey: 'angle' }, { rowKey: 'dofHit', benchKey: 'dof', camKey: 'dof' }, { rowKey: 'lightingTypeHit', benchKey: 'lightingType', camKey: 'lightingType' }, { rowKey: 'lightingConditionHit', benchKey: 'lightingCondition', camKey: 'lightingCondition' }, { rowKey: 'compositionHit', benchKey: 'composition', camKey: 'composition' } ]; let learned = 0; for (const row of rows) { if (!row.detectedScene) continue; const features = row.detectedScene.camera?._features; if (!features) continue; for (const f of LEARNABLE) { if (row[f.rowKey] === false) { const correctLabel = row.benchmarkScene[f.benchKey]; if (!correctLabel) continue; addLearningEntry(f.camKey, correctLabel, features, videoFile?.name); learned++; } } } return learned; } function getLearningDBStats() { const db = loadLearningDB(); const byField = {}; for (const e of db.entries) byField[e.field] = (byField[e.field] || 0) + 1; return { total: db.entries.length, byField }; } function clearLearningDB() { if (!confirm(`학습 데이터 ${getLearningDBStats().total}개를 모두 삭제할까요?`)) return; localStorage.removeItem(LEARNING_DB_KEY); showToast('학습 데이터가 모두 삭제됐습니다.'); renderBenchmarkSection(); } function renderLearningStats() { const el = document.getElementById('learningStats'); if (!el) return; const stats = getLearningDBStats(); if (stats.total === 0) { el.innerHTML = '<span style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:12px;">학습 데이터 없음</span>'; return; } const detail = Object.entries(stats.byField) .map(([k, v]) => `${k}:${v}`) .join(' 쨌 '); } // ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Elements const uploadSection = document.getElementById('uploadSection'); function detectEnvironment() { // claude.ai artifacts run inside an iframe on specific domains try { const host = window.location.hostname; // In claude.ai artifact, the API proxy handles auth automatically if (host.includes('claude.ai') || host.includes('anthropic.com') || host === '') { isClaudeAI = true; } } catch(e) { // If we can't access hostname (cross-origin), likely in an iframe = claude.ai isClaudeAI = true; } // Also try a lightweight test updateApiKeyStatus(); } function updateApiKeyStatus() { const statusEl = document.getElementById('apiKeyStatus'); newPlayer.load(); } function readFileAsDataURL(file) { return new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const reader = new FileReader(); reader.onload = () => resolve(reader.result); reader.onerror = () => reject(reader.error || new Error('Failed to read file')); reader.readAsDataURL(file); }); } function loadImageFromSource(src) { return new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const img = new Image(); img.onload = () => resolve(img); img.onerror = () => reject(new Error('Failed to load image')); img.src = src; }); } async function analyzeStillSignature(src) { const img = await loadImageFromSource(src); const targetWidth = 160; const targetHeight = Math.max(1, Math.round(targetWidth * (img.height / img.width))); } async function loadPhoto(file) { currentMediaType = 'photo'; videoFile = file; fileInput.value = ''; const vp = getVideoPlayer(); vp.pause(); vp.removeAttribute('src'); vp.innerHTML = ''; vp.load(); vp.style.display = 'none'; if (videoUrl) { URL.revokeObjectURL(videoUrl); videoUrl = null; } try { showProgress(); updateProgress('Loading photo...', 10); const dataUrl = await readFileAsDataURL(file); const img = await loadImageFromSource(dataUrl); const signature = await analyzeStillSignature(dataUrl); photoPreview.src = dataUrl; photoPreview.style.display = 'block'; videoDuration = 1; scenes = [{ index: 1, startTime: 0, endTime: 1, duration: 1, keyframeTime: 0, image: dataUrl, multiFrames: [dataUrl], transition: 'cut', score: 1, description: '', brightness: signature?.brightness ?? 0.5, colorDominant: signature?.colorDominant || 'Photo' }]; document.getElementById('videoName').textContent = file.name; document.getElementById('videoMeta').textContent = `${img.naturalWidth}x${img.naturalHeight} / PHOTO / ${(file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1)}MB`; uploadSection.style.display = 'none'; workspace.classList.add('active'); headerActions.style.display = 'flex'; updateProgress('Analyzing shot...', 45); scenes[0].camera = await analyzeFrameAdvanced(scenes[0]); scenes[0].description = generateLocalDescription(scenes[0]); renderStoryboard(); hideProgress(); showToast('Photo analysis completed.'); } catch (err) { console.error(err); hideProgress(); showToast(`Photo analysis failed: ${err.message}`); } } // Helper to always get current video player (since we clone it) function getVideoPlayer() { return window._videoPlayer || document.getElementById('videoPlayer'); } function formatTime(sec) { const m = Math.floor(sec / 60); const s = Math.floor(sec % 60); return `${m}:${s.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`; } function formatTimecode(sec) { const h = Math.floor(sec / 3600); const m = Math.floor((sec % 3600) / 60); const s = Math.floor(sec % 60); const f = Math.floor((sec % 1) * 30); return `${h.toString().padStart(2,'0')}:${m.toString().padStart(2,'0')}:${s.toString().padStart(2,'0')}:${f.toString().padStart(2,'0')}`; } function clamp(value, min, max) { return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max); } function percentile(values, rank) { if (!values.length) return 0; const sorted = [...values].sort((a, b) => a - b); const idx = clamp((rank / 100) * (sorted.length - 1), 0, sorted.length - 1); const low = Math.floor(idx); const high = Math.ceil(idx); if (low === high) return sorted[low]; const t = idx - low; return sorted[low] * (1 - t) + sorted[high] * t; } function summarizeValues(values) { if (!values.length) return { mean: 0, std: 0 }; const mean = values.reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0) / values.length; const variance = values.reduce((sum, value) => sum + Math.pow(value - mean, 2), 0) / values.length; return { mean, std: Math.sqrt(variance) }; } const BENCHMARK_OPTIONS = { transitions: [ '', /* 而?怨꾩뿴 */ 'cut', 'match-cut', 'action-cut', 'jump-cut', 'smash-cut', 'cross-cut', 'graphic-cut', 'flash', /* ?붿「釉??섏씠??*/ 'dissolve', 'match-dissolve', 'fade', 'fade-white', 'defocus', /* ??댄봽/臾대툕 */ 'wipe', 'iris', 'whip-pan', 'zoom', /* ?ㅻ뵒??*/ 'l-cut', 'j-cut', ], shotSizes: ['', 'ECU', 'BCU', 'CU', 'MCU', 'MS', 'Cowboy', 'MLS', 'FS', 'LS', 'ELS', 'Establishing', 'INSERT'], framings: ['', 'Single', 'Two-shot', 'Three-shot', 'OTS', 'POV', 'Crowd', 'Empty'], movements: ['', 'Static', 'Pan', 'Whip-pan', 'Tilt', 'Push-in', 'Pull-out', 'Tracking', 'Trucking', 'Arc', 'Crane', 'Pedestal', 'Handheld', 'Steadicam', 'Zoom-in', 'Zoom-out', 'Dolly-zoom', 'Rack-focus', 'Drone'] }; function escapeHtml(value) { return String(value ?? '') .replace(/&/g, '&') .replace(/</g, '<') .replace(/>/g, '>') .replace(/"/g, '"') .replace(/'/g, '''); } function matchOption(value, options) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const found = options.find(option => option.toLowerCase() === raw.toLowerCase()); return found || raw; } const TRANSITION_LABELS = { 'cut': 'CUT', 'match-cut': 'MATCH CUT', 'action-cut': 'ACT. CUT', 'jump-cut': 'JUMP CUT', 'smash-cut': 'SMASH', 'cross-cut': 'CROSS', 'graphic-cut': 'GRAPHIC', 'flash': 'FLASH', 'dissolve': 'DISSOLVE', 'match-dissolve':'M. DSLV', 'fade': 'FADE', 'fade-white': 'FADE W', 'defocus': 'DEFOCUS', 'wipe': 'WIPE', 'iris': 'IRIS', 'whip-pan': 'WHIP PAN', 'zoom': 'ZOOM', 'l-cut': 'L-CUT', 'j-cut': 'J-CUT', }; const TRANSITION_KO = { '': 'Not specified', 'cut': 'Cut transition', 'match-cut': 'Match cut', 'action-cut': 'Action cut', 'jump-cut': 'Jump cut', 'smash-cut': 'Smash cut', 'cross-cut': 'Cross cut', 'graphic-cut': 'Graphic cut', 'flash': 'Flash cut', 'dissolve': 'Dissolve transition', 'match-dissolve':'Match dissolve', 'fade': 'Fade transition', 'fade-white': 'Fade to white', 'defocus': 'Defocus transition', 'wipe': 'Wipe transition', 'iris': 'Iris transition', 'whip-pan': 'Whip pan transition', 'zoom': 'Zoom transition', 'l-cut': 'L-cut', 'j-cut': 'J-cut', }; function canonicalTransition(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase(); if (!raw) return ''; if (raw.includes('match') && raw.includes('dissolve')) return 'match-dissolve'; if (raw.includes('graphic') || (raw.includes('match') && raw.includes('cut'))) return 'match-cut'; if (raw.includes('jump')) return 'jump-cut'; if (raw.includes('smash')) return 'smash-cut'; if (raw.includes('action cut') || raw.includes('cut on action') || raw === 'action') return 'action-cut'; if (raw.includes('cross') || raw.includes('parallel') || raw.includes('intercut')) return 'cross-cut'; if (raw.includes('flash') && !raw.includes('back') && !raw.includes('forward')) return 'flash'; if (raw.includes('whip') || raw.includes('swish') || raw.includes('swipe pan')) return 'whip-pan'; if (raw.includes('zoom')) return 'zoom'; if (raw.includes('iris')) return 'iris'; if (raw.includes('wipe') || (raw.includes('push') && raw.includes('transition'))) return 'wipe'; if (raw.includes('dissolve') || raw.includes('crossfade') || raw.includes('cross fade')) return 'dissolve'; if (raw.includes('defocus') || raw.includes('blur tran')) return 'defocus'; if (raw.includes('fade') && (raw.includes('white') || raw.includes('bright'))) return 'fade-white'; if (raw.includes('fade')) return 'fade'; if (raw.includes('l-cut') || raw === 'l cut' || raw.includes('audio advance')) return 'l-cut'; if (raw.includes('j-cut') || raw === 'j cut' || raw.includes('audio delay')) return 'j-cut'; return 'cut'; } function canonicalShotSize(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase(); const aliasMap = { ews: 'ELS', ws: 'LS', 'wide shot': 'LS', 'long shot': 'LS', 'extreme long shot': 'ELS', 'establishing shot': 'Establishing', 'extreme close-up': 'ECU', 'big close-up': 'BCU', 'close-up': 'CU', 'medium close-up': 'MCU', 'medium shot': 'MS', 'american shot': 'Cowboy', 'cowboy shot': 'Cowboy', 'medium long shot': 'MLS', 'full shot': 'FS', 'full figure': 'FS' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.shotSizes); } function canonicalFraming(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase(); const aliasMap = { 'over-the-shoulder': 'OTS', 'over the shoulder': 'OTS', pov: 'POV', 'point of view': 'POV', crowd: 'Crowd', empty: 'Empty', single: 'Single' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.framings); } function canonicalMovement(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase(); const aliasMap = { static: 'Static', 'slight move': 'Static', 'dolly/tracking': 'Tracking', tracking: 'Tracking', trucking: 'Trucking', truck: 'Trucking', arc: 'Arc', pedestal: 'Pedestal', crane: 'Crane', handheld: 'Handheld', steadicam: 'Steadicam', gimbal: 'Steadicam', pan: 'Pan', tilt: 'Tilt', 'push in': 'Push-in', 'pull out': 'Pull-out', 'zoom in': 'Zoom-in', 'zoom out': 'Zoom-out', 'dolly zoom': 'Dolly-zoom', 'whip pan': 'Whip-pan' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.movements); } function parseTimecodeInput(value) { if (typeof value === 'number' && Number.isFinite(value)) return value; const text = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!text) return null; if (/^\d+(\.\d+)?$/.test(text)) return parseFloat(text); const parts = text.split(':').map(part => part.trim()); if (parts.length < 2 || parts.length > 4 || parts.some(part => part === '' || Number.isNaN(Number(part)))) { return null; } const nums = parts.map(Number); if (parts.length === 4) { const [h, m, s, f] = nums; return h * 3600 + m * 60 + s + f / 30; } if (parts.length === 3) { const [h, m, s] = nums; return h * 3600 + m * 60 + s; } const [m, s] = nums; return m * 60 + s; } function coerceBenchmarkTime(value, fallback = 0) { const parsed = parseTimecodeInput(value); if (parsed === null || !Number.isFinite(parsed)) return fallback; const maxDuration = videoDuration || Math.max(parsed, fallback, 1); return clamp(parsed, 0, maxDuration); } function renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(options, selectedValue) { return options.map(option => { const selected = option === selectedValue ? ' selected' : ''; const label = option || 'Not specified'; return `<option value="${escapeHtml(option)}"${selected}>${escapeHtml(label)}</option>`; }).join(''); } function getSceneCanonicalValue(scene, field) { if (!scene) return ''; if (field === 'transition') return canonicalTransition(scene.transition); if (field === 'shotSize') return canonicalShotSize(scene.camera?.shotSize); if (field === 'framing') return canonicalFraming(scene.camera?.framing); if (field === 'movement') return canonicalMovement(scene.camera?.movement); return ''; } function buildBenchmarkSceneFromScene(scene, index) { return { id: `bench-${Date.now()}-${index + 1}`, index: index + 1, startTime: scene.startTime, endTime: scene.endTime, transition: canonicalTransition(scene.transition), shotSize: canonicalShotSize(scene.camera?.shotSize), framing: canonicalFraming(scene.camera?.framing), movement: canonicalMovement(scene.camera?.movement), notes: '' }; } function normalizeBenchmarkScene(scene, index) { const startTime = coerceBenchmarkTime(scene.startTime ?? scene.start ?? 0, 0); const rawEnd = scene.endTime ?? scene.end ?? startTime; const endTime = Math.max(coerceBenchmarkTime(rawEnd, startTime), startTime); return { id: scene.id || `bench-${Date.now()}-${index + 1}`, index: index + 1, startTime, endTime, transition: canonicalTransition(scene.transition), shotSize: canonicalShotSize(scene.shotSize ?? scene.shot_size), framing: canonicalFraming(scene.framing), movement: canonicalMovement(scene.movement ?? scene.camera_movement), notes: String(scene.notes ?? scene.note ?? '') }; } function reindexBenchmarkScenes() { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes) return; benchmarkData.scenes = benchmarkData.scenes.map((scene, index) => ({ ...scene, index: index + 1 })); } function getBenchmarkTolerance() { return Math.max(0.05, Number(benchmarkData?.scoring?.boundaryToleranceSec) || 0.35); } function metricPercent(metric) { if (!metric || !metric.total) return '-'; return `${Math.round((metric.hits / metric.total) * 100)}%`; } function metricNote(metric) { if (!metric || !metric.total) return 'n/a'; return `${metric.hits}/${metric.total}`; } function createBenchmarkFromCurrent() { if (!scenes.length) { showToast('먼저 스토리보드를 생성해주세요.'); return; } const now = new Date().toISOString(); benchmarkData = { version: 1, createdAt: now, updatedAt: now, video: { name: videoFile?.name || '', duration: videoDuration }, scoring: { boundaryToleranceSec: 0.35 }, scenes: scenes.map((scene, index) => buildBenchmarkSceneFromScene(scene, index)) }; benchmarkComparison = null; renderBenchmarkSection(); compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); showToast('현재 감지 결과를 벤치마크 초안으로 만들었습니다.'); } function triggerBenchmarkImport() { benchmarkFileInput.click(); } function normalizeBenchmarkData(payload) { const scenesInput = Array.isArray(payload?.scenes) ? payload.scenes : []; return { version: Number(payload?.version) || 1, createdAt: payload?.createdAt || new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(), video: { name: String(payload?.video?.name || videoFile?.name || ''), duration: Number(payload?.video?.duration) || videoDuration || 0 }, scoring: { boundaryToleranceSec: Math.max(0.05, Number(payload?.scoring?.boundaryToleranceSec) || 0.35) }, scenes: scenesInput.map((scene, index) => normalizeBenchmarkScene(scene, index)) }; } function learnFromBenchmarkDiff() { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { showToast('현재 감지 결과를 벤치마크 초안으로 만들었습니다.'); return 0; } if (!scenes.length) { showToast('먼저 스토리보드를 생성해주세요.'); return 0; } const FIELD_MAP = [ { benchKey: 'shotSize', camKey: 'shotSize', canon: canonicalShotSize }, { benchKey: 'framing', camKey: 'framing', canon: canonicalFraming }, { benchKey: 'movement', camKey: 'movement', canon: canonicalMovement }, { benchKey: 'lensType', camKey: 'lensType', canon: canonicalLensType }, { benchKey: 'angle', camKey: 'angle', canon: canonicalAngle }, { benchKey: 'dof', camKey: 'dof', canon: canonicalDOF }, { benchKey: 'lightingType', camKey: 'lightingType', canon: canonicalLightingType }, { benchKey: 'lightingCondition', camKey: 'lightingCondition', canon: canonicalLightingCondition }, { benchKey: 'composition', camKey: 'composition', canon: canonicalComposition } ]; const usedIndices = new Set(); let learnedCount = 0; for (const bScene of benchmarkData.scenes) { const match = findBestDetectedSceneMatch(bScene, scenes, usedIndices); if (!match?.scene) continue; usedIndices.add(match.detectedIndex); const dScene = match.scene; const features = dScene.camera?._features; if (!features) continue; for (const f of FIELD_MAP) { const correctLabel = f.canon(bScene[f.benchKey]); const detectedLabel = f.canon(dScene.camera?.[f.camKey]); if (!correctLabel) continue; if (correctLabel !== detectedLabel) { addLearningEntry(f.camKey, correctLabel, features, videoFile?.name); learnedCount++; } } } renderLearningStats(); return learnedCount; } function learnOnly() { const count = learnFromBenchmarkDiff(); if (count > 0) { showToast(`✨ ${count}개 장면 학습 완료 (전체 ${getLearningDBStats().total}개)`); } else { showToast('학습 이력이 없습니다. 벤치마크에서 장면을 설정해주세요.'); } } function exportBenchmark() { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { showToast('내보낼 벤치마크가 없습니다.'); return; } const learnedCount = learnFromBenchmarkDiff(); benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); const baseName = (videoFile?.name || benchmarkData.video.name || 'storyframe') .replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '') .replace(/[^\\w\\-]+/g, '_'); downloadBlob( JSON.stringify(benchmarkData, null, 2), `${baseName}_benchmark.json`, 'application/json' ); const msg = learnedCount > 0 ? `JSON 저장 완료 · ${learnedCount}개 장면 학습됨 (전체 ${getLearningDBStats().total}개)` : 'JSON 저장 완료'; showToast(msg); } function addBenchmarkScene() { if (!benchmarkData) { createBenchmarkFromCurrent(); return; } const last = benchmarkData.scenes[benchmarkData.scenes.length - 1]; const startTime = last ? Math.min(last.endTime, videoDuration || last.endTime) : 0; const endTime = Math.min(startTime + 1, videoDuration || startTime + 1); benchmarkData.scenes.push(normalizeBenchmarkScene({ startTime, endTime: Math.max(endTime, startTime), transition: 'cut', shotSize: '', framing: '', movement: '', notes: '' }, benchmarkData.scenes.length)); benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); reindexBenchmarkScenes(); renderBenchmarkSection(); if (scenes.length) compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); } function deleteBenchmarkScene(index) { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.[index]) return; benchmarkData.scenes.splice(index, 1); benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); reindexBenchmarkScenes(); benchmarkComparison = null; renderBenchmarkSection(); if (benchmarkData.scenes.length && scenes.length) compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); } function updateBenchmarkTolerance(value) { if (!benchmarkData) return; const parsed = parseFloat(value); if (!Number.isFinite(parsed) || parsed <= 0) { renderBenchmarkSection(); return; } benchmarkData.scoring.boundaryToleranceSec = Math.max(0.05, parsed); benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); if (scenes.length) compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); else renderBenchmarkSection(); } function updateBenchmarkSceneField(index, field, value) { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.[index]) return; const scene = benchmarkData.scenes[index]; if (field === 'startTime' || field === 'endTime') { const parsed = parseTimecodeInput(value); if (parsed === null) { showToast('시간 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.'); renderBenchmarkSection(); return; } scene[field] = clamp(parsed, 0, videoDuration || parsed); if (scene.endTime < scene.startTime) scene.endTime = scene.startTime; } else if (field === 'transition') { scene.transition = canonicalTransition(value); } else if (field === 'shotSize') { scene.shotSize = canonicalShotSize(value); } else if (field === 'framing') { scene.framing = canonicalFraming(value); } else if (field === 'movement') { scene.movement = canonicalMovement(value); } else if (field === 'notes') { scene.notes = String(value ?? ''); } benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); if (scenes.length) compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); else renderBenchmarkSection(); } function findBestDetectedSceneMatch(targetScene, detectedScenes, usedIndices) { let best = null; detectedScenes.forEach((scene, detectedIndex) => { if (usedIndices.has(detectedIndex)) return; const overlap = Math.max(0, Math.min(targetScene.endTime, scene.endTime) - Math.max(targetScene.startTime, scene.startTime)); const benchDuration = Math.max(targetScene.endTime - targetScene.startTime, 0.01); const detectedDuration = Math.max(scene.endTime - scene.startTime, 0.01); const overlapRatio = overlap / Math.max(benchDuration, detectedDuration); const startError = Math.abs(scene.startTime - targetScene.startTime); const endError = Math.abs(scene.endTime - targetScene.endTime); const score = overlapRatio * 5 - (startError + endError) * 0.65 - (overlap <= 0 ? 0.45 : 0); if (!best || score > best.score) { best = { scene, detectedIndex, score, overlapRatio, startError, endError }; } }); if (best) return best; detectedScenes.forEach((scene, detectedIndex) => { const startError = Math.abs(scene.startTime - targetScene.startTime); const endError = Math.abs(scene.endTime - targetScene.endTime); const score = -startError - endError; if (!best || score > best.score) { best = { scene, detectedIndex, score, overlapRatio: 0, startError, endError }; } }); return best; } function compareLabeledField(metric, expected, actual, canonicalize, metrics) { const normalizedExpected = canonicalize(expected); if (!normalizedExpected) return null; metrics[metric].total++; const hit = canonicalize(actual) === normalizedExpected; if (hit) metrics[metric].hits++; return hit; } function compareCurrentToBenchmark(showNotification = true) { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { if (showNotification) showToast('현재 감지 결과를 벤치마크 초안으로 만들었습니다.'); return; } if (!scenes.length) { if (showNotification) showToast('비교할 스토리보드 결과가 없습니다.'); return; } const tolerance = getBenchmarkTolerance(); const usedIndices = new Set(); const metrics = { boundary: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, transition: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, shot: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, framing: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, movement: { hits: 0, total: 0 } }; const rows = benchmarkData.scenes.map((benchmarkScene, rowIndex) => { const match = findBestDetectedSceneMatch(benchmarkScene, scenes, usedIndices); const detectedScene = match?.scene || null; if (match?.detectedIndex !== undefined) usedIndices.add(match.detectedIndex); const startError = detectedScene ? Math.abs(detectedScene.startTime - benchmarkScene.startTime) : null; const endError = detectedScene ? Math.abs(detectedScene.endTime - benchmarkScene.endTime) : null; metrics.boundary.total++; const boundaryHit = !!detectedScene && startError <= tolerance && endError <= tolerance; if (boundaryHit) metrics.boundary.hits++; const transitionHit = compareLabeledField('transition', benchmarkScene.transition, detectedScene?.transition, canonicalTransition, metrics); const shotHit = compareLabeledField('shot', benchmarkScene.shotSize, detectedScene?.camera?.shotSize, canonicalShotSize, metrics); const framingHit = compareLabeledField('framing', benchmarkScene.framing, detectedScene?.camera?.framing, canonicalFraming, metrics); const movementHit = compareLabeledField('movement', benchmarkScene.movement, detectedScene?.camera?.movement, canonicalMovement, metrics); const checks = [boundaryHit, transitionHit, shotHit, framingHit, movementHit].filter(value => value !== null); const hits = checks.filter(Boolean).length; const misses = checks.length - hits; const status = !detectedScene ? 'bad' : misses === 0 ? 'ok' : misses <= 2 ? 'warn' : 'bad'; return { benchmarkScene, detectedScene, rowIndex, overlapRatio: match?.overlapRatio ?? 0, startError, endError, boundaryHit, transitionHit, shotHit, framingHit, movementHit, status }; }); const availableMetrics = Object.values(metrics).filter(metric => metric.total > 0); const overall = availableMetrics.length ? availableMetrics.reduce((sum, metric) => sum + metric.hits / metric.total, 0) / availableMetrics.length : 0; benchmarkComparison = { generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(), tolerance, rows, metrics, overall, sceneCountDiff: scenes.length - benchmarkData.scenes.length, unmatchedDetected: scenes.filter((_, index) => !usedIndices.has(index)) }; renderBenchmarkSection(); if (showNotification) { showToast(`벤치마크 비교 완료 · overall ${Math.round(overall * 100)}%`); } } function renderBenchmarkCompareCell(row) { if (!row?.detectedScene) { return `<div class="benchmark-compare"> <div class="benchmark-status bad">Mismatch</div> <div>No detected scene matched this benchmark row.</div> </div>`; } const lines = [ `<div class="benchmark-status ${row.status}">${row.status === 'ok' ? 'Match' : row.status === 'warn' ? 'Partial' : 'Mismatch'}</div>`, `<div><strong>Detected Scene</strong> SCENE ${row.detectedScene.index}</div>`, `<div><strong>Boundary Error</strong> ${row.startError.toFixed(2)}s / ${row.endError.toFixed(2)}s</div>` ]; if (row.benchmarkScene.shotSize) { lines.push(`<div><strong>??/strong> ${escapeHtml(row.benchmarkScene.shotSize)} ??${escapeHtml(canonicalShotSize(row.detectedScene.camera?.shotSize) || '-')}</div>`); } if (row.benchmarkScene.framing) { lines.push(`<div><strong>?꾨젅?대컢</strong> ${escapeHtml(row.benchmarkScene.framing)} ??${escapeHtml(canonicalFraming(row.detectedScene.camera?.framing) || '-')}</div>`); } if (row.benchmarkScene.movement) { lines.push(`<div><strong>臾대튃</strong> ${escapeHtml(row.benchmarkScene.movement)} ??${escapeHtml(canonicalMovement(row.detectedScene.camera?.movement) || '-')}</div>`); } return `<div class="benchmark-compare">${lines.join('')}</div>`; } function renderBenchmarkSummary() { const summaryEl = document.getElementById('benchmarkSummary'); const tolerance = benchmarkData ? getBenchmarkTolerance() : 0.35; if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { summaryEl.innerHTML = ` <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Detected Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${scenes.length}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Current storyboard output</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Benchmark Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">0</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">No ground truth yet</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Tolerance</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${tolerance.toFixed(2)}s</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Boundary tolerance</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Video</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${formatTime(videoDuration)}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${escapeHtml(videoFile?.name || '')}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Status</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">Draft</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Create a draft and adjust the rows</div> </div>`; return; } const metrics = benchmarkComparison?.metrics; summaryEl.innerHTML = ` <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Benchmark Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${benchmarkData.scenes.length}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${escapeHtml(benchmarkData.video?.name || videoFile?.name || '')}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Detected Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${scenes.length}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Diff ${benchmarkComparison ? benchmarkComparison.sceneCountDiff : scenes.length - benchmarkData.scenes.length}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Boundary</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? metricPercent(metrics.boundary) : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? metricNote(metrics.boundary) : 'Before compare'} / tol ${tolerance.toFixed(2)}s</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Shot / Lens</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? `${metricPercent(metrics.shot)} / ${metricPercent(metrics.lens)}` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? `${metricNote(metrics.shot)} / ${metricNote(metrics.lens)}` : 'Before compare'}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Move / Angle</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? `${metricPercent(metrics.movement)} / ${metricPercent(metrics.angle)}` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? `${metricNote(metrics.movement)} / ${metricNote(metrics.angle)}` : 'Before compare'}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">DOF / Light</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? `${metricPercent(metrics.dof)} / ${metricPercent(metrics.lightingCondition)}` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? `type ${metricPercent(metrics.lightingType)} / comp ${metricPercent(metrics.composition)}` : 'Before compare'}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Overall</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${benchmarkComparison ? `${Math.round(benchmarkComparison.overall * 100)}%` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${benchmarkComparison ? `framing ${metricPercent(metrics.framing)} / transition ${metricPercent(metrics.transition)}` : 'Not compared yet'}</div> </div>`; } function renderBenchmarkTable() { const body = document.getElementById('benchmarkTableBody'); if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { body.innerHTML = ''; return; } body.innerHTML = benchmarkData.scenes.map((scene, index) => { const comparisonRow = benchmarkComparison?.rows?.[index]; return ` <tr class="benchmark-row" data-status="${comparisonRow?.status || 'neutral'}"> <td> <div style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:8px;">S${index + 1}</div> <button class="btn" style="padding:5px 8px;font-size:11px;" onclick="deleteBenchmarkScene(${index})">??젣</button> </td> <td> <input class="benchmark-input" value="${escapeHtml(formatTimecode(scene.startTime))}" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'startTime', this.value)"> </td> <td> <input class="benchmark-input" value="${escapeHtml(formatTimecode(scene.endTime))}" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'endTime', this.value)"> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'transition', this.value)"> ${BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.transitions.map(t => { const sel = t === scene.transition ? ' selected' : ''; return `<option value="${escapeHtml(t)}"${sel}>${escapeHtml((TRANSITION_KO[t] ?? t) || 'Not specified')}</option>`; }).join('')} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'shotSize', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.shotSizes, scene.shotSize)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'framing', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.framings, scene.framing)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'movement', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.movements, scene.movement)} </select> </td> <td>${renderBenchmarkCompareCell(comparisonRow)}</td> <td> <textarea class="benchmark-textarea" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'notes', this.value)">${escapeHtml(scene.notes)}</textarea> </td> </tr>`; }).join(''); } function renderBenchmarkSection() { const section = document.getElementById('benchmarkSection'); const emptyEl = document.getElementById('benchmarkEmpty'); const toolbar = document.getElementById('benchmarkToolbar'); const tableWrap = document.getElementById('benchmarkTableWrap'); const metaEl = document.getElementById('benchmarkMeta'); const compareBtn = document.getElementById('benchmarkCompareBtn'); const exportBtn = document.getElementById('benchmarkExportBtn'); const learnBtn = document.getElementById('benchmarkLearnBtn'); const headerBtn = document.getElementById('headerBenchmarkBtn'); const visible = scenes.length > 0 || !!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length; section.style.display = visible ? 'block' : 'none'; headerBtn.style.display = visible ? 'inline-flex' : 'none'; compareBtn.disabled = !benchmarkData?.scenes?.length || !scenes.length; exportBtn.disabled = !benchmarkData?.scenes?.length; if (learnBtn) learnBtn.disabled = !benchmarkData?.scenes?.length || !scenes.length; renderBenchmarkSummary(); if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { emptyEl.style.display = 'block'; toolbar.style.display = 'none'; tableWrap.style.display = 'none'; return; } emptyEl.style.display = 'none'; toolbar.style.display = 'flex'; tableWrap.style.display = 'block'; metaEl.innerHTML = ` 踰ㅼ튂留덊겕 ${benchmarkData.scenes.length}媛??λ㈃ 쨌 寃쎄퀎 ?덉슜 ?ㅼ감 <input class="benchmark-input" id="benchmarkToleranceInput" type="number" min="0.05" step="0.05" value="${getBenchmarkTolerance().toFixed(2)}" style="width:84px;display:inline-block;margin:0 6px;" onchange="updateBenchmarkTolerance(this.value)">珥? <button class="btn" style="padding:5px 10px;font-size:11px;margin-left:8px;" onclick="addBenchmarkScene()">竊???異붽?</button> `; renderBenchmarkTable(); } function scrollToBenchmark() { const el = document.getElementById('benchmarkSection'); if (el && el.style.display !== 'none') { el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' }); } } Object.assign(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS, { lensTypes: ['', 'Ultra-wide(<16mm)', 'Wide(16-35mm)', 'Normal(35-60mm)', 'Telephoto(60-135mm)', 'Super-telephoto(>135mm)', 'Macro'], angles: ['', 'Overhead', 'High', 'Eye-level', 'Shoulder-level', 'Low', 'Worms-eye', 'Dutch', 'Aerial'], dofs: ['', 'Deep', 'Moderate', 'Shallow', 'Very-shallow'], lightingTypes: ['', 'Natural', 'Artificial', 'Mixed', 'Practical'], lightingConditions: ['', 'High-key', 'Low-key', 'Silhouette', 'Chiaroscuro', 'Flat', 'Rembrandt'], compositions: ['', 'Rule-of-thirds', 'Center-framed', 'Symmetrical', 'Leading-lines', 'Frame-within-frame', 'Negative-space', 'Golden-ratio'] }); function optionListWithSelected(options, selectedValue) { const selected = String(selectedValue ?? '').trim(); if (!selected) return options; return options.some(option => option.toLowerCase() === selected.toLowerCase()) ? options : [...options, selected]; } function canonicalLensType(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, ' '); if ((key.includes('ultra') || key.includes('super wide')) && key.includes('wide')) return 'Ultra-wide(<16mm)'; if (key.includes('super') && key.includes('tele')) return 'Super-telephoto(>135mm)'; if (key === 'wide' || key.includes('wide angle') || key.includes('wide-angle')) return 'Wide(16-35mm)'; if (key === 'normal' || key === 'standard' || key.includes('standard lens')) return 'Normal(35-60mm)'; if (key === 'tele' || key === 'telephoto' || key.includes('portrait lens')) return 'Telephoto(60-135mm)'; if (key.includes('macro') || key.includes('close focus')) return 'Macro'; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.lensTypes); } function canonicalAngle(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, ' '); const aliasMap = { overhead: 'Overhead', 'birds-eye': 'Overhead', "bird's-eye": 'Overhead', 'birds eye': 'Overhead', "bird's eye": 'Overhead', high: 'High', 'high angle': 'High', 'eye level': 'Eye-level', eyelevel: 'Eye-level', 'shoulder level': 'Shoulder-level', low: 'Low', 'low angle': 'Low', 'worms eye': 'Worms-eye', "worm's eye": 'Worms-eye', dutch: 'Dutch', 'dutch angle': 'Dutch', aerial: 'Aerial', drone: 'Aerial' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.angles); } function canonicalDOF(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, ' '); const aliasMap = { deep: 'Deep', 'deep focus': 'Deep', moderate: 'Moderate', medium: 'Moderate', 'medium dof': 'Moderate', shallow: 'Shallow', 'shallow focus': 'Shallow', 'very shallow': 'Very-shallow', 'very-shallow': 'Very-shallow', 'extremely shallow': 'Very-shallow' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.dofs); } function canonicalLightingType(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, ' '); const aliasMap = { natural: 'Natural', daylight: 'Natural', sunlight: 'Natural', practical: 'Practical', 'practical light': 'Practical', artificial: 'Artificial', studio: 'Artificial', mixed: 'Mixed', 'mixed lighting': 'Mixed' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.lightingTypes); } function canonicalLightingCondition(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, ' '); const aliasMap = { flat: 'Flat', silhouette: 'Silhouette', 'high key': 'High-key', 'high-key': 'High-key', 'low key': 'Low-key', 'low-key': 'Low-key', chiaroscuro: 'Chiaroscuro', rembrandt: 'Rembrandt' }; if (aliasMap[key]) return aliasMap[key]; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.lightingConditions); } function canonicalComposition(value) { const raw = String(value ?? '').trim(); if (!raw) return ''; const key = raw.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, ' '); if (key.includes('golden')) return 'Golden-ratio'; if (key.includes('frame within')) return 'Frame-within-frame'; if (key.includes('negative')) return 'Negative-space'; if (key.includes('leading')) return 'Leading-lines'; if (key.includes('symmet')) return 'Symmetrical'; if (key.includes('center')) return 'Center-framed'; if (key.includes('third')) return 'Rule-of-thirds'; return matchOption(raw, BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.compositions); } function renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(options, selectedValue) { const normalizedSelected = String(selectedValue ?? '').trim().toLowerCase(); return optionListWithSelected(options, selectedValue).map(option => { const selected = option.toLowerCase() === normalizedSelected ? ' selected' : ''; const label = option || '-'; return `<option value="${escapeHtml(option)}"${selected}>${escapeHtml(label)}</option>`; }).join(''); } function getSceneCanonicalValue(scene, field) { if (!scene) return ''; if (field === 'transition') return canonicalTransition(scene.transition); if (field === 'shotSize') return canonicalShotSize(scene.camera?.shotSize); if (field === 'framing') return canonicalFraming(scene.camera?.framing); if (field === 'movement') return canonicalMovement(scene.camera?.movement); if (field === 'lensType') return canonicalLensType(scene.camera?.lensType); if (field === 'angle') return canonicalAngle(scene.camera?.angle); if (field === 'dof') return canonicalDOF(scene.camera?.dof); if (field === 'lightingType') return canonicalLightingType(scene.camera?.lightingType); if (field === 'lightingCondition') return canonicalLightingCondition(scene.camera?.lightingCondition); if (field === 'composition') return canonicalComposition(scene.camera?.composition); return ''; } function buildBenchmarkSceneFromScene(scene, index) { return { id: `bench-${Date.now()}-${index + 1}`, index: index + 1, startTime: scene.startTime, endTime: scene.endTime, transition: canonicalTransition(scene.transition), shotSize: canonicalShotSize(scene.camera?.shotSize), framing: canonicalFraming(scene.camera?.framing), movement: canonicalMovement(scene.camera?.movement), lensType: canonicalLensType(scene.camera?.lensType), angle: canonicalAngle(scene.camera?.angle), dof: canonicalDOF(scene.camera?.dof), lightingType: canonicalLightingType(scene.camera?.lightingType), lightingCondition: canonicalLightingCondition(scene.camera?.lightingCondition), composition: canonicalComposition(scene.camera?.composition), notes: '' }; } function normalizeBenchmarkScene(scene, index) { const startTime = coerceBenchmarkTime(scene.startTime ?? scene.start ?? 0, 0); const rawEnd = scene.endTime ?? scene.end ?? startTime; const endTime = Math.max(coerceBenchmarkTime(rawEnd, startTime), startTime); return { id: scene.id || `bench-${Date.now()}-${index + 1}`, index: index + 1, startTime, endTime, transition: canonicalTransition(scene.transition), shotSize: canonicalShotSize(scene.shotSize ?? scene.shot_size ?? scene.camera?.shotSize), framing: canonicalFraming(scene.framing ?? scene.camera?.framing), movement: canonicalMovement(scene.movement ?? scene.camera_movement ?? scene.camera?.movement), lensType: canonicalLensType(scene.lensType ?? scene.lens_type ?? scene.camera?.lensType), angle: canonicalAngle(scene.angle ?? scene.camera_angle ?? scene.camera?.angle), dof: canonicalDOF(scene.dof ?? scene.depth_of_field ?? scene.camera?.dof), lightingType: canonicalLightingType(scene.lightingType ?? scene.lighting_type ?? scene.camera?.lightingType), lightingCondition: canonicalLightingCondition(scene.lightingCondition ?? scene.lighting_condition ?? scene.camera?.lightingCondition), composition: canonicalComposition(scene.composition ?? scene.composition_tag ?? scene.camera?.composition), notes: String(scene.notes ?? scene.note ?? '') }; } function addBenchmarkScene() { if (!benchmarkData) { createBenchmarkFromCurrent(); return; } const last = benchmarkData.scenes[benchmarkData.scenes.length - 1]; const startTime = last ? Math.min(last.endTime, videoDuration || last.endTime) : 0; const endTime = Math.min(startTime + 1, videoDuration || startTime + 1); benchmarkData.scenes.push(normalizeBenchmarkScene({ startTime, endTime: Math.max(endTime, startTime), transition: 'cut', shotSize: '', framing: '', movement: '', lensType: '', angle: '', dof: '', lightingType: '', lightingCondition: '', composition: '', notes: '' }, benchmarkData.scenes.length)); benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); reindexBenchmarkScenes(); renderBenchmarkSection(); if (scenes.length) compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); } function updateBenchmarkSceneField(index, field, value) { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.[index]) return; const scene = benchmarkData.scenes[index]; if (field === 'startTime' || field === 'endTime') { const parsed = parseTimecodeInput(value); if (parsed === null) { showToast('Invalid timecode. Use HH:MM:SS:FF or seconds.'); renderBenchmarkSection(); return; } scene[field] = clamp(parsed, 0, videoDuration || parsed); if (scene.endTime < scene.startTime) scene.endTime = scene.startTime; } else if (field === 'transition') { scene.transition = canonicalTransition(value); } else if (field === 'shotSize') { scene.shotSize = canonicalShotSize(value); } else if (field === 'framing') { scene.framing = canonicalFraming(value); } else if (field === 'movement') { scene.movement = canonicalMovement(value); } else if (field === 'lensType') { scene.lensType = canonicalLensType(value); } else if (field === 'angle') { scene.angle = canonicalAngle(value); } else if (field === 'dof') { scene.dof = canonicalDOF(value); } else if (field === 'lightingType') { scene.lightingType = canonicalLightingType(value); } else if (field === 'lightingCondition') { scene.lightingCondition = canonicalLightingCondition(value); } else if (field === 'composition') { scene.composition = canonicalComposition(value); } else if (field === 'notes') { scene.notes = String(value ?? ''); } benchmarkData.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString(); if (scenes.length) compareCurrentToBenchmark(false); else renderBenchmarkSection(); } function compareCurrentToBenchmark(showNotification = true) { if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { if (showNotification) showToast('Create or import a benchmark first.'); return; } if (!scenes.length) { if (showNotification) showToast('No detected storyboard scenes to compare.'); return; } const tolerance = getBenchmarkTolerance(); const usedIndices = new Set(); const metrics = { boundary: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, transition: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, shot: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, framing: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, movement: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, lens: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, angle: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, dof: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, lightingType: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, lightingCondition: { hits: 0, total: 0 }, composition: { hits: 0, total: 0 } }; const rows = benchmarkData.scenes.map((benchmarkScene, rowIndex) => { const match = findBestDetectedSceneMatch(benchmarkScene, scenes, usedIndices); const detectedScene = match?.scene || null; if (match?.detectedIndex !== undefined) usedIndices.add(match.detectedIndex); const startError = detectedScene ? Math.abs(detectedScene.startTime - benchmarkScene.startTime) : null; const endError = detectedScene ? Math.abs(detectedScene.endTime - benchmarkScene.endTime) : null; metrics.boundary.total++; const boundaryHit = !!detectedScene && startError <= tolerance && endError <= tolerance; if (boundaryHit) metrics.boundary.hits++; const transitionHit = compareLabeledField('transition', benchmarkScene.transition, detectedScene?.transition, canonicalTransition, metrics); const shotHit = compareLabeledField('shot', benchmarkScene.shotSize, detectedScene?.camera?.shotSize, canonicalShotSize, metrics); const framingHit = compareLabeledField('framing', benchmarkScene.framing, detectedScene?.camera?.framing, canonicalFraming, metrics); const movementHit = compareLabeledField('movement', benchmarkScene.movement, detectedScene?.camera?.movement, canonicalMovement, metrics); const lensHit = compareLabeledField('lens', benchmarkScene.lensType, detectedScene?.camera?.lensType, canonicalLensType, metrics); const angleHit = compareLabeledField('angle', benchmarkScene.angle, detectedScene?.camera?.angle, canonicalAngle, metrics); const dofHit = compareLabeledField('dof', benchmarkScene.dof, detectedScene?.camera?.dof, canonicalDOF, metrics); const lightingTypeHit = compareLabeledField('lightingType', benchmarkScene.lightingType, detectedScene?.camera?.lightingType, canonicalLightingType, metrics); const lightingConditionHit = compareLabeledField('lightingCondition', benchmarkScene.lightingCondition, detectedScene?.camera?.lightingCondition, canonicalLightingCondition, metrics); const compositionHit = compareLabeledField('composition', benchmarkScene.composition, detectedScene?.camera?.composition, canonicalComposition, metrics); const checks = [ boundaryHit, transitionHit, shotHit, framingHit, movementHit, lensHit, angleHit, dofHit, lightingTypeHit, lightingConditionHit, compositionHit ].filter(value => value !== null); const hits = checks.filter(Boolean).length; const misses = checks.length - hits; const warnThreshold = Math.max(2, Math.floor(checks.length / 3)); const status = !detectedScene ? 'bad' : misses === 0 ? 'ok' : misses <= warnThreshold ? 'warn' : 'bad'; return { benchmarkScene, detectedScene, rowIndex, overlapRatio: match?.overlapRatio ?? 0, startError, endError, boundaryHit, transitionHit, shotHit, framingHit, movementHit, lensHit, angleHit, dofHit, lightingTypeHit, lightingConditionHit, compositionHit, status }; }); const availableMetrics = Object.values(metrics).filter(metric => metric.total > 0); const overall = availableMetrics.length ? availableMetrics.reduce((sum, metric) => sum + metric.hits / metric.total, 0) / availableMetrics.length : 0; benchmarkComparison = { generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(), tolerance, rows, metrics, overall, sceneCountDiff: scenes.length - benchmarkData.scenes.length, unmatchedDetected: scenes.filter((_, index) => !usedIndices.has(index)) }; renderBenchmarkSection(); renderLearningStats(); if (showNotification) { showToast(`비교 완료. 정확도 ${Math.round(overall * 100)}% (정답 JSON 저장하면 학습됩니다)`); } } function renderBenchmarkFieldLine(label, expected, actual, canonicalize) { const normalizedExpected = canonicalize(expected); if (!normalizedExpected) return ''; const normalizedActual = canonicalize(actual) || '-'; return `<div><strong>${escapeHtml(label)}</strong> ${escapeHtml(normalizedExpected)} -> ${escapeHtml(normalizedActual)}</div>`; } function renderBenchmarkCompareCell(row) { if (!row?.detectedScene) { return `<div class="benchmark-compare"> <div class="benchmark-status bad">Mismatch</div> <div>No detected scene matched this benchmark row.</div> </div>`; } const lines = [ `<div class="benchmark-status ${row.status}">${row.status === 'ok' ? 'Match' : row.status === 'warn' ? 'Partial' : 'Mismatch'}</div>`, `<div><strong>Detected</strong> SCENE ${row.detectedScene.index}</div>`, `<div><strong>Boundary</strong> ${row.startError.toFixed(2)}s / ${row.endError.toFixed(2)}s</div>`, renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Transition', row.benchmarkScene.transition, row.detectedScene.transition, canonicalTransition), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Shot', row.benchmarkScene.shotSize, row.detectedScene.camera?.shotSize, canonicalShotSize), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Framing', row.benchmarkScene.framing, row.detectedScene.camera?.framing, canonicalFraming), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Move', row.benchmarkScene.movement, row.detectedScene.camera?.movement, canonicalMovement), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Lens', row.benchmarkScene.lensType, row.detectedScene.camera?.lensType, canonicalLensType), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Angle', row.benchmarkScene.angle, row.detectedScene.camera?.angle, canonicalAngle), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('DOF', row.benchmarkScene.dof, row.detectedScene.camera?.dof, canonicalDOF), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Light Type', row.benchmarkScene.lightingType, row.detectedScene.camera?.lightingType, canonicalLightingType), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Light Cond', row.benchmarkScene.lightingCondition, row.detectedScene.camera?.lightingCondition, canonicalLightingCondition), renderBenchmarkFieldLine('Composition', row.benchmarkScene.composition, row.detectedScene.camera?.composition, canonicalComposition) ].filter(Boolean); return `<div class="benchmark-compare">${lines.join('')}</div>`; } function renderBenchmarkSummary() { const summaryEl = document.getElementById('benchmarkSummary'); const tolerance = benchmarkData ? getBenchmarkTolerance() : 0.35; if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { summaryEl.innerHTML = ` <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Detected Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${scenes.length}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Current storyboard output</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Benchmark Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">0</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">No ground truth yet</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Tolerance</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${tolerance.toFixed(2)}s</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Boundary tolerance</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Video</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${formatTime(videoDuration)}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${escapeHtml(videoFile?.name || '')}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Status</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">Draft</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Create a draft and adjust the rows</div> </div>`; return; } const metrics = benchmarkComparison?.metrics; summaryEl.innerHTML = ` <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Benchmark Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${benchmarkData.scenes.length}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${escapeHtml(benchmarkData.video?.name || videoFile?.name || '')}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Detected Scenes</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${scenes.length}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">Diff ${benchmarkComparison ? benchmarkComparison.sceneCountDiff : scenes.length - benchmarkData.scenes.length}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Boundary</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? metricPercent(metrics.boundary) : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? metricNote(metrics.boundary) : 'Before compare'} / tol ${tolerance.toFixed(2)}s</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Shot / Lens</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? `${metricPercent(metrics.shot)} / ${metricPercent(metrics.lens)}` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? `${metricNote(metrics.shot)} / ${metricNote(metrics.lens)}` : 'Before compare'}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Move / Angle</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? `${metricPercent(metrics.movement)} / ${metricPercent(metrics.angle)}` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? `${metricNote(metrics.movement)} / ${metricNote(metrics.angle)}` : 'Before compare'}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">DOF / Light</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${metrics ? `${metricPercent(metrics.dof)} / ${metricPercent(metrics.lightingCondition)}` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${metrics ? `type ${metricPercent(metrics.lightingType)} / comp ${metricPercent(metrics.composition)}` : 'Before compare'}</div> </div> <div class="benchmark-card"> <div class="benchmark-card-label">Overall</div> <div class="benchmark-card-value">${benchmarkComparison ? `${Math.round(benchmarkComparison.overall * 100)}%` : '-'}</div> <div class="benchmark-card-note">${benchmarkComparison ? `framing ${metricPercent(metrics.framing)} / transition ${metricPercent(metrics.transition)}` : 'Not compared yet'}</div> </div>`; } function renderBenchmarkTableHead() { const headRow = document.querySelector('#benchmarkTableWrap thead tr'); if (!headRow) return; headRow.innerHTML = ` <th>#</th> <th>Start</th> <th>End</th> <th>Transition</th> <th>Shot</th> <th>Framing</th> <th>Movement</th> <th>Lens</th> <th>Angle</th> <th>DOF</th> <th>Light Type</th> <th>Light Cond</th> <th>Composition</th> <th>Compare</th> <th>Notes</th>`; } function renderBenchmarkTable() { const body = document.getElementById('benchmarkTableBody'); if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { body.innerHTML = ''; return; } body.innerHTML = benchmarkData.scenes.map((scene, index) => { const comparisonRow = benchmarkComparison?.rows?.[index]; const thumb = comparisonRow?.detectedScene?.image || scenes.find(s => Math.abs(s.startTime - scene.startTime) < 1.5)?.image || null; return ` <tr class="benchmark-row" data-status="${comparisonRow?.status || 'neutral'}"> <td> ${thumb ? `<img src="${thumb}" style="width:90px;height:52px;object-fit:cover;border-radius:6px;display:block;margin-bottom:6px;border:1px solid var(--border);">` : ''} <div style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:6px;">S${index + 1}</div> <button class="btn" style="padding:5px 8px;font-size:11px;" onclick="deleteBenchmarkScene(${index})">Delete</button> </td> <td> <input class="benchmark-input" value="${escapeHtml(formatTimecode(scene.startTime))}" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'startTime', this.value)"> </td> <td> <input class="benchmark-input" value="${escapeHtml(formatTimecode(scene.endTime))}" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'endTime', this.value)"> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'transition', this.value)"> ${BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.transitions.map(t => { const sel = t === scene.transition ? ' selected' : ''; return `<option value="${escapeHtml(t)}"${sel}>${escapeHtml((TRANSITION_KO[t] ?? t) || 'Not specified')}</option>`; }).join('')} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'shotSize', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.shotSizes, scene.shotSize)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'framing', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.framings, scene.framing)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'movement', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.movements, scene.movement)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'lensType', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.lensTypes, scene.lensType)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'angle', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.angles, scene.angle)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'dof', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.dofs, scene.dof)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'lightingType', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.lightingTypes, scene.lightingType)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'lightingCondition', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.lightingConditions, scene.lightingCondition)} </select> </td> <td> <select class="benchmark-select" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'composition', this.value)"> ${renderBenchmarkSelectOptions(BENCHMARK_OPTIONS.compositions, scene.composition)} </select> </td> <td>${renderBenchmarkCompareCell(comparisonRow)}</td> <td> <textarea class="benchmark-textarea" onchange="updateBenchmarkSceneField(${index}, 'notes', this.value)">${escapeHtml(scene.notes)}</textarea> </td> </tr>`; }).join(''); } function renderBenchmarkSection() { const section = document.getElementById('benchmarkSection'); const emptyEl = document.getElementById('benchmarkEmpty'); const toolbar = document.getElementById('benchmarkToolbar'); const tableWrap = document.getElementById('benchmarkTableWrap'); const metaEl = document.getElementById('benchmarkMeta'); const compareBtn = document.getElementById('benchmarkCompareBtn'); const exportBtn = document.getElementById('benchmarkExportBtn'); const learnBtn = document.getElementById('benchmarkLearnBtn'); const headerBtn = document.getElementById('headerBenchmarkBtn'); const visible = scenes.length > 0 || !!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length; section.style.display = visible ? 'block' : 'none'; headerBtn.style.display = visible ? 'inline-flex' : 'none'; compareBtn.disabled = !benchmarkData?.scenes?.length || !scenes.length; exportBtn.disabled = !benchmarkData?.scenes?.length; if (learnBtn) learnBtn.disabled = !benchmarkData?.scenes?.length || !scenes.length; renderBenchmarkTableHead(); renderBenchmarkSummary(); renderLearningStats(); if (!benchmarkData?.scenes?.length) { emptyEl.style.display = 'block'; toolbar.style.display = 'none'; tableWrap.style.display = 'none'; return; } emptyEl.style.display = 'none'; toolbar.style.display = 'flex'; tableWrap.style.display = 'block'; metaEl.innerHTML = ` Benchmark ${benchmarkData.scenes.length} scenes / boundary tolerance <input class="benchmark-input" id="benchmarkToleranceInput" type="number" min="0.05" step="0.05" value="${getBenchmarkTolerance().toFixed(2)}" style="width:84px;display:inline-block;margin:0 6px;" onchange="updateBenchmarkTolerance(this.value)">sec <button class="btn" style="padding:5px 10px;font-size:11px;margin-left:8px;" onclick="addBenchmarkScene()">+ Add row</button> `; renderBenchmarkTable(); } function getFrameSignatureFromPixels(pixels, w, h) { const histBins = 24; const gridCols = 16; const gridRows = 9; const HUE_BINS = 36; // 10째 ?⑥쐞 Hue ?덉뒪?좉렇??(?됱긽 ?뺤껜?? const hist = new Array(histBins).fill(0); const hueHist = new Array(HUE_BINS).fill(0); // ???좉퇋 const grid = new Float32Array(gridCols * gridRows); const gridCounts = new Uint16Array(gridCols * gridRows); let totalLum = 0, totalR = 0, totalG = 0, totalB = 0; let totalSat = 0, edgeSum = 0, edgeCount = 0, sampleCount = 0; let huePixels = 0; // 梨꾨룄 ?덈뒗 ?쎌? ?? for (let y = 0; y < h; y += 2) { for (let x = 0; x < w; x += 2) { const idx = (y * w + x) * 4; const r = pixels[idx]; const g = pixels[idx + 1]; const b = pixels[idx + 2]; const lum = r * 0.299 + g * 0.587 + b * 0.114; const max = Math.max(r, g, b); const min = Math.min(r, g, b); const delta = max - min; const sat = max > 0 ? delta / max : 0; totalR += r; totalG += g; totalB += b; totalLum += lum; totalSat += sat; sampleCount++; const histIdx = Math.min(histBins - 1, Math.floor((lum / 256) * histBins)); hist[histIdx]++; const gx = Math.min(gridCols - 1, Math.floor((x / w) * gridCols)); const gy = Math.min(gridRows - 1, Math.floor((y / h) * gridRows)); grid[gy * gridCols + gx] += lum; gridCounts[gy * gridCols + gx]++; // ?? Hue ?덉뒪?좉렇?????????????????????????????????????????????? // 梨꾨룄媛 ??굅???덈Т ?대몢???쎌?? ?됱“ ?뺣낫媛 遺덉븞?????쒖쇅 if (sat > 0.12 && max > 24) { let hue; if (max === r) hue = ((g - b) / delta) % 6; else if (max === g) hue = (b - r) / delta + 2; else hue = (r - g) / delta + 4; hue = ((hue * 60) + 360) % 360; // 0??60째 hueHist[Math.min(HUE_BINS - 1, Math.floor(hue / 10))]++; huePixels++; } // ?????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? if (x + 2 < w) { const ri = (y * w + (x + 2)) * 4; edgeSum += Math.abs(lum - (pixels[ri] * 0.299 + pixels[ri+1] * 0.587 + pixels[ri+2] * 0.114)); edgeCount++; } if (y + 2 < h) { const bi = ((y + 2) * w + x) * 4; edgeSum += Math.abs(lum - (pixels[bi] * 0.299 + pixels[bi+1] * 0.587 + pixels[bi+2] * 0.114)); edgeCount++; } } } for (let i = 0; i < grid.length; i++) { if (gridCounts[i] > 0) grid[i] /= gridCounts[i]; } // Hue ?덉뒪?좉렇???뺢퇋??(梨꾨룄 ?덈뒗 ?쎌? ??= 1) if (huePixels > 0) { for (let i = 0; i < HUE_BINS; i++) hueHist[i] /= huePixels; } const avgR = totalR / Math.max(sampleCount, 1); const avgG = totalG / Math.max(sampleCount, 1); const avgB = totalB / Math.max(sampleCount, 1); return { hist, hueHist, grid, sampleCount, brightness: totalLum / Math.max(sampleCount, 1) / 255, saturation: totalSat / Math.max(sampleCount, 1), edgeDensity: edgeSum / Math.max(edgeCount, 1), colorDominant: getColorLabel(avgR, avgG, avgB) }; } function compareFrameSignatures(prev, current) { // ?? 怨듦컙 援ъ“ 李⑥씠 (16횞9 洹몃━??luminance) ??????????????????????????? let gridDiff = 0; for (let i = 0; i < current.grid.length; i++) { gridDiff += Math.abs(current.grid[i] - prev.grid[i]); } gridDiff /= current.grid.length * 255; // ?? 諛앷린 遺꾪룷 李⑥씠 (24-bin ?덉뒪?좉렇?? ??????????????????????????????? let histDiff = 0; for (let i = 0; i < current.hist.length; i++) { histDiff += Math.abs(current.hist[i] - prev.hist[i]); } histDiff /= Math.max(current.sampleCount * 2, 1); // ?? Hue ?됱“ 李⑥씠 (36-bin, ?뺢퇋?붾맖) ????????????????????????????????? let hueDiff = 0; if (current.hueHist && prev.hueHist) { for (let i = 0; i < current.hueHist.length; i++) { hueDiff += Math.abs(current.hueHist[i] - prev.hueHist[i]); } hueDiff /= 2; // L1 distance normalized to 0..1. } const brightnessDiff = Math.abs(current.brightness - prev.brightness); const saturationDiff = Math.abs(current.saturation - prev.saturation); const edgeDiff = Math.abs(current.edgeDensity - prev.edgeDensity) / Math.max(current.edgeDensity, prev.edgeDensity, 1); // ?? 媛以묒튂 ?ъ“??(?⑷퀎 = 1.00) ?????????????????????????????????????? // 湲곗〈: grid(0.42) hist(0.24) brightness(0.16) sat(0.08) edge(0.10) // 蹂寃? hue(0.22) 異붽? ???됱긽 蹂?붽? 媛??媛뺥븳 而??좏샇?꾩쓣 諛섏쁺 // grid 鍮꾩쨷 ?뚰룺 媛먯냼, edge???몄씠利?留롮븘 異뺤냼 const score = gridDiff * 0.32 // 怨듦컙 援ъ“ + hueDiff * 0.22 // ?됱“ ?뺤껜?????좉퇋 + histDiff * 0.18 // 諛앷린 遺꾪룷 + brightnessDiff * 0.12 // ?됯퇏 諛앷린 + saturationDiff * 0.10 // 梨꾨룄 + edgeDiff * 0.06; // ?ｌ? (?몄씠利?誘쇨컧, 鍮꾩쨷 異뺤냼) return { gridDiff, hueDiff, histDiff, brightnessDiff, saturationDiff, edgeDiff, score }; } // ?? ?λ㈃ ?대?吏 ?곗씠?캵RL ??160px ?꾨젅???쒓렇?덉쿂 異붿텧 ?????????????????????? async function _getSignatureFromDataUrl(dataUrl, targetW = 160) { if (!dataUrl) return null; try { const img = new Image(); img.src = dataUrl; await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { img.onload = resolve; img.onerror = reject; }); if (!img.width) return null; const h = Math.max(1, Math.round(targetW * img.height / img.width)); const tc = document.createElement('canvas'); tc.width = targetW; tc.height = h; tc.getContext('2d').drawImage(img, 0, 0, targetW, h); const px = tc.getContext('2d').getImageData(0, 0, targetW, h).data; return getFrameSignatureFromPixels(px, targetW, h); } catch (_) { return null; } } // ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // 媛쒖꽑???몃옖吏??遺꾨쪟湲????щ씪?대뵫 ?덈룄???쒓퀎??遺꾩꽍 // // ??FLASH : 1~3?꾨젅??諛앷린 ?ㅽ뙆?댄겕 (brightness > 0.83) // ??FADE-WHITE : 諛앷린 ?⑥“利앷? ??4?꾨젅???????붾㈃ // ??FADE : 諛앷린 ?⑥“媛먯냼 ??4?꾨젅????寃? ?붾㈃ // ??WHIP-PAN : ?곗냽 5+ ?꾨젅??score ?곸듅 + edgeDiff ?믪쓬 // ??DISSOLVE : bell-curve score ?⑦꽩 + ?ｌ? ?쇱떆 ?섍컯 // ??CUT : 湲곕낯媛?(?⑥씪 ?꾨젅??湲됱긽?? // ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? function classifySceneTransition(samples, index) { const cur = samples[index]; const prev = samples[index - 1]; const next = samples[index + 1]; // ?? ??FLASH ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // ?꾩옱 ?꾨젅?꾩씠 留ㅼ슦 諛앷퀬 ?꾪썑 ?꾨젅?꾨낫???꾩???諛앹쓬 { const bAfter = samples[Math.min(index + 2, samples.length - 1)]?.brightness ?? cur.brightness; const bBefore = samples[Math.max(index - 2, 0)]?.brightness ?? cur.brightness; const avgNeighbor = (bBefore + bAfter) / 2; if (cur.brightness > 0.83 && cur.brightnessDiff > 0.18 && cur.brightness > avgNeighbor + 0.18) { return 'flash'; } } // ?? ??FADE-WHITE ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // 理쒓렐 4~6?꾨젅?꾩뿉??諛앷린媛 ?⑥“利앷??섎ŉ 諛앹? ?붾㈃?쇰줈 ?섎졃 { const LB = Math.min(6, index); if (LB >= 3) { let allRising = true; for (let j = index - LB + 1; j <= index; j++) { if (!samples[j] || !samples[j - 1]) { allRising = false; break; } if (samples[j].brightness < samples[j - 1].brightness - 0.015) { allRising = false; break; } } const bStart = samples[index - LB]?.brightness ?? cur.brightness; if (allRising && cur.brightness > 0.76 && cur.brightness - bStart > 0.18 && cur.gridDiff < 0.22) { return 'fade-white'; } } } // ?? ??FADE (to black) ???????????????????????????????????????????????????? // 理쒓렐 4~6?꾨젅?꾩뿉??諛앷린媛 ?⑥“媛먯냼?섎ŉ ?대몢???붾㈃?쇰줈 ?섎졃 { const LB = Math.min(6, index); if (LB >= 3) { let allFalling = true; for (let j = index - LB + 1; j <= index; j++) { if (!samples[j] || !samples[j - 1]) { allFalling = false; break; } if (samples[j].brightness > samples[j - 1].brightness + 0.015) { allFalling = false; break; } } const bStart = samples[index - LB]?.brightness ?? cur.brightness; if (allFalling && cur.brightness < 0.24 && bStart - cur.brightness > 0.18 && cur.gridDiff < 0.22) { return 'fade'; } } // ?⑥씪 ?꾨젅??諛앷린 湲됰? (?먮옒 濡쒖쭅 ?좎?) const monotonicBrightness = prev && next && ((prev.brightness < cur.brightness && cur.brightness < next.brightness) || (prev.brightness > cur.brightness && cur.brightness > next.brightness)); if ((cur.brightnessDiff > 0.14 && cur.gridDiff < 0.18) || (monotonicBrightness && cur.brightnessDiff > 0.08)) { return cur.brightness > 0.65 ? 'fade-white' : 'fade'; } } // ?? ??WHIP-PAN ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // ?몄젒 짹7?꾨젅?꾩뿉??score媛 ?곗냽?곸쑝濡??믪쓬 + ?됯퇏 edgeDiff ?믪쓬 + 諛앷린 ?덉젙 { let consecutiveElevated = 0; const halfScore = cur.score * 0.40; for (let j = Math.max(0, index - 7); j <= Math.min(samples.length - 1, index + 7); j++) { if (j !== index && samples[j] && samples[j].score > halfScore) consecutiveElevated++; } const nearFrames = []; for (let j = Math.max(0, index - 4); j <= Math.min(samples.length - 1, index + 4); j++) { if (samples[j]) nearFrames.push(samples[j]); } const avgEdgeDiff = nearFrames.reduce((s, f) => s + f.edgeDiff, 0) / Math.max(nearFrames.length, 1); const avgBrightDiff = nearFrames.reduce((s, f) => s + f.brightnessDiff, 0) / Math.max(nearFrames.length, 1); if (consecutiveElevated >= 5 && avgEdgeDiff > 0.32 && avgBrightDiff < 0.14) { return 'whip-pan'; } } // ?? ??DISSOLVE ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Bell-curve: ?쇳겕 ?꾪썑 ?꾨젅?꾨룄 ?곷떦??score ?좎? (?댁쨷?몄텧 ?⑦꽩) // + ?ｌ? 諛???쇱떆 ?섍컯 (???대?吏???먯?媛 遺遺??곸뇙) { const sustainedChange = (prev && prev.score > cur.score * 0.52) || (next && next.score > cur.score * 0.52); let sustainedCount = 0; for (let j = Math.max(0, index - 5); j <= Math.min(samples.length - 1, index + 5); j++) { if (j !== index && samples[j] && samples[j].score > cur.score * 0.42) sustainedCount++; } const edgeBefore = samples[Math.max(0, index - 3)]?.edgeDiff ?? cur.edgeDiff; const edgeAfter = samples[Math.min(samples.length - 1, index + 3)]?.edgeDiff ?? cur.edgeDiff; const avgSurroundEdge = (edgeBefore + edgeAfter) / 2; const edgeDrop = avgSurroundEdge > 0.01 && cur.edgeDiff < avgSurroundEdge * 0.82; if ((sustainedChange && sustainedCount >= 2) || sustainedCount >= 4 || (edgeDrop && sustainedChange)) { return 'dissolve'; } if (cur.histDiff > 0.14 && cur.gridDiff < 0.24) { return 'dissolve'; } } // ?? ??CUT (湲곕낯媛? ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????? return 'cut'; } // ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // ?λ㈃ 而⑦뀓?ㅽ듃 遺꾩꽍 ??match-cut / jump-cut / graphic-cut ?ы썑 蹂댁젙 // // detectScenes ???λ㈃ ?대?吏?쇰━ 鍮꾧탳??'cut'?쇰줈 遺꾨쪟??寃껊쭔 ?щ텇瑜? // 媛??ъ쓽 160px ?쒓렇?덉쿂瑜?異붿텧??cosineSimilarity濡?鍮꾧탳: // // Match Cut : 怨듦컙 援ъ“ ?좎궗 (gridSim > 0.86) + ?됱긽 ?붾젅???ㅻ쫫 (hueSim < 0.68) // Graphic Cut: 援щ룄 ?좎궗 (gridSim > 0.78) + ?됱긽쨌諛앷린 紐⑤몢 ?ㅻ쫫 // Jump Cut : ?됱긽쨌諛앷린 嫄곗쓽 ?숈씪 (媛숈? ?μ냼) but 誘몄꽭??怨듦컙 李⑥씠 // ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? async function applySceneContextTransitions(scenes) { for (let i = 1; i < scenes.length; i++) { // ?대? dissolve / fade / whip-pan ?깆쑝濡?遺꾨쪟??嫄?嫄대뱶由ъ? ?딆쓬 if (scenes[i].transition !== 'cut') continue; const sigPrev = await _getSignatureFromDataUrl(scenes[i - 1].image); const sigCurr = await _getSignatureFromDataUrl(scenes[i].image); if (!sigPrev || !sigCurr) continue; // Hue 肄붿궗???좎궗??(?됱긽 ?붾젅?? const hueSim = cosineSimilarity(sigPrev.hueHist, sigCurr.hueHist); // Grid L1 ?좎궗??(怨듦컙 諛앷린 援ъ“) let gridL1 = 0; for (let k = 0; k < sigPrev.grid.length; k++) { gridL1 += Math.abs(sigPrev.grid[k] - sigCurr.grid[k]); } const gridSim = 1 - gridL1 / (sigPrev.grid.length * 255); // ?덉뒪?좉렇??肄붿궗???좎궗??(諛앷린 遺꾪룷) const histSim = cosineSimilarity(sigPrev.hist, sigCurr.hist); const brightDiff = Math.abs(sigPrev.brightness - sigCurr.brightness); // ?? Match Cut ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // 怨듦컙 援ъ“ 留ㅼ슦 ?좎궗 + ?됱긽 ?붾젅?몃뒗 ?꾪? ?ㅻ쫫 (?λ㈃? 諛붾? if (gridSim > 0.86 && hueSim < 0.68 && brightDiff < 0.30) { scenes[i].transition = 'match-cut'; continue; } // ?? Graphic Cut ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // 援щ룄쨌?뺥깭 ?좎궗 + ?댁슜쨌?됱긽? ?ㅻ쫫 (?뺥깭???쒓컖???댁쑉) if (gridSim > 0.78 && hueSim < 0.72 && histSim < 0.78) { scenes[i].transition = 'graphic-cut'; continue; } // ?? Jump Cut ?????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? if (hueSim > 0.84 && histSim > 0.80 && gridSim > 0.70 && brightDiff < 0.12) { scenes[i].transition = 'jump-cut'; continue; } } } function mergeNearbySceneChanges(candidates, minScene) { const merged = []; for (const candidate of candidates.sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time)) { const last = merged[merged.length - 1]; if (!last || candidate.time - last.time >= minScene) { merged.push(candidate); continue; } if (candidate.score > last.score) { merged[merged.length - 1] = candidate; } } return merged; } async function createSamplingVideo() { const video = document.createElement('video'); video.muted = true; video.preload = 'auto'; video.src = videoUrl; await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { video.onloadeddata = resolve; video.onerror = reject; }); return video; } async function seekVideo(video, time) { const safeTime = clamp(time, 0, Math.max(video.duration - 0.02, 0)); if (Math.abs(video.currentTime - safeTime) < 0.01) return; await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const onSeeked = () => { video.removeEventListener('error', onError); resolve(); }; const onError = () => { video.removeEventListener('seeked', onSeeked); reject(video.error || new Error('seek failed')); }; video.addEventListener('seeked', onSeeked, { once: true }); video.addEventListener('error', onError, { once: true }); video.currentTime = safeTime; }); } function cleanupSamplingVideo(video) { video.pause(); video.removeAttribute('src'); video.load(); video.remove(); } function captureVideoFrameData(video, targetWidth) { const width = Math.min(video.videoWidth || targetWidth, targetWidth); const height = Math.max(1, Math.round(width * (video.videoHeight / Math.max(video.videoWidth, 1)))); frameCanvas.width = width; frameCanvas.height = height; ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, width, height); return ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height); } function captureVideoFrameImage(video, targetWidth = 960, quality = 0.85) { const width = Math.min(video.videoWidth || targetWidth, targetWidth); const height = Math.max(1, Math.round(width * (video.videoHeight / Math.max(video.videoWidth, 1)))); frameCanvas.width = width; frameCanvas.height = height; ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, width, height); return frameCanvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', quality); } function estimateHistogramContrast(histogram, sampleCount) { if (!sampleCount) return 0; let mean = 0; histogram.forEach((count, idx) => { mean += idx * count; }); mean /= sampleCount; let variance = 0; histogram.forEach((count, idx) => { variance += Math.pow(idx - mean, 2) * count; }); variance /= sampleCount; return Math.sqrt(variance) / histogram.length; } function evaluateFrameCandidate(pixels, w, h, relativeTime) { const signature = getFrameSignatureFromPixels(pixels, w, h); const edgeMap = computeEdgeMap(pixels, w, h);
