const contrast = estimateHistogramContrast(signature.hist, signature.sampleCount); const sharpness = clamp(edgeMap.avgEdge / 28, 0, 1.2); const midBias = 1 - Math.abs(relativeTime - 0.5) * 1.4; const exposurePenalty = signature.brightness < 0.1 || signature.brightness > 0.92 ? 0.18 : 0; const flatPenalty = contrast < 0.08 ? 0.12 : 0; const score = sharpness * 0.5 + contrast * 0.22 + signature.saturation * 0.14 + clamp(midBias, 0, 1) * 0.14 - exposurePenalty - flatPenalty; return { score, brightness: signature.brightness, colorDominant: signature.colorDominant }; } function buildSceneCandidateTimes(startTime, endTime, fractions) { const duration = Math.max(endTime - startTime, 0.01); if (duration < 0.2) return [clamp(startTime + duration * 0.5, startTime, endTime)]; const pad = Math.min(Math.max(duration * 0.08, 0.08), 0.6); const minTime = Math.min(startTime + pad, endTime); const maxTime = Math.max(endTime - pad, minTime); const deduped = new Set(); fractions.forEach(fraction => { const time = clamp(startTime + duration * fraction, minTime, maxTime); deduped.add(time.toFixed(3)); }); return [...deduped].map(value => parseFloat(value)).sort((a, b) => a - b); } async function captureSceneFrameSet(video, startTime, endTime) { const candidateTimes = buildSceneCandidateTimes(startTime, endTime, [0.16, 0.32, 0.5, 0.68, 0.84]); let best = null; for (const time of candidateTimes) { await seekVideo(video, time); const frame = captureVideoFrameData(video, 320); const relativeTime = (time - startTime) / Math.max(endTime - startTime, 0.01); const metrics = evaluateFrameCandidate(frame.data, frame.width, frame.height, relativeTime); if (!best || metrics.score > best.metrics.score) { best = { time, metrics }; } } const keyframeTime = best ? best.time : startTime; await seekVideo(video, keyframeTime); const image = captureVideoFrameImage(video, 960, 0.85); const motionTimes = buildSceneCandidateTimes(startTime, endTime, [0.12, 0.5, 0.88]); const multiFrames = []; for (const time of motionTimes) { await seekVideo(video, time); multiFrames.push(captureVideoFrameImage(video, 720, 0.82)); } return { image, multiFrames, keyframeTime, brightness: best ? best.metrics.brightness : 0.5, colorDominant: best ? best.metrics.colorDominant : '' }; } // Scene detection async function generateStoryboard() { const sensitivity = parseInt(document.getElementById('sensitivity').value); const minScene = parseFloat(document.getElementById('minScene').value); const maxFrames = parseInt(document.getElementById('maxFrames').value); const aiMode = document.getElementById('aiMode').value; showProgress(); scenes = []; try { updateProgress('?꾨젅??異붿텧 諛??λ㈃ 遺꾩꽍 以?..', 5); const sceneChanges = await detectScenes(sensitivity, minScene, maxFrames); updateProgress('?ㅽ봽?덉엫 罹≪쿂 以?..', 50); const samplingVideo = await createSamplingVideo(); try { for (let i = 0; i < sceneChanges.length; i++) { const sc = sceneChanges[i]; const endTime = i < sceneChanges.length - 1 ? sceneChanges[i + 1].time : videoDuration; const duration = endTime - sc.time; const frameSet = await captureSceneFrameSet(samplingVideo, sc.time, endTime); scenes.push({ index: i + 1, startTime: sc.time, endTime: endTime, duration: duration, keyframeTime: frameSet.keyframeTime, image: frameSet.image, multiFrames: frameSet.multiFrames, transition: sc.transition, score: sc.score, description: '', brightness: frameSet.brightness ?? sc.brightness, colorDominant: frameSet.colorDominant || sc.colorDominant }); updateProgress(`?ㅽ봽?덉엫 罹≪쿂 以?.. (${i+1}/${sceneChanges.length})`, 50 + (i / sceneChanges.length) * 30); } } finally { cleanupSamplingVideo(samplingVideo); } // ?? ?λ㈃ 而⑦뀓?ㅽ듃 遺꾩꽍: match-cut / jump-cut / graphic-cut 蹂댁젙 ?????????? updateProgress('?몃옖吏??而⑦뀓?ㅽ듃 遺꾩꽍 以?..', 82); await applySceneContextTransitions(scenes); if (aiMode === 'on') { updateProgress('AI ?λ㈃ ?ㅻ챸 ?앹꽦 以?..', 80); await generateAIDescriptions(); } else { updateProgress('濡쒖뺄 移대찓??遺꾩꽍 以?..', 80); for (let i = 0; i < scenes.length; i++) { const s = scenes[i]; try { s.camera = await analyzeFrameAdvanced(s); } catch(e) { console.warn('Local analysis failed for scene', i, e); s.camera = generateLocalCamera(); } s.description = generateLocalDescription(s); updateProgress(`濡쒖뺄 移대찓??遺꾩꽍 以?.. (${i+1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (i / scenes.length) * 15); } } updateProgress('?ㅽ넗由щ낫???뚮뜑留?以?..', 95); await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300)); renderStoryboard(); hideProgress(); showToast('?ㅽ넗由щ낫?쒓? ?앹꽦?섏뿀?듬땲??'); } catch (err) { console.error(err); hideProgress(); showToast('?ㅻ쪟媛 諛쒖깮?덉뒿?덈떎: ' + err.message); } } // ?? 2?⑥뒪 ?λ㈃ 媛먯? ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // // PASS 1 (coarse): ?꾩껜 ?곸긽??~0.12s 媛꾧꺽?쇰줈 鍮좊Ⅴ寃??묒쓬 // ???먯닔媛 ?믪? "怨좎쐞??援ш컙" ?뚯븙 // // PASS 2 (fine) : 怨좎쐞??援ш컙留?0.05s(=20fps) 媛꾧꺽?쇰줈 ?뺣? ?ъ뒪罹?// ??1?⑥뒪?먯꽌 ?볦튇 ?곗냽 而?蹂듭썝 // // ?쇳겕 ?먯? : 諛곗뿴 ?몃뜳??짹2 ???쒓컙 湲곕컲 짹0.2s ?덈룄??// ?꾧퀎媛? : ?덈?媛??섑븳 0.035 ??0.022 (媛먮룄 ?μ긽) // ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // 二쇱뼱吏??쒓컙 踰붿쐞瑜?scanRate 媛꾧꺽?쇰줈 ?ㅼ틪?섏뿬 frameDiff 諛곗뿴 諛섑솚 // prevSig: 援ш컙 吏곸쟾 ?꾨젅?꾩쓽 ?쒓렇?덉쿂 (?곗냽??蹂댁옣) async function _scanRange(video, start, end, scanRate, prevSig) { const diffs = []; let prev = prevSig; // prevSig ?놁쑝硫?start 吏곸쟾 ?꾨젅?꾩쓣 罹≪쿂???곗냽???뺣낫 if (!prev && start > 0.01) { const priorT = Math.max(0, start - scanRate); await seekVideo(video, priorT); ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, 160, 90); prev = getFrameSignatureFromPixels(ctx.getImageData(0, 0, 160, 90).data, 160, 90); } for (let t = start; t < end - 0.005; t += scanRate) { await seekVideo(video, t); ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, 160, 90); const sig = getFrameSignatureFromPixels(ctx.getImageData(0, 0, 160, 90).data, 160, 90); if (prev) { const comp = compareFrameSignatures(prev, sig); diffs.push({ time: t, brightness: sig.brightness, colorDominant: sig.colorDominant, ...comp }); } prev = sig; } return { diffs, lastSig: prev }; } async function detectScenes(sensitivity, minScene, maxFrames) { const video = await createSamplingVideo(); const duration = video.duration; frameCanvas.width = 160; frameCanvas.height = 90; // ?? PASS 1: ?꾩껜 coarse ?ㅼ틪 ?????????????????????????????????????????? // 理쒖냼 0.10s, 理쒕? 1200?섑뵆 ??1遺??곸긽: ~0.10s, 5遺? ~0.13s const coarseRate = Math.max(0.10, duration / Math.min(1200, Math.max(400, duration * 10))); const coarseDiffs = []; let firstSignature = null; let prevSig = null; for (let t = 0; t < duration; t += coarseRate) { await seekVideo(video, t); ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, 160, 90); const sig = getFrameSignatureFromPixels(ctx.getImageData(0, 0, 160, 90).data, 160, 90); if (!firstSignature) firstSignature = sig; if (prevSig) { const comp = compareFrameSignatures(prevSig, sig); coarseDiffs.push({ time: t, brightness: sig.brightness, colorDominant: sig.colorDominant, ...comp }); } prevSig = sig; updateProgress( `[1/2] ?꾩껜 ?ㅼ틪 以?.. ${Math.round((t / Math.max(duration, 0.01)) * 100)}%`, 5 + (t / Math.max(duration, 0.01)) * 22 ); } // ?? 怨좎쐞??援ш컙 怨꾩궛 ?????????????????????????????????????????????????? // coarse ?ㅼ퐫??遺꾪룷瑜?蹂닿퀬 ?곸쐞 ?ㅼ퐫???꾨젅??二쇰????뺣? ?ㅼ틪 const coarseScores = coarseDiffs.map(f => f.score); const coarseStat = summarizeValues(coarseScores); // 怨좎쐞???몃━嫄? mean + std 횞 0.4 ?댁긽 (?곸쐞 ~35% ?섏?) // ?덈Т ??쑝硫??꾩껜瑜??ㅼ떆 ?ㅼ틪???섎? ?녾퀬, ?덈Т ?믪쑝硫??볦묠 const hotTrigger = Math.max(0.018, coarseStat.mean + coarseStat.std * 0.4); // 怨좎쐞???꾨젅????짹FINE_RADIUS 踰붿쐞???덈룄?곕줈 ?뺤옣 const FINE_RATE = 0.05; // 20fps const FINE_RADIUS = 0.40; // 짹0.4s 踰붿쐞 ?ъ뒪罹? const rawWindows = coarseDiffs .filter(f => f.score >= hotTrigger) .map(f => ({ start: Math.max(0, f.time - FINE_RADIUS), end: Math.min(duration, f.time + FINE_RADIUS) })); // 寃뱀튂???덈룄??蹂묓빀 (?뺣젹 ???쒖감 ?⑸퀝) const mergedWindows = []; for (const w of rawWindows.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start)) { const last = mergedWindows[mergedWindows.length - 1]; if (last && w.start <= last.end + 0.05) { last.end = Math.max(last.end, w.end); // ?몄젒 ?덈룄???≪닔 } else { mergedWindows.push({ ...w }); } } // ?꾩껜 而ㅻ쾭由ъ?媛 ?곸긽??65% 珥덇낵硫??꾩껜瑜?fine-scan?쇰줈 ?泥?(?⑥닚?? const totalCoverage = mergedWindows.reduce((s, w) => s + (w.end - w.start), 0); const useFullFineScan = totalCoverage > duration * 0.65; // ?? PASS 2: ?뺣? ?ъ뒪罹???????????????????????????????????????????????? const fineDiffs = []; if (useFullFineScan) { // 耳?댁뒪 A: 怨좎쐞??援ш컙???덈Т 留롮쓬 ???꾩껜瑜?fine?쇰줈 ?泥? updateProgress('[2/2] ?꾩껜 ?뺣? ?ㅼ틪 以?..', 30); const { diffs } = await _scanRange(video, 0, duration, FINE_RATE, null); fineDiffs.push(...diffs); } else { // 耳?댁뒪 B: ?덈룄?곕퀎 ?뺣? ?ㅼ틪 for (let wi = 0; wi < mergedWindows.length; wi++) { const win = mergedWindows[wi]; updateProgress( `[2/2] ?뺣? ?ㅼ틪 以?.. (${wi + 1}/${mergedWindows.length})`, 30 + (wi / Math.max(mergedWindows.length, 1)) * 17 ); const { diffs } = await _scanRange(video, win.start, win.end, FINE_RATE, null); fineDiffs.push(...diffs); } } cleanupSamplingVideo(video); // ?? ???⑥뒪 寃곌낵 蹂묓빀 ????????????????????????????????????????????????? // fine 援ш컙?먯꽌??coarse diff瑜??쒓굅?섍퀬 fine diff瑜??ъ슜 // (媛숈? ?쒓컙???以묐났 怨꾩궛??diff ?쒓굅) const filteredCoarse = useFullFineScan ? [] : coarseDiffs.filter(cf => !fineDiffs.some(ff => Math.abs(ff.time - cf.time) < coarseRate * 0.55) ); const allDiffs = [...filteredCoarse, ...fineDiffs].sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time); if (!allDiffs.length) { return [{ time: 0, score: 0, transition: 'cut', brightness: firstSignature?.brightness ?? 0.5, colorDominant: firstSignature?.colorDominant ?? '' }]; } // ?? ?꾩뿭 ?듦퀎 ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? const allScores = allDiffs.map(f => f.score); const scoreSummary = summarizeValues(allScores); const sensitivityRatio = sensitivity / 100; const percentileRank = clamp(92 - sensitivity * 0.32, 58, 90); // ?꾩뿭 ?꾧퀎媛?(?대갚?? const globalThreshold = Math.max( 0.022, scoreSummary.mean + scoreSummary.std * (0.45 - sensitivityRatio * 0.1), percentile(allScores, percentileRank) * (0.78 + (1 - sensitivityRatio) * 0.08) ); // ?? 濡쒖뺄 ?щ씪?대뵫 ?꾧퀎媛?怨꾩궛 ????????????????????????????????????????? // 臾몄젣: 鍮좊Ⅸ ?몄쭛 援ш컙?먯꽌 ?꾩뿭 mean/std媛 ?щ씪媛 ?꾧퀎媛믪씠 ?④퍡 ?곸듅 // ???뺤옉 李얠븘????而룸뱾???꾧퀎媛??꾨옒濡?臾삵옒 // ?닿껐: 媛??꾨젅?꾨쭏??짹SLIDE_WIN ?쒓컙 ??濡쒖뺄 遺꾪룷濡?媛쒕퀎 ?꾧퀎媛?怨꾩궛 // ?먮┛ 援ш컙? ??? ?꾧퀎媛? 鍮좊Ⅸ 援ш컙???먭린 濡쒖뺄 湲곗??쇰줈 ?먮떒 const SLIDE_WIN_SEC = 12.0; const localThresholds = allDiffs.map((cur, i) => { const localScores = []; for (let j = i; j >= 0 && (cur.time - allDiffs[j].time) <= SLIDE_WIN_SEC; j--) localScores.push(allDiffs[j].score); for (let j = i + 1; j < allDiffs.length && (allDiffs[j].time - cur.time) <= SLIDE_WIN_SEC; j++) localScores.push(allDiffs[j].score); const { mean, std } = summarizeValues(localScores); // 媛먮룄 ?щ씪?대뜑 諛섏쁺: 媛먮룄 ?믪쓣?섎줉 怨꾩닔 ??떠???꾧퀎媛???땄 return Math.max(0.022, mean + std * (0.48 - sensitivityRatio * 0.14)); }); // ?? ?쇳겕 ?먯?: 濡쒖뺄 ?꾧퀎媛?+ ?숈쟻 ?덈룄?????????????????????????????? // ?숈쟻 ?덈룄?? 二쇰? 1.5s ??怨좎뒪肄붿뼱 ?꾨젅?꾩씠 留롮쓣?섎줉 ?덈룄?곕? 醫곹옒 const hotBase = scoreSummary.mean + scoreSummary.std * 0.5; const peaks = []; for (let i = 0; i < allDiffs.length; i++) { const cur = allDiffs[i]; // 濡쒖뺄 ?꾧퀎媛?誘몃떖?대㈃ ?ㅽ궢 if (cur.score < localThresholds[i]) continue; // ?숈쟻 ?쇳겕 ?듭젣 ?덈룄??怨꾩궛 let hotNeighbors = 0; for (let j = i - 1; j >= 0 && (cur.time - allDiffs[j].time) < 1.5; j--) if (allDiffs[j].score > hotBase) hotNeighbors++; for (let j = i + 1; j < allDiffs.length && (allDiffs[j].time - cur.time) < 1.5; j++) if (allDiffs[j].score > hotBase) hotNeighbors++; // ?댁썐??留롮쓣?섎줉 ?덈룄??醫곹옒 (湲됲렪吏?援ш컙 蹂댄샇) const dynWin = hotNeighbors >= 8 ? 0.08 // 裕ㅼ쭅鍮꾨뵒???≪뀡: 80ms : hotNeighbors >= 4 ? 0.13 // ?쇰컲 ??붿뵮 : 0.20; // ?먮┛ ?몄쭛 let isPeak = true; for (let j = i - 1; j >= 0 && (cur.time - allDiffs[j].time) <= dynWin; j--) { if (allDiffs[j].score > cur.score) { isPeak = false; break; } } if (!isPeak) continue; for (let j = i + 1; j < allDiffs.length && (allDiffs[j].time - cur.time) <= dynWin; j++) { if (allDiffs[j].score > cur.score) { isPeak = false; break; } } if (!isPeak) continue; peaks.push({ ...cur, transition: classifySceneTransition(allDiffs, i) }); } if (!peaks.length) { const relaxed = Math.max(0.015, scoreSummary.mean + scoreSummary.std * 0.15); for (let i = 0; i < allDiffs.length; i++) { const cur = allDiffs[i]; if (cur.score < relaxed) continue; const prevScore = allDiffs[i - 1]?.score ?? -Infinity; const nextScore = allDiffs[i + 1]?.score ?? -Infinity; if (cur.score < prevScore || cur.score < nextScore) continue; peaks.push({ ...cur, transition: classifySceneTransition(allDiffs, i) }); } } // ?? 理쒖쥌 ?꾪꽣留???????????????????????????????????????????????????????? let filtered = mergeNearbySceneChanges(peaks, minScene); if (filtered.length > maxFrames - 1) { filtered = filtered .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score) .slice(0, maxFrames - 1) .sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time); } return [{ time: 0, score: 0, transition: 'cut', brightness: firstSignature?.brightness ?? 0.5, colorDominant: firstSignature?.colorDominant ?? '' }, ...filtered].sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time); } function getColorLabel(r, g, b) { if (r > 180 && g > 180 && b > 180) return 'bright tones'; if (r < 60 && g < 60 && b < 60) return 'dark tones'; if (r > g && r > b) return 'warm tones'; if (b > r && b > g) return 'cool tones'; if (g > r && g > b) return 'green tones'; return 'neutral tones'; } function generateLocalDescription(scene) { const dur = scene.duration.toFixed(1); const bright = scene.brightness > 0.6 ? 'bright' : scene.brightness < 0.3 ? 'dark' : 'mid-brightness'; const _transDesc = { 'cut': 'cut transition', 'match-cut': 'match cut', 'action-cut': 'action cut', 'jump-cut': 'jump cut', 'smash-cut': 'smash cut', 'cross-cut': 'cross cut', 'graphic-cut': 'graphic match cut', 'flash': 'flash cut', 'dissolve': 'dissolve', 'match-dissolve': 'match dissolve', 'fade': 'fade', 'fade-white': 'fade to white', 'defocus': 'defocus transition', 'wipe': 'wipe', 'iris': 'iris transition', 'whip-pan': 'whip pan', 'zoom': 'zoom transition', 'l-cut': 'L-cut', 'j-cut': 'J-cut', }; const transition = _transDesc[scene.transition] || `${scene.transition || 'CUT'} transition`; const cam = scene.camera || {}; const shotLabel = cam.shotSize && cam.shotSize !== 'Unknown' ? ` ${cam.shotSize} framing` : ''; const movement = (cam.movement || '').toLowerCase(); const moveLabel = movement && movement !== 'static' ? ` with ${cam.movement} movement` : ' with a static camera'; return `${bright} ${scene.colorDominant}${shotLabel}${moveLabel}. It lasts ${dur}s and begins with a ${transition}.`; } // ===== LOCAL HEURISTIC CAMERA ANALYSIS ENGINE ===== function getFaceDetector() { if (faceDetectorInstance !== undefined) return faceDetectorInstance; if (!('FaceDetector' in window)) { faceDetectorInstance = null; return faceDetectorInstance; } try { faceDetectorInstance = new window.FaceDetector({ fastMode: true, maxDetectedFaces: 5 }); } catch (err) { faceDetectorInstance = null; } return faceDetectorInstance; } async function analyzeFaces(source, w, h) { const detector = getFaceDetector(); const fallback = { supported: !!detector, count: 0, framing: 'Empty', confidence: 0, largestAreaRatio: 0, maxHeightRatio: 0, subjectCenterX: 0.5, subjectCenterY: 0.5, boxes: [] }; if (!detector) return fallback; try { const faces = await detector.detect(source); if (!faces || !faces.length) return fallback; const boxes = faces.map(face => { const box = face.boundingBox || face; const width = box.width / w; const height = box.height / h; return { x: box.x / w, y: box.y / h, width, height, area: width * height, cx: (box.x + box.width / 2) / w, cy: (box.y + box.height / 2) / h }; }).sort((a, b) => b.area - a.area); let framing = 'Single'; if (boxes.length === 2) framing = 'Two-shot'; else if (boxes.length === 3) framing = 'Three-shot'; else if (boxes.length > 3) framing = 'Crowd'; const edgeFace = boxes.find(box => box.area > 0.035 && (box.x < 0.08 || (box.x + box.width) > 0.92)); const centerFace = boxes.find(box => box.cx > 0.28 && box.cx < 0.72); if (edgeFace && centerFace && boxes.length >= 2) framing = 'OTS'; const largest = boxes[0]; return { supported: true, count: boxes.length, framing, confidence: clamp(0.58 + Math.min(largest.area * 1.6, 0.24) + Math.min(boxes.length, 3) * 0.04, 0.58, 0.92), largestAreaRatio: largest.area, maxHeightRatio: largest.height, subjectCenterX: largest.cx, subjectCenterY: largest.cy, boxes }; } catch (err) { return fallback; } } async function getPoseLandmarker() { if (poseLandmarkerUnavailable) return null; if (poseLandmarkerInstance) return poseLandmarkerInstance; if (poseLandmarkerPromise) return poseLandmarkerPromise; poseLandmarkerPromise = (async () => { try { const vision = await import(`https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@mediapipe/tasks-vision@${POSE_TASKS_VERSION}/vision_bundle.mjs`); const { FilesetResolver, PoseLandmarker } = vision; const resolver = await FilesetResolver.forVisionTasks(POSE_WASM_ROOT); let lastError = null; for (const modelAssetPath of POSE_MODEL_CANDIDATES) { try { poseLandmarkerInstance = await PoseLandmarker.createFromOptions(resolver, { baseOptions: { modelAssetPath }, runningMode: 'IMAGE', numPoses: 4, minPoseDetectionConfidence: 0.45, minPosePresenceConfidence: 0.45, minTrackingConfidence: 0.45, outputSegmentationMasks: true }); break; } catch (err) { lastError = err; } } if (!poseLandmarkerInstance) throw lastError || new Error('PoseLandmarker init failed'); return poseLandmarkerInstance; } catch (err) { console.warn('Pose landmarker unavailable, falling back to heuristics.', err); poseLandmarkerUnavailable = true; poseLandmarkerInstance = null; return null; } })(); return poseLandmarkerPromise; } function getLandmarkConfidence(point) { if (!point) return 0; const visibility = Number.isFinite(point.visibility) ? point.visibility : 1; const presence = Number.isFinite(point.presence) ? point.presence : 1; return Math.min(visibility, presence); } function isUsableLandmark(point) { return !!point && Number.isFinite(point.x) && Number.isFinite(point.y) && point.x >= -0.25 && point.x <= 1.25 && point.y >= -0.25 && point.y <= 1.25; } function getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, indices, threshold = 0.4) { const points = indices .map(index => landmarks[index]) .filter(point => isUsableLandmark(point) && getLandmarkConfidence(point) >= threshold); if (!points.length) return null; let totalWeight = 0; let sumX = 0; let sumY = 0; let maxScore = 0; points.forEach(point => { const weight = Math.max(0.001, getLandmarkConfidence(point)); totalWeight += weight; sumX += point.x * weight; sumY += point.y * weight; maxScore = Math.max(maxScore, weight); }); return { x: sumX / totalWeight, y: sumY / totalWeight, score: maxScore, count: points.length }; } function getMaskBounds(mask, threshold = 0.25, step = 2) { if (!mask || typeof mask.getAsFloat32Array !== 'function') return null; try { const width = mask.width || 0; const height = mask.height || 0; const data = mask.getAsFloat32Array(); if (!width || !height || !data?.length) return null; let minX = width; let minY = height; let maxX = -1; let maxY = -1; let count = 0; let total = 0; for (let y = 0; y < height; y += step) { for (let x = 0; x < width; x += step) { const value = data[y * width + x]; if (value < threshold) continue; count++; total += value; if (x < minX) minX = x; if (x > maxX) maxX = x; if (y < minY) minY = y; if (y > maxY) maxY = y; } } if (!count || maxX < minX || maxY < minY) return null; return { left: minX / width, right: (maxX + 1) / width, top: minY / height, bottom: (maxY + 1) / height, widthRatio: (maxX - minX + 1) / width, heightRatio: (maxY - minY + 1) / height, areaRatio: Math.min(1, (count * step * step) / (width * height)), confidence: clamp(total / count, 0, 1) }; } catch (err) { return null; } } function summarizePoseLandmarks(landmarks, maskBounds = null) { const reliable = landmarks .map((point, index) => ({ point, index, score: getLandmarkConfidence(point) })) .filter(item => isUsableLandmark(item.point) && item.score >= 0.35); if (reliable.length < 6) return null; const xs = reliable.map(item => item.point.x); const ys = reliable.map(item => item.point.y); const rawBounds = { left: clamp(Math.min(...xs), 0, 1), right: clamp(Math.max(...xs), 0, 1), top: clamp(Math.min(...ys), 0, 1), bottom: clamp(Math.max(...ys), 0, 1) }; const shoulders = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [11, 12], 0.42); const hips = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [23, 24], 0.42); const knees = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [25, 26], 0.38); const ankles = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [27, 28], 0.35); const wrists = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [15, 16], 0.35); const eyes = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [2, 5], 0.35) || getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [1, 4], 0.35); const ears = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [7, 8], 0.35); const nose = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [0], 0.35); const mouth = getReliablePosePoint(landmarks, [9, 10], 0.35); const mergedBounds = maskBounds ? { left: clamp(Math.min(rawBounds.left, maskBounds.left), 0, 1), right: clamp(Math.max(rawBounds.right, maskBounds.right), 0, 1), top: clamp(Math.min(rawBounds.top, maskBounds.top), 0, 1), bottom: clamp(Math.max(rawBounds.bottom, maskBounds.bottom), 0, 1) } : rawBounds; const topCandidates = [eyes?.y, ears?.y, nose?.y].filter(Number.isFinite); const headTopY = topCandidates.length ? clamp(Math.min(...topCandidates) - 0.04, 0, 1) : mergedBounds.top; const shoulderY = shoulders?.y ?? null; const hipY = hips?.y ?? null; const kneeY = knees?.y ?? (shoulders && hips ? clamp(hipY + (hipY - shoulderY) * 0.95, 0, 1.3) : null); const ankleY = ankles?.y ?? (shoulders && hips ? clamp(hipY + (hipY - shoulderY) * 1.9, 0, 1.4) : null); const torsoSpan = shoulders && hips ? Math.max(hipY - shoulderY, 0.08) : null; let faceBottomY = shoulderY ?? mergedBounds.bottom; if (hipY !== null) faceBottomY = Math.min(faceBottomY, hipY); const faceHeightRatio = clamp((faceBottomY - headTopY) * 1.08, 0.04, 0.9); const visibleBelowHip = hipY === null ? 0 : Math.max(0, mergedBounds.bottom - hipY); const lowerBodyRatio = torsoSpan ? visibleBelowHip / torsoSpan : 0; const headRoom = mergedBounds.top; const footRoom = Math.max(0, 1 - mergedBounds.bottom); let cropLevel = 'unknown'; if (ankles) cropLevel = headRoom < 0.08 && footRoom < 0.08 ? 'full-tight' : 'full'; else if (knees) cropLevel = lowerBodyRatio > 1.3 ? 'fullish' : 'knee'; else if (hips) cropLevel = lowerBodyRatio > 0.72 ? 'cowboy' : lowerBodyRatio > 0.3 ? 'waist' : 'chest'; else if (shoulders) { if (mouth && shoulderY !== null) { const faceSpan = Math.max(mouth.y - headTopY, 0.03); const chinY = mouth.y + faceSpan * 0.28; const throatY = mouth.y + faceSpan * 0.65; const fb = mergedBounds.bottom; if (fb < chinY + 0.02) cropLevel = 'face'; else if (fb < throatY + 0.01) cropLevel = 'chin'; else if (fb < shoulderY - 0.03) cropLevel = 'throat'; else cropLevel = faceHeightRatio > 0.6 ? 'head' : 'shoulders'; } else { cropLevel = faceHeightRatio > 0.6 ? 'face' : faceHeightRatio > 0.42 ? 'head' : 'shoulders'; } } else { if (mouth) { const faceSpan = Math.max(mouth.y - headTopY, 0.03); const chinY = mouth.y + faceSpan * 0.28; const throatY = mouth.y + faceSpan * 0.65; const fb = mergedBounds.bottom; if (fb < chinY + 0.02) cropLevel = 'face'; else if (fb < throatY + 0.01) cropLevel = 'chin'; else if (fb < throatY + faceSpan * 0.6) cropLevel = 'throat'; else cropLevel = faceHeightRatio > 0.65 ? 'face' : 'head'; } else { cropLevel = faceHeightRatio > 0.65 ? 'face' : 'head'; } } const widthRatio = mergedBounds.right - mergedBounds.left; const heightRatio = mergedBounds.bottom - mergedBounds.top; const areaRatio = maskBounds?.areaRatio || (widthRatio * heightRatio); return { left: mergedBounds.left, right: mergedBounds.right, top: mergedBounds.top, bottom: mergedBounds.bottom, widthRatio, heightRatio, areaRatio, centerX: (mergedBounds.left + mergedBounds.right) / 2, centerY: (mergedBounds.top + mergedBounds.bottom) / 2, faceHeightRatio, cropLevel, torsoSpan: torsoSpan || 0, lowerBodyRatio, headRoom, footRoom, confidence: clamp(reliable.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.score, 0) / reliable.length, 0.38, 0.92), headTopY, shoulderY, hipY, kneeY, ankleY, wristY: wrists?.y ?? null, mouthY: mouth?.y ?? null, hasShoulders: !!shoulders, hasHips: !!hips, hasKnees: !!knees, hasAnkles: !!ankles, hasMask: !!maskBounds, visibleCount: reliable.length }; } async function analyzePoseFrame(source, w, h, faceAnalysis) { const fallback = { supported: !poseLandmarkerUnavailable, count: 0, framing: 'Empty', confidence: 0, subjectCenterX: faceAnalysis?.subjectCenterX ?? 0.5, subjectCenterY: faceAnalysis?.subjectCenterY ?? 0.5, primary: null }; const landmarker = await getPoseLandmarker(); if (!landmarker) return { ...fallback, supported: false }; let result = null; try { result = landmarker.detect(source); const poses = Array.isArray(result?.landmarks) ? result.landmarks : []; if (!poses.length) return { ...fallback, supported: true }; const preferredX = faceAnalysis?.count ? faceAnalysis.subjectCenterX : 0.5; const preferredY = faceAnalysis?.count ? faceAnalysis.subjectCenterY : 0.52; const summaries = poses .map((landmarks, index) => { const summary = summarizePoseLandmarks(landmarks, getMaskBounds(result?.segmentationMasks?.[index] || null)); if (!summary) return null; const centerDistance = Math.hypot(summary.centerX - preferredX, summary.centerY - preferredY); summary.selectionScore = (summary.areaRatio * 2.2) + (summary.heightRatio * 0.8) + (summary.confidence * 0.7) - (centerDistance * 0.35); return summary; }) .filter(Boolean) .sort((a, b) => b.selectionScore - a.selectionScore); if (!summaries.length) return { ...fallback, supported: true, count: poses.length }; const framing = poses.length > 3 ? 'Crowd' : poses.length === 3 ? 'Three-shot' : poses.length === 2 ? 'Two-shot' : 'Single'; return { supported: true, count: poses.length, framing, confidence: clamp(summaries[0].confidence + Math.min(0.1, (poses.length - 1) * 0.03), 0.45, 0.95), subjectCenterX: summaries[0].centerX, subjectCenterY: summaries[0].centerY, primary: summaries[0], poses: summaries }; } catch (err) { return { ...fallback, supported: true }; } finally { result?.close?.(); } } function getPrimarySubject(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis) { if (poseAnalysis?.primary) { return { count: poseAnalysis.count, centerX: poseAnalysis.primary.centerX, centerY: poseAnalysis.primary.centerY, size: poseAnalysis.primary.heightRatio, faceHeight: poseAnalysis.primary.faceHeightRatio, source: 'pose' }; } if (faceAnalysis?.count > 0) { return { count: faceAnalysis.count, centerX: faceAnalysis.subjectCenterX, centerY: faceAnalysis.subjectCenterY, size: faceAnalysis.maxHeightRatio, faceHeight: faceAnalysis.maxHeightRatio, source: 'face' }; } return null; } function estimateFraming(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis, composition) { const faceCount = faceAnalysis?.count || 0; const poseCount = poseAnalysis?.count || 0; const count = Math.max(faceCount, poseCount); if (!count) return composition.hasFace ? 'Single' : 'Empty'; if (count > 3) return 'Crowd'; if (count === 3) return 'Three-shot'; const faceBoxes = faceAnalysis?.boxes || []; if (count >= 2) { const edgeFace = faceBoxes.find(box => box.area > 0.03 && box.height > 0.2 && (box.cx < 0.2 || box.cx > 0.8) ); const centerFace = faceBoxes.find(box => box.height > 0.12 && box.cx > 0.3 && box.cx < 0.7 ); if (edgeFace && centerFace) return 'OTS'; const poses = poseAnalysis?.poses || []; const edgePose = poses.find(pose => pose.widthRatio > 0.2 && (pose.centerX < 0.2 || pose.centerX > 0.8) ); const centerPose = poses.find(pose => pose.centerX > 0.3 && pose.centerX < 0.7); if (edgePose && centerPose) return 'OTS'; return count === 2 ? 'Two-shot' : 'Three-shot'; } if (faceAnalysis?.framing === 'OTS') return 'OTS'; return 'Single'; } function compositionDistanceScore(x, y, targets, radiusX = 0.16, radiusY = 0.16) { let best = 0; for (const [tx, ty] of targets) { const dx = (x - tx) / radiusX; const dy = (y - ty) / radiusY; best = Math.max(best, clamp(1 - Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy), 0, 1)); } return best; } function buildCompositionDetail(type, metrics) { const pct = v => `${Math.round(clamp(v, 0, 1) * 100)}%`; const aX = `${Math.round(metrics.anchorX * 100)}%`; const aY = `${Math.round(metrics.anchorY * 100)}%`; switch (type) { case 'Symmetrical': return `Strong left-right balance ${pct(metrics.symmetryCore)} with a centered anchor at (${aX}, ${aY}).`; case 'Center-framed': return `The subject mass sits near the center at (${aX}, ${aY}), with center weighting ${pct(metrics.centerMass)}.`; case 'Rule-of-thirds': return `The anchor lands near a thirds hotspot (${pct(metrics.thirdScore)}), keeping the frame off-center.`; case 'Golden-ratio': return `The anchor aligns with a golden-ratio hotspot (${pct(metrics.goldenScore)}) at (${aX}, ${aY}).`; case 'Leading-lines': return `Directional lines flow at ${pct(metrics.diagonalFlow)} and guide attention toward the subject.`; case 'Frame-within-frame': return `Axis-aligned enclosure strength is ${pct(metrics.axisFrame)}, creating a frame-within-frame effect around the subject.`; case 'Negative-space': return `The subject anchor sits at (${aX}, ${aY}) with side openness ${pct(metrics.sideOpen)} and sparse-frame ratio ${pct(metrics.sparseFrame)}.`; case 'Diagonal': return `Diagonal emphasis reaches ${pct(metrics.diagFocused)} with corner-to-corner energy at ${pct(metrics.cornerDiag)}.`; case 'Vanishing-point': return `Line convergence is ${pct(metrics.convergence)}, pulling the eye toward a vanishing point.`; case 'Layered': return `Depth separation is ${pct(metrics.depthSep)} with foreground detail ${pct(metrics.fgDetail)}.`; case 'Environmental': return `The subject occupies ${pct(1 - metrics.subjectTiny)} while environmental richness reaches ${pct(metrics.envRichness)}.`; case 'Dynamic-tension': return `Visual weight dispersion is ${pct(metrics.weightDispersion)}, creating a more tense and unstable frame.`; default: return `Spatial distribution and anchor placement support a ${type} composition.`; } } function estimateCompositionTag(composition, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis, focus, edgeMap) { const subject = getPrimarySubject(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis); // ?? Anchor point ??????????????????????????????????????????????? const thirdPoints = [[1/3,1/3],[2/3,1/3],[1/3,2/3],[2/3,2/3]]; const phi = 0.618; const goldenPoints = [[1-phi,1-phi],[phi,1-phi],[1-phi,phi],[phi,phi]]; const anchorX = subject?.centerX ?? composition.visualCentroidX ?? 0.5; const anchorY = subject?.centerY ?? composition.visualCentroidY ?? 0.5; // ?? Distance/proximity scores ????????????????????????????????? const centerScore = compositionDistanceScore(anchorX, anchorY, [[0.5,0.5]], 0.18, 0.16); const thirdScore = compositionDistanceScore(anchorX, anchorY, thirdPoints, 0.18, 0.18); const goldenScore = compositionDistanceScore(anchorX, anchorY, goldenPoints, 0.16, 0.16); const offCenter = clamp(Math.hypot(anchorX - 0.5, anchorY - 0.5) / 0.35, 0, 1); const offCenterX = clamp(Math.abs(anchorX - 0.5) / 0.32, 0, 1); // ?? Symmetry ?????????????????????????????????????????????????? const symmetryCore = clamp(composition.verticalSymmetry * 0.72 + composition.horizontalSymmetry * 0.28, 0, 1); // ?? Focus/depth signals ??????????????????????????????????????? const focusTunnel = clamp((focus.avgPeriphery / Math.max(focus.centerSharpness, 0.001) - 1.02) / 0.35, 0, 1); const centerSharpBias = clamp((focus.centerSharpness / Math.max(focus.avgPeriphery, 0.001) - 1.02) / 0.45, 0, 1); const zoneVar = focus.zoneVariance ?? 0; const outerEdge = focus.outerRingSharpness ?? 0; const depthSep = clamp((zoneVar - 0.005) / 0.015, 0, 1); const fgDetail = clamp((outerEdge - 0.30) / 0.40, 0, 1); // ?? Edge/line signals ????????????????????????????????????????? const diagonalFlow = clamp((edgeMap.diagonalEnergyRatio - 0.18) / 0.22, 0, 1); const axisFrame = clamp((edgeMap.axisEnergyRatio - 0.58) / 0.26, 0, 1); const edgeRichness = clamp((edgeMap.avgEdge - 10) / 16, 0, 1); // Diagonal orientation cluster from 18-bin histogram // bins 0=vertical ??bins 4-5??5째 ??bins 8-9=horizontal ??bins 13-14??35째 const bins = Array.isArray(edgeMap.orientationBins) ? edgeMap.orientationBins : Array(18).fill(0); const totalBinE = bins.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) + 0.001; const diag45E = (bins[4] || 0) + (bins[5] || 0); const diag135E = (bins[13] || 0) + (bins[14] || 0); const diagCluster = Math.max(diag45E, diag135E) / totalBinE; const diagFocused = clamp((diagCluster - 0.08) / 0.12, 0, 1); // ?? Region weight signals ????????????????????????????????????? const R = composition.regions || []; const rw = i => (R[i]?.weightRatio || 0); const centerMass = clamp((composition.centerWeight - 0.16) / 0.16, 0, 1); const modestCenterMass = 1 - clamp(Math.abs(composition.centerWeight - 0.22) / 0.18, 0, 1); const lowCenterMass = clamp((0.26 - composition.centerWeight) / 0.14, 0, 1); const outerBandWR = composition.outerBandWeightRatio ?? 0; const densePerimeter = clamp((outerBandWR - 0.46) / 0.22, 0, 1); const frameIsolation = clamp((focus.avgPeriphery / Math.max(focus.centerSharpness, 0.001) - 1.08) / 0.32, 0, 1); // Corner-to-corner diagonal weight balance const diagTLBR = rw(0) + rw(8); // top-left ??bottom-right const diagTRBL = rw(2) + rw(6); // top-right ??bottom-left const cornerDiagFocus = clamp((Math.max(diagTLBR, diagTRBL) - 0.12) / 0.18, 0, 1); // Region weight dispersion across all 9 cells ??multi-pole tension const regionWts = [0,1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8].map(i => rw(i)); const rwMean = regionWts.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / 9; const rwVar = regionWts.reduce((s, v) => s + (v - rwMean) ** 2, 0) / 9; const weightDispersion = clamp((rwVar - 0.001) / 0.006, 0, 1); // ?? Subject/space signals ????????????????????????????????????? const sideOpen = anchorX <= 0.5 ? composition.rightOpenness : composition.leftOpenness; const sparseFrame = clamp((composition.emptyRegionRatio - 0.22) / 0.40, 0, 1); const subjectSmall = subject ? clamp((0.30 - Math.min(subject.size, 0.30)) / 0.22, 0, 1) : clamp((0.24 - composition.centerWeight) / 0.14, 0, 1); const subjectTiny = subject ? clamp((0.12 - Math.min(subject.size, 0.12)) / 0.08, 0, 1) : clamp((0.16 - composition.centerWeight) / 0.10, 0, 1); const envRichness = clamp((edgeMap.avgEdge - 8) / 12, 0, 1); // ?? Convergence (vanishing point) ????????????????????????????? const convergence = clamp(axisFrame * 0.50 + composition.centerHotspotWeight * 0.50, 0, 1); // ?? Score all 12 types ???????????????????????????????????????? const scores = {}; scores['Symmetrical'] = clamp( symmetryCore * 0.44 + centerScore * 0.18 + composition.centerHotspotWeight * 0.14 + centerMass * 0.12 + axisFrame * 0.12, 0, 1); scores['Center-framed'] = clamp( centerScore * 0.40 + composition.centerHotspotWeight * 0.22 + centerMass * 0.16 + centerSharpBias * 0.12 + (1 - offCenter) * 0.10, 0, 1); scores['Rule-of-thirds'] = clamp( thirdScore * 0.40 + composition.thirdsHotspotWeight * 0.24 + (1 - centerMass) * 0.10 + (subject ? 0.08 : 0.03) + clamp(1 - Math.abs(anchorY - 0.5) / 0.34, 0, 1) * 0.08 + Math.max(composition.leftOpenness, composition.rightOpenness) * 0.10, 0, 1); scores['Golden-ratio'] = clamp( goldenScore * 0.48 + composition.goldenHotspotWeight * 0.26 + (1 - centerMass) * 0.10 + subjectSmall * 0.08 + offCenter * 0.08, 0, 1); scores['Leading-lines'] = clamp( diagonalFlow * 0.36 + focusTunnel * 0.20 + Math.max(centerScore, thirdScore) * 0.16 + densePerimeter * 0.14 + edgeRichness * 0.14, 0, 1); scores['Frame-within-frame'] = clamp( axisFrame * 0.30 + frameIsolation * 0.26 + centerScore * 0.16 + densePerimeter * 0.16 + modestCenterMass * 0.12, 0, 1); scores['Negative-space'] = clamp( offCenterX * 0.22 + sideOpen * 0.22 + sparseFrame * 0.20 + subjectSmall * 0.18 + lowCenterMass * 0.10 + Math.max(composition.leftOpenness, composition.rightOpenness) * 0.08, 0, 1); // Diagonal ??single bold diagonal element crossing the frame scores['Diagonal'] = clamp( diagFocused * 0.38 + cornerDiagFocus * 0.30 + diagonalFlow * 0.20 + (1 - axisFrame) * 0.12, 0, 1); // Vanishing-point ??perspective lines converging to a single point scores['Vanishing-point'] = clamp( convergence * 0.36 + focusTunnel * 0.28 + axisFrame * 0.20 + edgeRichness * 0.16, 0, 1); // Layered ??distinct foreground / midground / background planes scores['Layered'] = clamp( depthSep * 0.44 + fgDetail * 0.30 + edgeRichness * 0.14 + (1 - centerSharpBias) * 0.12, 0, 1); // Environmental ??tiny subject dominated by rich environment scores['Environmental'] = clamp( subjectTiny * 0.40 + envRichness * 0.28 + sparseFrame * 0.16 + (1 - centerMass) * 0.16, 0, 1); // Dynamic-tension ??competing asymmetric weight poles scores['Dynamic-tension'] = clamp( weightDispersion * 0.38 + (1 - composition.centerWeight) * 0.26 + offCenter * 0.20 + (1 - symmetryCore) * 0.16, 0, 1); // ?? Winner selection ?????????????????????????????????????????? const ordered = Object.entries(scores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]); let [type, topScore] = ordered[0]; const secondScore = ordered[1]?.[1] || 0; // Tie-breaking if (scores['Symmetrical'] > 0.58 && scores['Center-framed'] > 0.54 && Math.abs(scores['Symmetrical'] - scores['Center-framed']) < 0.05) { type = 'Symmetrical'; topScore = scores[type]; } else if (scores['Frame-within-frame'] > 0.54 && scores['Leading-lines'] > 0.50 && axisFrame >= diagonalFlow) { type = 'Frame-within-frame'; topScore = scores[type]; } else if (scores['Diagonal'] > 0.50 && scores['Leading-lines'] > 0.50 && diagFocused > diagonalFlow) { type = 'Diagonal'; topScore = scores[type]; } else if (!subject && topScore < 0.44) { type = composition.centerHotspotWeight >= composition.thirdsHotspotWeight ? 'Center-framed' : 'Rule-of-thirds'; topScore = scores[type]; } // ?? Secondary subtype (if runner-up is ??72% of winner) ??????? const runner = ordered.find(([t]) => t !== type); const compositionSubtype = (runner && runner[1] >= topScore * 0.72) ? runner[0] : null; // ?? Balance classification ????????????????????????????????????? let compositionBalance; if (symmetryCore > 0.72) compositionBalance = 'Symmetric'; else if (weightDispersion > 0.55 || scores['Dynamic-tension'] > 0.45) compositionBalance = 'Dynamic'; else compositionBalance = 'Asymmetric'; // ?? Depth classification ??????????????????????????????????????? let compositionDepth; if (type === 'Layered' || depthSep > 0.55) compositionDepth = 'Layered'; else if (fgDetail > 0.40 || zoneVar > 0.012) compositionDepth = '2-plane'; else compositionDepth = 'Flat'; // ?? Confidence ???????????????????????????????????????????????? const confidence = clamp(0.36 + topScore * 0.42 + (topScore - secondScore) * 0.25, subject ? 0.40 : 0.33, 0.94); const metrics = { anchorX, anchorY, anchorSource: subject?.source || 'saliency', centerScore, thirdScore, goldenScore, symmetryCore, centerMass, diagonalFlow, axisFrame, sideOpen, sparseFrame, diagFocused, cornerDiag: cornerDiagFocus, convergence, depthSep, fgDetail, subjectTiny, envRichness, weightDispersion, topAlternatives: ordered.slice(0, 3).map(([label, score]) => ({ label, score })) }; return { type, confidence, detail: buildCompositionDetail(type, metrics), metrics, scores, compositionSubtype, compositionBalance, compositionDepth }; } function estimateLighting(colorAnalysis, composition, faceAnalysis, edgeMap) { const { avgBrightness, shadowRatio, highlightRatio, warmRatio, coolRatio, contrastRatio, avgR = 128, avgG = 128, avgB = 128 } = colorAnalysis; // ?? Color temperature via R:B ratio ??????????????????????????? const rbRatio = (avgR + 0.001) / (avgB + 0.001); let colorTemp, colorTempK; if (rbRatio > 1.85) { colorTemp = 'Very-warm'; colorTempK = 2700; } else if (rbRatio > 1.40) { colorTemp = 'Warm'; colorTempK = 3800; } else if (rbRatio > 0.90) { colorTemp = 'Neutral'; colorTempK = 5500; } else if (rbRatio > 0.68) { colorTemp = 'Cool'; colorTempK = 7000; } else { colorTemp = 'Very-cool'; colorTempK = 9000; } // ?? 3횞3 region brightness (raw 0-255) ????????????????????????? const R = composition.regions || []; const bri = i => (R[i] ? R[i].brightness : avgBrightness * 255); const topAvg = (bri(0) + bri(1) + bri(2)) / 3; const bottomAvg = (bri(6) + bri(7) + bri(8)) / 3; const leftAvg = (bri(0) + bri(3) + bri(6)) / 3; const rightAvg = (bri(2) + bri(5) + bri(8)) / 3; const centerBri = bri(4); const perimMax = Math.max(topAvg, bottomAvg, leftAvg, rightAvg, 1); // Normalized deltas (0-1 scale) const vertBias = (topAvg - bottomAvg) / 255; // >0 = top-lit const horizBias = (rightAvg - leftAvg) / 255; // >0 = right-lit const sideAsym = Math.abs(horizBias); // ?? Backlit detection ????????????????????????????????????????? const isBacklit = (centerBri / (perimMax + 1)) < 0.70 && highlightRatio > 0.10; // ?? Light direction ??????????????????????????????????????????? let lightingDirection; if (isBacklit) { lightingDirection = 'Back'; } else if (vertBias > 0.20 && horizBias > 0.12) { lightingDirection = 'Top-right'; } else if (vertBias > 0.20 && horizBias < -0.12) { lightingDirection = 'Top-left'; } else if (vertBias > 0.18) { lightingDirection = 'Top'; } else if (vertBias < -0.18) { lightingDirection = 'Bottom'; } else if (horizBias > 0.16) { lightingDirection = 'Right'; } else if (horizBias < -0.16) { lightingDirection = 'Left'; } else { lightingDirection = 'Front'; } // ?? Hardness (histogram bimodality) ?????????????????????????? const midRatio = Math.max(0, 1 - shadowRatio - highlightRatio); const bimodalScore = shadowRatio + highlightRatio - midRatio * 0.7; let lightingHardness; if (bimodalScore > 0.45 && contrastRatio > 0.40) lightingHardness = 'Hard'; else if (bimodalScore < 0.12 && contrastRatio < 0.28) lightingHardness = 'Soft'; else lightingHardness = 'Mixed'; // ?? Face presence ????????????????????????????????????????????? const hasFace = !!(faceAnalysis && faceAnalysis.faces && faceAnalysis.faces.length > 0); // ?? Condition scores ?????????????????????????????????????????? const scores = {}; // High-key: bright, low shadow, low contrast scores['High-key'] = clamp((avgBrightness - 0.55) * 4, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((0.22 - shadowRatio) * 5, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((0.38 - contrastRatio) * 4, 0, 1) * 0.5; // Low-key: dark, heavy shadow scores['Low-key'] = clamp((0.42 - avgBrightness) * 4, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((shadowRatio - 0.35) * 4, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((contrastRatio - 0.25) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.5; // Flat: low contrast, even distribution scores['Flat'] = clamp((0.35 - contrastRatio) * 5, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((0.12 - sideAsym) * 8, 0, 1) * 0.6 + clamp((0.12 - Math.abs(vertBias)) * 8, 0, 1) * 0.6; // Chiaroscuro: simultaneous deep shadow + bright highlight + high contrast scores['Chiaroscuro'] = clamp((shadowRatio - 0.25) * 4, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((highlightRatio - 0.10) * 5, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((contrastRatio - 0.38) * 4, 0, 1) * 1.0 + (lightingHardness === 'Hard' ? 0.5 : 0); // Silhouette: backlit subject, center darker than edges scores['Silhouette'] = (isBacklit ? 1.5 : 0) + clamp((highlightRatio - 0.15) * 4, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((0.55 - centerBri / 255) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.7; // Rembrandt: face + moderate side asymmetry + shadow/highlight balance scores['Rembrandt'] = hasFace ? clamp((sideAsym - 0.08) * 5, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((0.55 - avgBrightness) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.5 + clamp((highlightRatio - 0.05) * 6, 0, 1) * 0.6 + clamp((shadowRatio - 0.20) * 4, 0, 1) * 0.5 : 0; // Split: face + extreme horizontal asymmetry scores['Split'] = hasFace ? clamp((sideAsym - 0.25) * 4, 0, 1) * 1.5 + clamp((contrastRatio - 0.35) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.8 : clamp((sideAsym - 0.30) * 4, 0, 1) * 1.0; // Butterfly: face + top-down vertical light scores['Butterfly'] = hasFace ? clamp((vertBias - 0.12) * 5, 0, 1) * 1.5 + clamp((avgBrightness - 0.40) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.5 : 0; // Golden-hour: warm R:B ratio, medium brightness scores['Golden-hour'] = clamp((rbRatio - 1.35) * 3, 0, 1) * 1.2 + clamp((warmRatio - 0.30) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((avgBrightness - 0.35) * 2, 0, 1) * 0.5 + clamp((0.82 - avgBrightness) * 2, 0, 1) * 0.3; // Blue-hour: cool R:B ratio, low-medium brightness scores['Blue-hour'] = clamp((0.80 - rbRatio) * 3, 0, 1) * 1.2 + clamp((coolRatio - 0.28) * 3, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((0.48 - avgBrightness) * 4, 0, 1) * 0.5; // Overcast: low contrast, neutral color, mid brightness scores['Overcast'] = clamp((0.38 - contrastRatio) * 4, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((0.12 - Math.abs(warmRatio - coolRatio)) * 8, 0, 1) * 0.6 + clamp((avgBrightness - 0.35) * 2, 0, 1) * 0.4 + clamp((0.78 - avgBrightness) * 2, 0, 1) * 0.3; // ?? Pick winner ??????????????????????????????????????????????? let bestCondition = 'Flat', bestScore = -1; for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(scores)) { if (v > bestScore) { bestScore = v; bestCondition = k; } } // ?? Lighting type (source classification) ????????????????????? const warmBias = warmRatio - coolRatio; let lightingType; if (bestCondition === 'Golden-hour' || bestCondition === 'Overcast') lightingType = 'Natural'; else if (bestCondition === 'Blue-hour') lightingType = 'Natural'; else if (warmBias > 0.15 && shadowRatio > 0.25) lightingType = 'Practical'; else if (avgBrightness > 0.55 && Math.abs(warmBias) < 0.10) lightingType = 'Natural'; else if (warmBias > 0.08 || coolRatio > 0.30) lightingType = 'Artificial'; else lightingType = 'Mixed'; // ?? Confidence ???????????????????????????????????????????????? const sortedScores = Object.values(scores).sort((a, b) => b - a); const lightingConf = (sortedScores[1] > 0) ? clamp(sortedScores[0] / (sortedScores[0] + sortedScores[1]), 0.30, 0.99) : 0.80; // ?? Detail ???????????????????????????????????????????????????? const lightingDetail = [ `dir:${lightingDirection}`, `hard:${lightingHardness}`, `temp:${colorTemp}(${colorTempK}K)`, `rb:${rbRatio.toFixed(2)}`, `vBias:${vertBias.toFixed(2)}`, `hBias:${horizBias.toFixed(2)}` ].join(' '); return { lightingType, lightingCondition: bestCondition, lightingDirection, lightingHardness, colorTemp, colorTempK, lightingConf: Math.round(lightingConf * 100) / 100, lightingDetail }; } function sampleNormalizedRegionStats(pixels, w, h, left, top, right, bottom, step = 2) { const x1 = Math.max(0, Math.min(w - 1, Math.floor(left * w))); const y1 = Math.max(0, Math.min(h - 1, Math.floor(top * h))); const x2 = Math.max(x1 + 1, Math.min(w, Math.ceil(right * w))); const y2 = Math.max(y1 + 1, Math.min(h, Math.ceil(bottom * h))); let totalLum = 0, totalSat = 0; let warm = 0, cool = 0, shadow = 0, highlight = 0; let clippedShadow = 0, clippedHighlight = 0; let count = 0; for (let y = y1; y < y2; y += step) { for (let x = x1; x < x2; x += step) { const idx = (y * w + x) * 4; const r = pixels[idx], g = pixels[idx + 1], b = pixels[idx + 2]; const max = Math.max(r, g, b); const min = Math.min(r, g, b); const sat = max > 0 ? (max - min) / max : 0; const lum = r * 0.299 + g * 0.587 + b * 0.114; totalLum += lum; totalSat += sat; if (lum < 55) shadow++; if (lum > 200) highlight++; if (lum <= 12 && min <= 8) clippedShadow++; if (lum >= 245 || max >= 250) clippedHighlight++; if (r > b + 12 && r >= g - 4) warm++; if (b > r + 12) cool++; count++; } } if (!count) { return { avgLum: 0, avgBrightness: 0, avgSaturation: 0, warmRatio: 0, coolRatio: 0, shadowRatio: 0, highlightRatio: 0, clippedShadowRatio: 0, clippedHighlightRatio: 0 }; } return { avgLum: totalLum / count, avgBrightness: totalLum / (count * 255), avgSaturation: totalSat / count, warmRatio: warm / count, coolRatio: cool / count, shadowRatio: shadow / count, highlightRatio: highlight / count, clippedShadowRatio: clippedShadow / count, clippedHighlightRatio: clippedHighlight / count }; } function sampleNormalizedRingStats(pixels, w, h, box, padX = 0.05, padY = 0.06, step = 2) { if (!box) return null; const outer = { left: clamp(box.left - padX, 0, 1), top: clamp(box.top - padY, 0, 1), right: clamp(box.right + padX, 0, 1), bottom: clamp(box.bottom + padY, 0, 1) }; const x1 = Math.max(0, Math.min(w - 1, Math.floor(outer.left * w))); const y1 = Math.max(0, Math.min(h - 1, Math.floor(outer.top * h))); const x2 = Math.max(x1 + 1, Math.min(w, Math.ceil(outer.right * w))); const y2 = Math.max(y1 + 1, Math.min(h, Math.ceil(outer.bottom * h))); const innerX1 = Math.max(0, Math.min(w, Math.floor(box.left * w))); const innerY1 = Math.max(0, Math.min(h, Math.floor(box.top * h))); const innerX2 = Math.max(innerX1 + 1, Math.min(w, Math.ceil(box.right * w))); const innerY2 = Math.max(innerY1 + 1, Math.min(h, Math.ceil(box.bottom * h))); let totalLum = 0, totalSat = 0; let warm = 0, cool = 0, shadow = 0, highlight = 0; let count = 0; for (let y = y1; y < y2; y += step) { for (let x = x1; x < x2; x += step) { if (x >= innerX1 && x < innerX2 && y >= innerY1 && y < innerY2) continue; const idx = (y * w + x) * 4; const r = pixels[idx], g = pixels[idx + 1], b = pixels[idx + 2]; const max = Math.max(r, g, b); const min = Math.min(r, g, b); const sat = max > 0 ? (max - min) / max : 0; const lum = r * 0.299 + g * 0.587 + b * 0.114; totalLum += lum; totalSat += sat; if (lum < 55) shadow++; if (lum > 200) highlight++; if (r > b + 12 && r >= g - 4) warm++; if (b > r + 12) cool++; count++; } } if (!count) return null; return { avgLum: totalLum / count, avgBrightness: totalLum / (count * 255), avgSaturation: totalSat / count, warmRatio: warm / count, coolRatio: cool / count, shadowRatio: shadow / count, highlightRatio: highlight / count }; } function getLightingSubjectBox(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis) { const faceBox = faceAnalysis?.boxes?.[0]; if (faceBox) { return { left: faceBox.x, top: faceBox.y, right: faceBox.x + faceBox.width, bottom: faceBox.y + faceBox.height, source: 'face' }; } const pose = poseAnalysis?.primary; if (pose && Number.isFinite(pose.left) && Number.isFinite(pose.right) && Number.isFinite(pose.top) && Number.isFinite(pose.bottom)) { return { left: pose.left, top: pose.top, right: pose.right, bottom: pose.bottom, source: 'pose' }; } return null; } function hasMeaningfulText(value) { return typeof value === 'string' && value.trim() !== ''; } function hasUsefulNumber(value) { return Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0; } function pickValue(primary, fallback) { if (primary === undefined || primary === null) return fallback; if (typeof primary === 'string' && primary.trim() === '') return fallback; return primary; } function blendConfidence(primary, secondary) { const a = hasUsefulNumber(primary) ? primary : null; const b = hasUsefulNumber(secondary) ? secondary : null; if (a != null && b != null) return Math.round((Math.max(a, b) * 0.62 + Math.min(a, b) * 0.38) * 100) / 100; if (a != null) return a; if (b != null) return b; return 0; } function buildLightingSummary(lighting) { if (!lighting) return ''; const colorTemp = pickValue(lighting.lightingColorTemp, lighting.colorTemp); const parts = []; const base = [lighting.lightingType, lighting.lightingCondition].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim(); if (base) parts.push(base); if (lighting.lightingSubtype) parts.push(lighting.lightingSubtype); if (lighting.lightingDirection && lighting.lightingDirection !== 'Front') parts.push(`${lighting.lightingDirection} key`); if (lighting.lightingHardness && lighting.lightingHardness !== 'Mixed') parts.push(`${lighting.lightingHardness} quality`); if (lighting.lightingContrast && lighting.lightingContrast !== 'Medium') parts.push(`${lighting.lightingContrast} contrast`); if (colorTemp && colorTemp !== 'Neutral') parts.push(colorTemp); if (lighting.lightingMotivation && lighting.lightingMotivation !== 'Studio') parts.push(`${lighting.lightingMotivation} motivated`); return parts.join(' / '); } function buildLightingMetricSuffix(lighting) { if (!lighting) return ''; const keyFillRatio = pickValue(lighting.lightingKeyFillRatio, lighting.keyFillRatio); const rimStrength = pickValue(lighting.lightingRimStrength, lighting.rimLightStrength); const mixedColorContrast = pickValue(lighting.lightingMixedColorContrast, lighting.mixedColorContrast); const colorTempK = pickValue(lighting.lightingColorTempK, lighting.colorTempK); const parts = []; if (hasUsefulNumber(keyFillRatio)) parts.push(`K:F ${keyFillRatio.toFixed(1)}:1`); if (hasUsefulNumber(colorTempK)) parts.push(`${Math.round(colorTempK)}K`); if (hasUsefulNumber(rimStrength) && rimStrength > 0.18) parts.push(`rim ${Math.round(rimStrength * 100)}%`); if (hasUsefulNumber(mixedColorContrast) && mixedColorContrast > 0.18) parts.push(`mix ${mixedColorContrast.toFixed(2)}`); return parts.length ? ` Local cues: ${parts.join(', ')}.` : ''; } function buildLightingDetail(lighting) { const summary = buildLightingSummary(lighting) || [lighting?.lightingType, lighting?.lightingCondition].filter(Boolean).join(' ') || 'Unspecified lighting'; const keyFillRatio = pickValue(lighting?.lightingKeyFillRatio, lighting?.keyFillRatio); const rimStrength = pickValue(lighting?.lightingRimStrength, lighting?.rimLightStrength); const mixedColorContrast = pickValue(lighting?.lightingMixedColorContrast, lighting?.mixedColorContrast); const sentences = [`Primary read: ${summary}.`]; if (hasUsefulNumber(keyFillRatio)) sentences.push(`Key/fill sits near ${keyFillRatio.toFixed(1)}:1.`); if (hasUsefulNumber(rimStrength) && rimStrength > 0.2) sentences.push(`Rim separation is visible at about ${Math.round(rimStrength * 100)}%.`); if (hasUsefulNumber(mixedColorContrast) && mixedColorContrast > 0.28) sentences.push('Warm/cool source separation is noticeable.'); return sentences.join(' '); } function buildLocalEvidenceBlock(camera) { if (!camera) return ''; const lines = [ '', 'Local heuristic cross-check from the same frame set. Use it as evidence, not as a script:' ]; const cameraPrior = [camera.shotSize, camera.lensType, camera.angle, camera.movement].filter(Boolean).join(' / '); if (cameraPrior) lines.push(`- Local camera prior: ${cameraPrior}`); const lightingSummary = buildLightingSummary(camera); if (lightingSummary) lines.push(`- Local lighting prior: ${lightingSummary}`); const lightingMetricSuffix = buildLightingMetricSuffix(camera); if (lightingMetricSuffix) lines.push(`- Local lighting metrics:${lightingMetricSuffix.replace(' Local cues:', '')}`); const compositionPrior = [camera.composition, camera.compositionSubtype, camera.compositionBalance, camera.compositionDepth].filter(Boolean).join(' / '); if (compositionPrior) lines.push(`- Local composition prior: ${compositionPrior}`); if (hasMeaningfulText(camera.compositionDetail)) lines.push(`- Local composition evidence: ${camera.compositionDetail}`); return lines.join('\n'); } function buildAICameraFromParsed(parsed) { return { shotSize: parsed.shot_size || '', shotSizeConf: parsed.shot_size_confidence || 0, shotSizeDetail: parsed.shot_size_detail || '', framing: parsed.framing || '', lensType: parsed.lens_type || '', lensConf: parsed.lens_confidence || 0, lensDetail: parsed.lens_detail || '', movement: parsed.camera_movement || '', movementConf: parsed.movement_confidence || 0, movementDetail: parsed.movement_detail || '', mechanism: parsed.camera_mechanism || '', angle: parsed.camera_angle || '', angleConf: parsed.angle_confidence || 0, dof: parsed.depth_of_field || '', dofConf: parsed.dof_confidence || 0, dofDetail: parsed.dof_detail || '', lightingType: parsed.lighting_type || '', lightingCondition: parsed.lighting_condition || '', lightingDirection: parsed.lighting_direction || '', lightingHardness: parsed.lighting_hardness || '', lightingContrast: parsed.lighting_contrast || '', lightingColorTemp: parsed.lighting_color_temp || '', lightingMotivation: parsed.lighting_motivation || '', lightingSubtype: parsed.lighting_subtype || '', lightingConf: parsed.lighting_confidence || 0, lightingDetail: parsed.lighting_detail || '', composition: parsed.composition || '', compositionConf: parsed.composition_confidence || 0, compositionDetail: parsed.composition_detail || '', narrativePurpose: parsed.narrative_purpose || '' }; } function mergeCameraWithLocalEvidence(aiCamera, localCamera) { if (!localCamera) return aiCamera; const merged = { ...localCamera }; for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(aiCamera || {})) { if (value === undefined || value === null) continue; if (typeof value === 'string' && value.trim() === '') continue; merged[key] = value; } const aiLightConf = hasUsefulNumber(aiCamera?.lightingConf) ? aiCamera.lightingConf : 0; const localLightConf = hasUsefulNumber(localCamera.lightingConf) ? localCamera.lightingConf : 0; const aiHasLighting = hasMeaningfulText(aiCamera?.lightingCondition); const localHasLighting = hasMeaningfulText(localCamera.lightingCondition); const lightingMismatch = aiHasLighting && localHasLighting && ( aiCamera.lightingCondition !== localCamera.lightingCondition || pickValue(aiCamera.lightingSubtype, '') !== pickValue(localCamera.lightingSubtype, '') || pickValue(aiCamera.lightingDirection, '') !== pickValue(localCamera.lightingDirection, '') ); const useLocalLighting = !aiHasLighting || (lightingMismatch && localLightConf >= Math.max(0.62, aiLightConf + 0.12)); if (useLocalLighting && localHasLighting) { merged.lightingType = localCamera.lightingType; merged.lightingCondition = localCamera.lightingCondition; merged.lightingDirection = localCamera.lightingDirection; merged.lightingHardness = localCamera.lightingHardness; merged.lightingContrast = localCamera.lightingContrast; merged.lightingMotivation = localCamera.lightingMotivation; merged.lightingSubtype = localCamera.lightingSubtype; merged.lightingColorTemp = localCamera.lightingColorTemp; merged.lightingDetail = localCamera.lightingDetail; } else { merged.lightingType = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingType, localCamera.lightingType); merged.lightingCondition = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingCondition, localCamera.lightingCondition); merged.lightingDirection = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingDirection, localCamera.lightingDirection); merged.lightingHardness = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingHardness, localCamera.lightingHardness); merged.lightingContrast = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingContrast, localCamera.lightingContrast); merged.lightingMotivation = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingMotivation, localCamera.lightingMotivation); merged.lightingSubtype = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingSubtype, localCamera.lightingSubtype); merged.lightingColorTemp = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingColorTemp, localCamera.lightingColorTemp); merged.lightingDetail = pickValue(aiCamera.lightingDetail, localCamera.lightingDetail); } merged.lightingColorTempK = pickValue(aiCamera?.lightingColorTempK, localCamera.lightingColorTempK); merged.lightingKeyFillRatio = pickValue(aiCamera?.lightingKeyFillRatio, localCamera.lightingKeyFillRatio); merged.lightingRimStrength = pickValue(aiCamera?.lightingRimStrength, localCamera.lightingRimStrength); merged.lightingMixedColorContrast = pickValue(aiCamera?.lightingMixedColorContrast, localCamera.lightingMixedColorContrast); merged.lightingMetrics = pickValue(aiCamera?.lightingMetrics, localCamera.lightingMetrics); const aiLightingDetail = pickValue(aiCamera?.lightingDetail, ''); const localLightingDetail = pickValue(localCamera.lightingDetail, ''); if (hasMeaningfulText(aiLightingDetail) && !useLocalLighting) { merged.lightingDetail = `${aiLightingDetail}${buildLightingMetricSuffix(localCamera)}`; } else if (hasMeaningfulText(localLightingDetail)) { merged.lightingDetail = localLightingDetail; } else { merged.lightingDetail = buildLightingDetail(merged); } merged.shotSizeConf = blendConfidence(aiCamera?.shotSizeConf, localCamera.shotSizeConf); merged.lensConf = blendConfidence(aiCamera?.lensConf, localCamera.lensConf); merged.movementConf = blendConfidence(aiCamera?.movementConf, localCamera.movementConf); merged.angleConf = blendConfidence(aiCamera?.angleConf, localCamera.angleConf); merged.dofConf = blendConfidence(aiCamera?.dofConf, localCamera.dofConf); merged.lightingConf = blendConfidence(useLocalLighting ? localCamera.lightingConf : aiCamera?.lightingConf, localCamera.lightingConf); merged.compositionConf = blendConfidence(aiCamera?.compositionConf, localCamera.compositionConf); return merged; } async function getSceneLocalCamera(scene) { if (scene.localCameraAnalysis) return scene.localCameraAnalysis; try { scene.localCameraAnalysis = await analyzeFrameAdvanced(scene); } catch (err) { scene.localCameraAnalysis = generateLocalCamera(); } return scene.localCameraAnalysis; } function estimateLighting(colorAnalysis, composition, faceAnalysis, edgeMap, pixels, w, h, poseAnalysis) { const { avgBrightness, shadowRatio, highlightRatio, warmRatio, coolRatio, contrastRatio, avgR = 128, avgG = 128, avgB = 128, avgSaturation = 0.2, lumaStd = 0.1, clippedHighlightRatio = 0, clippedShadowRatio = 0, leftBrightness = avgBrightness, rightBrightness = avgBrightness, topBrightness = avgBrightness, bottomBrightness = avgBrightness, leftWarmRatio = warmRatio, rightWarmRatio = warmRatio, leftCoolRatio = coolRatio, rightCoolRatio = coolRatio } = colorAnalysis; const rbRatio = (avgR + 0.001) / (avgB + 0.001); let colorTemp, colorTempK; if (rbRatio > 1.85) { colorTemp = 'Very-warm'; colorTempK = 2700; } else if (rbRatio > 1.40) { colorTemp = 'Warm'; colorTempK = 3800; } else if (rbRatio > 0.90) { colorTemp = 'Neutral'; colorTempK = 5500; } else if (rbRatio > 0.68) { colorTemp = 'Cool'; colorTempK = 7000; } else { colorTemp = 'Very-cool'; colorTempK = 9000; } const R = composition.regions || []; const bri = i => (R[i] ? R[i].brightness : avgBrightness * 255); const topAvg = (bri(0) + bri(1) + bri(2)) / 3; const bottomAvg = (bri(6) + bri(7) + bri(8)) / 3; const leftAvg = (bri(0) + bri(3) + bri(6)) / 3; const rightAvg = (bri(2) + bri(5) + bri(8)) / 3; const centerBri = bri(4); const perimMax = Math.max(topAvg, bottomAvg, leftAvg, rightAvg, 1); const vertBias = (topAvg - bottomAvg) / 255; const horizBias = (rightAvg - leftAvg) / 255; const subjectBox = getLightingSubjectBox(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis); const subjectStats = subjectBox ? sampleNormalizedRegionStats(pixels, w, h, subjectBox.left, subjectBox.top, subjectBox.right, subjectBox.bottom) : null; const subjectLeft = subjectBox ? sampleNormalizedRegionStats(pixels, w, h, subjectBox.left, subjectBox.top, (subjectBox.left + subjectBox.right) / 2, subjectBox.bottom) : null; const subjectRight = subjectBox ? sampleNormalizedRegionStats(pixels, w, h, (subjectBox.left + subjectBox.right) / 2, subjectBox.top, subjectBox.right, subjectBox.bottom) : null; const subjectTop = subjectBox ? sampleNormalizedRegionStats(pixels, w, h, subjectBox.left, subjectBox.top, subjectBox.right, subjectBox.top + (subjectBox.bottom - subjectBox.top) * 0.56) : null; const subjectBottom = subjectBox ? sampleNormalizedRegionStats(pixels, w, h, subjectBox.left, subjectBox.top + (subjectBox.bottom - subjectBox.top) * 0.44, subjectBox.right, subjectBox.bottom) : null; const subjectRing = subjectBox ? sampleNormalizedRingStats(pixels, w, h, subjectBox) : null; const subjectHorizBias = subjectLeft && subjectRight ? (subjectRight.avgLum - subjectLeft.avgLum) / 255 : horizBias; const subjectVertBias = subjectTop && subjectBottom ? (subjectTop.avgLum - subjectBottom.avgLum) / 255 : vertBias; const modelingAsym = Math.abs(subjectHorizBias); const fillLum = Math.max(8, Math.min(subjectLeft?.avgLum ?? centerBri, subjectRight?.avgLum ?? centerBri)); const keyLum = Math.max(subjectLeft?.avgLum ?? centerBri, subjectRight?.avgLum ?? centerBri, centerBri); const keyFillRatio = Math.min(Math.max(keyLum / fillLum, 1), 12); const rimLightStrength = subjectRing && subjectStats ? clamp( ((subjectRing.avgLum - subjectStats.avgLum) / 65) + (subjectRing.highlightRatio - subjectStats.highlightRatio) * 2.8 + Math.max(subjectRing.avgSaturation - subjectStats.avgSaturation, 0) * 0.6, 0, 1 ) : clamp(((perimMax - centerBri) / 95) + highlightRatio * 1.2, 0, 1); const subjectShadowRatio = subjectStats?.shadowRatio ?? shadowRatio; const subjectHighlightRatio = subjectStats?.highlightRatio ?? highlightRatio; const subjectWarmSplit = subjectLeft && subjectRight ? Math.abs((subjectLeft.warmRatio - subjectLeft.coolRatio) - (subjectRight.warmRatio - subjectRight.coolRatio)) : 0; const mixedColorContrast = clamp( Math.min(warmRatio, coolRatio) * 4.2 + Math.abs((leftWarmRatio - leftCoolRatio) - (rightWarmRatio - rightCoolRatio)) * 1.8 + subjectWarmSplit * 1.4, 0, 1 ); const regionBrightness = composition.regions.map(region => (region?.brightness || 0) / 255).sort((a, b) => b - a); const hotspotIsolation = clamp(((regionBrightness[0] || 0) - (regionBrightness[1] || 0)) / 0.18, 0, 1); const warmBias = warmRatio - coolRatio; const naturalBias = clamp(1 - Math.abs(warmBias) * 2.6, 0, 1); const windowCue = Math.max( clamp((leftBrightness - avgBrightness) * 4.2, 0, 1) * clamp((composition.leftOpenness - 0.34) * 2.6, 0, 1), clamp((rightBrightness - avgBrightness) * 4.2, 0, 1) * clamp((composition.rightOpenness - 0.34) * 2.6, 0, 1), clamp((topBrightness - avgBrightness) * 4.0, 0, 1) * clamp((composition.topOpenness - 0.30) * 2.4, 0, 1) ); const sunlightCue = clamp((contrastRatio - 0.28) * 2.6, 0, 1) + clamp((clippedHighlightRatio - 0.01) * 10, 0, 1) * 0.6 + clamp((lumaStd - 0.10) * 6, 0, 1) * 0.5 + (colorTemp === 'Warm' || colorTemp === 'Very-warm' ? 0.18 : 0); const practicalCue = clamp((warmRatio - 0.18) * 3.2, 0, 1) + clamp((highlightRatio - 0.08) * 5, 0, 1) * 0.5 + hotspotIsolation * 0.55 + clamp((clippedHighlightRatio - 0.005) * 14, 0, 1) * 0.45; const mixedSourceCue = mixedColorContrast + clamp((avgSaturation - 0.20) * 2.5, 0, 1) * 0.25; const isBacklit = ( (centerBri / (perimMax + 1)) < 0.72 && highlightRatio > 0.08 ) || rimLightStrength > 0.62; const combinedVertBias = subjectVertBias * 0.68 + vertBias * 0.32; const combinedHorizBias = subjectHorizBias * 0.72 + horizBias * 0.28; let lightingDirection; if (isBacklit) lightingDirection = 'Back'; else if (combinedVertBias > 0.14 && combinedHorizBias > 0.08) lightingDirection = 'Top-right'; else if (combinedVertBias > 0.14 && combinedHorizBias < -0.08) lightingDirection = 'Top-left'; else if (combinedVertBias > 0.16) lightingDirection = 'Top'; else if (combinedVertBias < -0.14) lightingDirection = 'Bottom'; else if (combinedHorizBias > 0.12) lightingDirection = 'Right'; else if (combinedHorizBias < -0.12) lightingDirection = 'Left'; else lightingDirection = 'Front'; const hardnessScore = clamp( (contrastRatio - 0.24) * 2.6 + (lumaStd - 0.10) * 5 + (keyFillRatio - 1.8) * 0.16 + clippedHighlightRatio * 6 - Math.max(0, 0.18 - avgSaturation) * 0.4, 0, 1 ); let lightingHardness; if (hardnessScore > 0.66) lightingHardness = 'Hard'; else if (hardnessScore < 0.34 && contrastRatio < 0.30) lightingHardness = 'Soft'; else lightingHardness = 'Mixed'; let lightingContrast; if (keyFillRatio > 6 || contrastRatio > 0.52) lightingContrast = 'Extreme'; else if (keyFillRatio > 3.4 || contrastRatio > 0.38) lightingContrast = 'High'; else if (keyFillRatio > 1.9 || contrastRatio > 0.24) lightingContrast = 'Medium'; else lightingContrast = 'Low'; const hasFace = !!(faceAnalysis?.count > 0); const scores = {}; scores['High-key'] = clamp((avgBrightness - 0.54) * 4.2, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((0.24 - shadowRatio) * 5.2, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((0.34 - contrastRatio) * 4.5, 0, 1) * 0.6 + (lightingContrast === 'Low' ? 0.22 : 0); scores['Low-key'] = clamp((0.44 - avgBrightness) * 4.2, 0, 1) * 0.9 + clamp((shadowRatio - 0.34) * 4.2, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((keyFillRatio - 2.3) * 0.24, 0, 1) * 0.7 + clamp((contrastRatio - 0.26) * 3.5, 0, 1) * 0.5; scores['Flat'] = clamp((0.30 - contrastRatio) * 5.2, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((0.10 - modelingAsym) * 8, 0, 1) * 0.65 + clamp((1.8 - keyFillRatio) * 0.8, 0, 1) * 0.55 + (lightingHardness === 'Soft' ? 0.18 : 0); scores['Chiaroscuro'] = clamp((subjectShadowRatio - 0.22) * 4.2, 0, 1) * 0.8 + clamp((subjectHighlightRatio - 0.08) * 5.5, 0, 1) * 0.7 + clamp((contrastRatio - 0.34) * 4.5, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((keyFillRatio - 3.1) * 0.22, 0, 1) * 0.7 + (lightingHardness === 'Hard' ? 0.35 : 0); scores['Silhouette'] = (isBacklit ? 1.25 : 0) + rimLightStrength * 0.65 + clamp((0.55 - (subjectStats?.avgBrightness ?? centerBri / 255)) * 3.4, 0, 1) * 0.75 + clamp((subjectRing?.avgBrightness ?? perimMax / 255) - (subjectStats?.avgBrightness ?? centerBri / 255), 0, 1) * 0.7; scores['Rembrandt'] = hasFace ? clamp((modelingAsym - 0.10) * 5.5, 0, 1) * 0.9 + clamp((subjectVertBias - 0.05) * 5, 0, 1) * 0.45 + clamp((keyFillRatio - 2.0) * 0.22, 0, 1) * 0.55 + clamp((0.72 - (subjectStats?.avgBrightness ?? avgBrightness)) * 1.5, 0, 1) * 0.35 : 0; const subtypeScores = {}; subtypeScores['Split'] = hasFace ? clamp((modelingAsym - 0.22) * 4.4, 0, 1) * 1.1 + clamp((keyFillRatio - 4.0) * 0.22, 0, 1) * 0.8 + (['Left', 'Right'].includes(lightingDirection) ? 0.2 : 0) : 0; subtypeScores['Butterfly'] = hasFace ? clamp((subjectVertBias - 0.10) * 5.5, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((0.16 - modelingAsym) * 5, 0, 1) * 0.5 + (lightingDirection.startsWith('Top') || lightingDirection === 'Top' ? 0.18 : 0) : 0; subtypeScores['Golden-hour'] = clamp((rbRatio - 1.32) * 3.2, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((warmRatio - 0.28) * 3.5, 0, 1) * 0.7 + clamp((avgBrightness - 0.34) * 2.4, 0, 1) * 0.4; subtypeScores['Blue-hour'] = clamp((0.82 - rbRatio) * 3.4, 0, 1) * 1.0 + clamp((coolRatio - 0.26) * 3.5, 0, 1) * 0.7 + clamp((0.50 - avgBrightness) * 4.2, 0, 1) * 0.4; subtypeScores['Overcast'] = clamp((0.32 - contrastRatio) * 5.0, 0, 1) * 0.9 + clamp((0.12 - Math.abs(warmRatio - coolRatio)) * 8.5, 0, 1) * 0.55 + clamp((0.14 - modelingAsym) * 5.5, 0, 1) * 0.35; subtypeScores['Rim-lit'] = clamp((rimLightStrength - 0.24) * 1.45, 0, 1) * 1.0 + (lightingDirection === 'Back' ? 0.18 : 0); subtypeScores['Window-lit'] = windowCue * 0.8 + clamp((modelingAsym - 0.08) * 3.5, 0, 1) * 0.3 + (lightingDirection === 'Left' || lightingDirection === 'Right' || lightingDirection.startsWith('Top-') ? 0.12 : 0); subtypeScores['Neon-mixed'] = mixedSourceCue * 0.85 + clamp((avgSaturation - 0.24) * 3.4, 0, 1) * 0.35 + (lightingContrast === 'High' || lightingContrast === 'Extreme' ? 0.12 : 0); const rankedConditions = Object.entries(scores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]); let bestCondition = rankedConditions[0]?.[0] || 'Flat'; const bestConditionScore = rankedConditions[0]?.[1] || 0; if (subtypeScores['Split'] > 0.66 && scores['Chiaroscuro'] >= scores['Rembrandt']) bestCondition = 'Chiaroscuro'; if (subtypeScores['Butterfly'] > 0.66 && scores['High-key'] > scores['Flat']) bestCondition = 'High-key'; let lightingSubtype = null; const rankedSubtypes = Object.entries(subtypeScores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]); if ((rankedSubtypes[0]?.[1] || 0) > 0.44) lightingSubtype = rankedSubtypes[0][0]; let lightingMotivation = 'Studio'; if (practicalCue > 0.58 && practicalCue >= windowCue && practicalCue >= sunlightCue) lightingMotivation = 'Practical'; else if (windowCue > 0.54 && windowCue >= sunlightCue) lightingMotivation = 'Window'; else if (sunlightCue > 0.58 && sunlightCue >= windowCue) lightingMotivation = 'Sunlight'; else if (mixedSourceCue > 0.55) lightingMotivation = 'Mixed-source'; else if (bestCondition === 'High-key' && lightingHardness === 'Soft' && naturalBias > 0.55) lightingMotivation = 'Ambient'; let lightingType; if (lightingMotivation === 'Practical') lightingType = 'Practical'; else if (lightingMotivation === 'Sunlight' || lightingMotivation === 'Window' || ['Golden-hour', 'Blue-hour', 'Overcast'].includes(lightingSubtype)) lightingType = 'Natural'; else if (lightingMotivation === 'Mixed-source' || mixedColorContrast > 0.62) lightingType = 'Mixed'; else if (avgSaturation > 0.25 && (warmBias > 0.08 || coolRatio > 0.28)) lightingType = 'Artificial'; else if (naturalBias > 0.62 && contrastRatio < 0.42) lightingType = 'Natural'; else lightingType = warmBias > 0.06 || coolRatio > 0.30 ? 'Artificial' : 'Mixed'; const lightingConf = Math.round(clamp( 0.34 + bestConditionScore * 0.24 + ((rankedConditions[0]?.[1] || 0) - (rankedConditions[1]?.[1] || 0)) * 0.18 + (subjectStats ? 0.08 : 0) + (lightingSubtype ? 0.04 : 0), 0.36, 0.96 ) * 100) / 100; const result = { lightingType, lightingCondition: bestCondition, lightingSubtype, lightingDirection, lightingHardness, lightingContrast, lightingMotivation, colorTemp, colorTempK, keyFillRatio: Math.round(keyFillRatio * 10) / 10, rimLightStrength: Math.round(rimLightStrength * 100) / 100, mixedColorContrast: Math.round(mixedColorContrast * 100) / 100, lightingConf, metrics: { windowCue, sunlightCue, practicalCue, mixedSourceCue, bestConditionScore, subtypeScores, conditionScores: scores, subjectHorizBias, subjectVertBias, modelingAsym } }; return { ...result, lightingDetail: buildLightingDetail(result) }; } async function analyzeFrameAdvanced(scene) { // Draw the scene image to canvas for pixel analysis const img = new Image(); img.src = scene.image; await new Promise(r => { img.onload = r; }); const w = 640, h = Math.round(640 * (img.height / img.width)); frameCanvas.width = w; frameCanvas.height = h; ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h); const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h); const pixels = imageData.data; // 1. Edge detection (Sobel-like) for focus analysis const edgeMap = computeEdgeMap(pixels, w, h); // 2. Spatial composition analysis (where is visual weight?) const composition = analyzeComposition(pixels, w, h); // 3. Focus variance across regions (DOF estimation) const focusAnalysis = analyzeFocusRegions(edgeMap, w, h); // 4. Color distribution & contrast const colorAnalysis = analyzeColorDistribution(pixels, w, h); // 4.5. Subject detection when available const faceAnalysis = await analyzeFaces(frameCanvas, w, h); const poseAnalysis = await analyzePoseFrame(frameCanvas, w, h, faceAnalysis); // 5. Motion estimation (compare start/end frames if possible) const motionData = await estimateMotion(scene); // === SHOT SIZE ESTIMATION === let shotSize = estimateShotSize(composition, edgeMap, w, h, focusAnalysis, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis); let compositionTag = estimateCompositionTag(composition, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis, focusAnalysis, edgeMap); let lighting = estimateLighting(colorAnalysis, composition, faceAnalysis, edgeMap, pixels, w, h, poseAnalysis); // #2: multiFrames 3???ㅼ닔寃??ы몴 if (scene.multiFrames && scene.multiFrames.length >= 2) { try { const vCanvas = document.createElement('canvas'); const vCtx = vCanvas.getContext('2d'); const votes = [shotSize.type]; const compositionResults = [compositionTag]; const lightingResults = [lighting]; const compositionScoreTotals = Object.entries(compositionTag.scores || {}).reduce((acc, [label, score]) => { acc[label] = score; return acc; }, {}); for (const src of scene.multiFrames.slice(0, 2)) { const vi = new Image(); vi.src = src; await new Promise(r => { vi.onload = r; vi.onerror = r; }); if (!vi.width) continue; const vw = 320, vh = Math.round(320 * (vi.height / vi.width)); vCanvas.width = vw; vCanvas.height = vh; vCtx.drawImage(vi, 0, 0, vw, vh); const vpx = vCtx.getImageData(0, 0, vw, vh).data; const vc = analyzeComposition(vpx, vw, vh); const ve = computeEdgeMap(vpx, vw, vh); const vf = analyzeFocusRegions(ve, vw, vh); const vColor = analyzeColorDistribution(vpx, vw, vh); const vfa = await analyzeFaces(vCanvas, vw, vh); const vpa = await analyzePoseFrame(vCanvas, vw, vh, vfa); const vs = estimateShotSize(vc, ve, vw, vh, vf, vfa, vpa); const vComp = estimateCompositionTag(vc, vfa, vpa, vf, ve); const vLight = estimateLighting(vColor, vc, vfa, ve, vpx, vw, vh, vpa); votes.push(vs.type); compositionResults.push(vComp); lightingResults.push(vLight); Object.entries(vComp.scores || {}).forEach(([label, score]) => { compositionScoreTotals[label] = (compositionScoreTotals[label] || 0) + score; }); } const tally = {}; for (const v of votes) tally[v] = (tally[v] || 0) + 1; const best = Object.entries(tally).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]; if (best[1] >= 2 && best[0] !== shotSize.type) { shotSize = { ...shotSize, type: best[0], detail: shotSize.detail + ` [vote:${votes.join('/')}]` }; } const compositionVoteTally = {}; for (const result of compositionResults) { compositionVoteTally[result.type] = (compositionVoteTally[result.type] || 0) + 1; } const rankedComposition = Object.entries(compositionScoreTotals).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]); const [bestCompositionLabel, bestCompositionTotal] = rankedComposition[0] || [compositionTag.type, compositionTag.scores?.[compositionTag.type] || 0]; const bestCompositionVotes = compositionVoteTally[bestCompositionLabel] || 0; const currentCompositionAverage = (compositionScoreTotals[compositionTag.type] || 0) / compositionResults.length; const bestCompositionAverage = bestCompositionTotal / compositionResults.length; if ( bestCompositionLabel !== compositionTag.type && (bestCompositionVotes >= 2 || bestCompositionAverage > currentCompositionAverage + 0.08) ) { const reference = compositionResults .filter(result => result.type === bestCompositionLabel) .sort((a, b) => b.confidence - a.confidence)[0] || compositionTag; compositionTag = { ...reference, confidence: clamp( Math.max(reference.confidence, bestCompositionAverage * 0.78 + Math.min(0.12, bestCompositionVotes * 0.04)), 0.42, 0.95 ), detail: `${reference.detail} [votes:${compositionResults.map(result => result.type).join('/')}]`, metrics: { ...(reference.metrics || {}), multiFrameVotes: compositionResults.map(result => result.type) } }; } else if (bestCompositionVotes >= 2) { compositionTag = { ...compositionTag, confidence: clamp( Math.max(compositionTag.confidence, bestCompositionAverage * 0.72 + Math.min(0.1, bestCompositionVotes * 0.04)), 0.42, 0.95 ), detail: `${compositionTag.detail} [votes:${compositionResults.map(result => result.type).join('/')}]`, metrics: { ...(compositionTag.metrics || {}), multiFrameVotes: compositionResults.map(result => result.type) } }; } const pickLightingLabel = (field, fallback) => { const tally = {}; lightingResults.forEach(item => { const label = item?.[field]; if (!label) return; tally[label] = (tally[label] || 0) + Math.max(item.lightingConf || 0.4, 0.25); }); const bestLabel = Object.entries(tally).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]; return bestLabel ? bestLabel[0] : fallback; }; const averageLightingField = (field, fallback = null) => { const values = lightingResults.map(item => item?.[field]).filter(Number.isFinite); return values.length ? values.reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0) / values.length : fallback; }; const mergedLighting = { lightingType: pickLightingLabel('lightingType', lighting.lightingType), lightingCondition: pickLightingLabel('lightingCondition', lighting.lightingCondition), lightingSubtype: pickLightingLabel('lightingSubtype', lighting.lightingSubtype), lightingDirection: pickLightingLabel('lightingDirection', lighting.lightingDirection), lightingHardness: pickLightingLabel('lightingHardness', lighting.lightingHardness), lightingContrast: pickLightingLabel('lightingContrast', lighting.lightingContrast), lightingMotivation: pickLightingLabel('lightingMotivation', lighting.lightingMotivation), colorTemp: pickLightingLabel('colorTemp',
