lighting.colorTemp), colorTempK: Math.round(averageLightingField('colorTempK', lighting.colorTempK || 5500)), keyFillRatio: Math.round(averageLightingField('keyFillRatio', lighting.keyFillRatio || 1.8) * 10) / 10, rimLightStrength: Math.round(averageLightingField('rimLightStrength', lighting.rimLightStrength || 0) * 100) / 100, mixedColorContrast: Math.round(averageLightingField('mixedColorContrast', lighting.mixedColorContrast || 0) * 100) / 100 }; const dominantLightingMatches = lightingResults.filter(item => item.lightingCondition === mergedLighting.lightingCondition).length; const lightingReference = lightingResults .filter(item => item.lightingCondition === mergedLighting.lightingCondition) .sort((a, b) => (b.lightingConf || 0) - (a.lightingConf || 0))[0] || lighting; lighting = { ...lightingReference, ...mergedLighting, lightingConf: Math.round(clamp( lightingResults.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.lightingConf || 0.45), 0) / lightingResults.length + Math.min(0.08, Math.max(0, dominantLightingMatches - 1) * 0.04), 0.36, 0.97 ) * 100) / 100, metrics: { ...(lightingReference.metrics || {}), multiFrameConditions: lightingResults.map(item => item.lightingCondition), multiFrameTypes: lightingResults.map(item => item.lightingType) } }; lighting.lightingDetail = `${buildLightingDetail(lighting)} [votes:${lightingResults.map(item => item.lightingCondition).join('/')}]`; } catch (_) {} } // === LENS ESTIMATION === const lens = estimateLens(focusAnalysis, edgeMap, w, h, colorAnalysis, shotSize, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis); // === CAMERA MOVEMENT === const movement = motionData; // === ANGLE ESTIMATION === const angle = estimateAngle(composition, colorAnalysis, w, h, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis, edgeMap, shotSize); // === DOF ESTIMATION === const dof = estimateDOF(focusAnalysis, shotSize, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis); const framing = estimateFraming(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis, composition); // ?? ?숈뒿 DB ?곸슜 ?????????????????????????????????????????????????????? const _features = extractFeatureVector(composition, edgeMap, focusAnalysis, colorAnalysis); const _learnedOverrides = {}; for (const field of ['shotSize','framing','movement','lensType','angle','dof','lightingType','lightingCondition','composition']) { const match = findLearningMatch(_features, field); if (match) _learnedOverrides[field] = match.label; } const L = _learnedOverrides; // ?????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? return { shotSize: L.shotSize || shotSize.type, shotSizeConf: L.shotSize ? 1.0 : shotSize.confidence, shotSizeDetail: shotSize.detail, shotSizeMetrics: shotSize.metrics || null, framing: L.framing || framing, lensType: L.lensType || lens.type, lensConf: L.lensType ? 1.0 : lens.confidence, lensDetail: lens.detail, lensFocalRange: lens.focalRange ?? null, movement: L.movement || movement.type, movementConf: L.movement ? 1.0 : movement.confidence, movementDetail: movement.detail, movementDirection: movement.direction ?? null, movementSpeed: movement.speed ?? null, movementSmoothness: movement.smoothness ?? null, angle: L.angle || angle.type, angleConf: L.angle ? 1.0 : angle.confidence, angleDetail: angle.detail, angleTilt: angle.tilt ?? null, dof: L.dof || dof.type, dofConf: L.dof ? 1.0 : dof.confidence, dofDetail: dof.detail, dofFocusPlane: dof.focusPlane ?? null, dofSeparation: dof.separation ?? null, lightingType: L.lightingType || lighting.lightingType, lightingCondition: L.lightingCondition || lighting.lightingCondition, lightingDirection: lighting.lightingDirection ?? null, lightingHardness: lighting.lightingHardness ?? null, lightingContrast: lighting.lightingContrast ?? null, lightingMotivation: lighting.lightingMotivation ?? null, lightingSubtype: lighting.lightingSubtype ?? null, lightingColorTemp: lighting.colorTemp ?? null, lightingColorTempK: lighting.colorTempK ?? null, lightingKeyFillRatio: lighting.keyFillRatio ?? null, lightingRimStrength: lighting.rimLightStrength ?? null, lightingMixedColorContrast: lighting.mixedColorContrast ?? null, lightingConf: lighting.lightingConf ?? null, lightingDetail: lighting.lightingDetail ?? null, lightingMetrics: lighting.metrics ?? null, composition: L.composition || compositionTag.type, compositionConf: L.composition ? 1.0 : compositionTag.confidence, compositionDetail: L.composition ? 'Learned override from benchmark memory' : compositionTag.detail, compositionMetrics: compositionTag.metrics || null, compositionSubtype: compositionTag.compositionSubtype ?? null, compositionBalance: compositionTag.compositionBalance ?? null, compositionDepth: compositionTag.compositionDepth ?? null, _features, _learnedOverrides: Object.keys(_learnedOverrides).length > 0 ? _learnedOverrides : null }; } function computeEdgeMap(pixels, w, h) { const gray = new Float32Array(w * h); for (let i = 0; i < w * h; i++) { const idx = i * 4; gray[i] = pixels[idx] * 0.299 + pixels[idx+1] * 0.587 + pixels[idx+2] * 0.114; } const edges = new Float32Array(w * h); const orientationBins = new Float32Array(18); let totalEdge = 0; let axisEnergy = 0; let diagonalEnergy = 0; for (let y = 1; y < h - 1; y++) { for (let x = 1; x < w - 1; x++) { const gx = -gray[(y-1)*w+(x-1)] + gray[(y-1)*w+(x+1)] -2*gray[y*w+(x-1)] + 2*gray[y*w+(x+1)] -gray[(y+1)*w+(x-1)] + gray[(y+1)*w+(x+1)]; const gy = -gray[(y-1)*w+(x-1)] - 2*gray[(y-1)*w+x] - gray[(y-1)*w+(x+1)] +gray[(y+1)*w+(x-1)] + 2*gray[(y+1)*w+x] + gray[(y+1)*w+(x+1)]; const mag = Math.sqrt(gx*gx + gy*gy); edges[y*w+x] = mag; totalEdge += mag; if (mag > 12) { let lineAngle = (Math.atan2(gy, gx) * 180 / Math.PI) + 90; while (lineAngle < 0) lineAngle += 180; while (lineAngle >= 180) lineAngle -= 180; const bin = Math.max(0, Math.min(orientationBins.length - 1, Math.floor(lineAngle / 10))); orientationBins[bin] += mag; const axisDistance = Math.min( Math.abs(lineAngle), Math.abs(lineAngle - 90), Math.abs(lineAngle - 180) ); if (axisDistance < 12) axisEnergy += mag; else if (axisDistance > 18 && axisDistance < 72) diagonalEnergy += mag; } } } let dominantBin = 0; let dominantEnergy = 0; for (let i = 0; i < orientationBins.length; i++) { if (orientationBins[i] > dominantEnergy) { dominantEnergy = orientationBins[i]; dominantBin = i; } } const dominantAngle = dominantBin * 10 + 5; const axisTilt = Math.min( Math.abs(dominantAngle), Math.abs(dominantAngle - 90), Math.abs(dominantAngle - 180) ); edges.totalEdge = totalEdge; edges.avgEdge = totalEdge / (w * h); edges.dominantAngle = dominantAngle; edges.axisTilt = axisTilt; edges.axisEnergyRatio = totalEdge > 0 ? axisEnergy / totalEdge : 0; edges.diagonalEnergyRatio = totalEdge > 0 ? diagonalEnergy / totalEdge : 0; edges.orientationBins = Array.from(orientationBins); return edges; } function analyzeComposition(pixels, w, h) { // Divide into 3x3 grid and measure visual weight, detail, and spatial balance. const regions = Array(9).fill(null).map(() => ({ brightness: 0, edgeDensity: 0, count: 0, saturation: 0, visualWeight: 0, weightRatio: 0 })); const gridW = Math.max(1, Math.floor(w / 3)); const gridH = Math.max(1, Math.floor(h / 3)); const thirdPoints = [ [1 / 3, 1 / 3], [2 / 3, 1 / 3], [1 / 3, 2 / 3], [2 / 3, 2 / 3] ]; const phi = 0.618; const goldenPoints = [ [1 - phi, 1 - phi], [phi, 1 - phi], [1 - phi, phi], [phi, phi] ]; const hotspotAffinity = (nx, ny, targets, radiusX, radiusY) => { let best = 0; for (const [tx, ty] of targets) { const dx = (nx - tx) / radiusX; const dy = (ny - ty) / radiusY; const score = Math.exp(-(dx * dx + dy * dy) * 0.5); if (score > best) best = score; } return best; }; let centerWeight = 0, totalWeight = 0; let topHalf = 0, bottomHalf = 0; let skinTonePixels = 0; let leftWeight = 0, rightWeight = 0; let totalLum = 0; let weightedX = 0, weightedY = 0; let centerHotspot = 0, thirdsHotspot = 0, goldenHotspot = 0; let outerBandWeight = 0; const columnWeights = new Float32Array(w); const rowWeights = new Float32Array(h); for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) { for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) { const idx = (y * w + x) * 4; const r = pixels[idx], g = pixels[idx+1], b = pixels[idx+2]; const lum = r * 0.299 + g * 0.587 + b * 0.114; const max = Math.max(r, g, b), min = Math.min(r, g, b); const sat = max > 0 ? (max - min) / max : 0; const rightIdx = x < w - 1 ? idx + 4 : idx; const bottomIdx = y < h - 1 ? idx + w * 4 : idx; const rightLum = pixels[rightIdx] * 0.299 + pixels[rightIdx + 1] * 0.587 + pixels[rightIdx + 2] * 0.114; const bottomLum = pixels[bottomIdx] * 0.299 + pixels[bottomIdx + 1] * 0.587 + pixels[bottomIdx + 2] * 0.114; const localContrast = Math.abs(lum - rightLum) + Math.abs(lum - bottomLum); const gx = Math.min(Math.floor(x / gridW), 2); const gy = Math.min(Math.floor(y / gridH), 2); const ri = gy * 3 + gx; regions[ri].brightness += lum; regions[ri].saturation += sat; regions[ri].edgeDensity += localContrast; regions[ri].count++; // Weight detail and color separation more than flat luminance. const dx = (x / w - 0.5), dy = (y / h - 0.5); const distFromCenter = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy); const detailWeight = Math.min(localContrast, 160); const weight = lum * (0.3 + sat * 0.7) + detailWeight * 0.75; const nx = (x + 0.5) / w; const ny = (y + 0.5) / h; totalWeight += weight; totalLum += lum; weightedX += nx * weight; weightedY += ny * weight; centerHotspot += weight * hotspotAffinity(nx, ny, [[0.5, 0.5]], 0.16, 0.16); thirdsHotspot += weight * hotspotAffinity(nx, ny, thirdPoints, 0.16, 0.16); goldenHotspot += weight * hotspotAffinity(nx, ny, goldenPoints, 0.14, 0.14); regions[ri].visualWeight += weight; if (distFromCenter < 0.25) centerWeight += weight; if (distFromCenter > 0.36) outerBandWeight += weight; if (x < w / 3) leftWeight += weight; if (x > w * 2 / 3) rightWeight += weight; columnWeights[x] += weight; rowWeights[y] += weight; // Top vs bottom if (y < h / 2) topHalf += lum; else bottomHalf += lum; // Skin tone detection (rough heuristic) if (r > 95 && g > 40 && b > 20 && r > g && r > b && (r - g) > 15 && (max - min) > 15 && sat < 0.7 && sat > 0.1) { skinTonePixels++; } } } regions.forEach(r => { if (r.count > 0) { r.brightness /= r.count; r.saturation /= r.count; r.edgeDensity /= r.count; r.weightRatio = totalWeight > 0 ? r.visualWeight / totalWeight : 0; } }); let verticalDiff = 0, verticalBase = 0; for (let x = 0; x < Math.floor(w / 2); x++) { const left = columnWeights[x]; const right = columnWeights[w - 1 - x]; verticalDiff += Math.abs(left - right); verticalBase += left + right; } let horizontalDiff = 0, horizontalBase = 0; for (let y = 0; y < Math.floor(h / 2); y++) { const top = rowWeights[y]; const bottom = rowWeights[h - 1 - y]; horizontalDiff += Math.abs(top - bottom); horizontalBase += top + bottom; } const colWeights = [ regions[0].visualWeight + regions[3].visualWeight + regions[6].visualWeight, regions[1].visualWeight + regions[4].visualWeight + regions[7].visualWeight, regions[2].visualWeight + regions[5].visualWeight + regions[8].visualWeight ]; const rowWeights3 = [ regions[0].visualWeight + regions[1].visualWeight + regions[2].visualWeight, regions[3].visualWeight + regions[4].visualWeight + regions[5].visualWeight, regions[6].visualWeight + regions[7].visualWeight + regions[8].visualWeight ]; const avgRegionEdge = regions.reduce((sum, region) => sum + region.edgeDensity, 0) / 9; const avgRegionSat = regions.reduce((sum, region) => sum + region.saturation, 0) / 9; const avgComplexity = regions.reduce((sum, region) => sum + region.edgeDensity * (0.55 + region.saturation), 0) / 9; const opennessFor = indices => { const complexity = indices.reduce((sum, index) => { const region = regions[index]; return sum + region.edgeDensity * (0.55 + region.saturation); }, 0) / Math.max(indices.length, 1); return clamp(1 - complexity / Math.max(avgComplexity * 1.15, 0.001), 0, 1); }; const emptyRegionRatio = regions.filter(region => region.weightRatio < 0.09 && region.edgeDensity < avgRegionEdge * 0.9 && region.saturation < Math.max(avgRegionSat * 1.05, 0.16) ).length / 9; const totalPixels = w * h; return { regions, centerWeight: totalWeight > 0 ? centerWeight / totalWeight : 0, leftWeightRatio: totalWeight > 0 ? leftWeight / totalWeight : 0, rightWeightRatio: totalWeight > 0 ? rightWeight / totalWeight : 0, lrBalance: Math.abs(leftWeight - rightWeight) / Math.max(leftWeight, rightWeight, 1), avgBrightness: totalLum / (totalPixels * 255), centerBrightness: (regions[4].brightness || 0) / 255, outerBrightness: regions .filter((_, index) => index !== 4) .reduce((sum, region) => sum + region.brightness, 0) / (8 * 255), topHeavy: topHalf > bottomHalf * 1.15, bottomHeavy: bottomHalf > topHalf * 1.15, visualCentroidX: totalWeight > 0 ? weightedX / totalWeight : 0.5, visualCentroidY: totalWeight > 0 ? weightedY / totalWeight : 0.5, centerHotspotWeight: totalWeight > 0 ? centerHotspot / totalWeight : 0, thirdsHotspotWeight: totalWeight > 0 ? thirdsHotspot / totalWeight : 0, goldenHotspotWeight: totalWeight > 0 ? goldenHotspot / totalWeight : 0, outerBandWeightRatio: totalWeight > 0 ? outerBandWeight / totalWeight : 0, verticalSymmetry: verticalBase > 0 ? clamp(1 - verticalDiff / verticalBase, 0, 1) : 0, horizontalSymmetry: horizontalBase > 0 ? clamp(1 - horizontalDiff / horizontalBase, 0, 1) : 0, colWeights: colWeights.map(weight => totalWeight > 0 ? weight / totalWeight : 0), rowWeights: rowWeights3.map(weight => totalWeight > 0 ? weight / totalWeight : 0), emptyRegionRatio, leftOpenness: opennessFor([0, 3, 6]), rightOpenness: opennessFor([2, 5, 8]), topOpenness: opennessFor([0, 1, 2]), bottomOpenness: opennessFor([6, 7, 8]), skinToneRatio: skinTonePixels / totalPixels, hasFace: skinTonePixels / totalPixels > 0.03 }; } function analyzeFocusRegions(edgeMap, w, h) { // 7 spatial zones: center square, 4 periphery thirds, horizontal mid-band, outer ring const R = { center: 0, top: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0, right: 0, midBand: 0, outer: 0, cC: 0, tC: 0, bC: 0, lC: 0, rC: 0, mC: 0, oC: 0 }; const cx1 = w * 0.25, cx2 = w * 0.75, cy1 = h * 0.25, cy2 = h * 0.75; for (let y = 1; y < h - 1; y++) { const ny = y / h; for (let x = 1; x < w - 1; x++) { const nx = x / w; const e = edgeMap[y * w + x]; if (x > cx1 && x < cx2 && y > cy1 && y < cy2) { R.center += e; R.cC++; } if (ny < 0.33) { R.top += e; R.tC++; } if (ny > 0.67) { R.bottom += e; R.bC++; } if (nx < 0.33) { R.left += e; R.lC++; } if (nx > 0.67) { R.right += e; R.rC++; } if (ny > 0.25 && ny < 0.75) { R.midBand += e; R.mC++; } // tilt-shift band if (nx < 0.14 || nx > 0.86 || ny < 0.14 || ny > 0.86) { R.outer += e; R.oC++; } // frame edge } } const cs = R.cC > 0 ? R.center / R.cC : 0; // center sharpness const ts = R.tC > 0 ? R.top / R.tC : 0; // top sharpness (background proxy) const bs = R.bC > 0 ? R.bottom / R.bC : 0; // bottom sharpness (foreground proxy) const ls = R.lC > 0 ? R.left / R.lC : 0; const rs = R.rC > 0 ? R.right / R.rC : 0; const mbs = R.mC > 0 ? R.midBand / R.mC : 0; // full-width horizontal mid-band const ors = R.oC > 0 ? R.outer / R.oC : 0; // outermost ring const peripherySharpness = [ts, bs, ls, rs]; const avgPeriphery = (ts + bs + ls + rs) / 4; const sharpnessRatio = avgPeriphery > 0 ? cs / avgPeriphery : 1; const overallSharpness = edgeMap.avgEdge; // Spatial variance across 5 named zones const allZones = [cs, ts, bs, ls, rs]; const zm = allZones.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / 5; const zoneVariance = allZones.reduce((s, v) => s + (v - zm) ** 2, 0) / 5; return { centerSharpness: cs, avgPeriphery, sharpnessRatio, overallSharpness, peripherySharpness, topSharpness: ts, bottomSharpness: bs, leftSharpness: ls, rightSharpness: rs, midBandSharpness: mbs, outerRingSharpness: ors, centerBgRatio: ts > 0 ? cs / ts : 1, // center vs background (top region) centerFgRatio: bs > 0 ? cs / bs : 1, // center vs foreground (bottom region) midVsEdgeRatio: ors > 0 ? mbs / ors : 1, // horizontal band vs frame edge (tilt-shift) zoneVariance }; } function analyzeColorDistribution(pixels, w, h) { let totalR = 0, totalG = 0, totalB = 0; let highContrast = 0, lowContrast = 0; let shadowPixels = 0, highlightPixels = 0; let warmPixels = 0, coolPixels = 0; let totalSat = 0; let clippedHighlightPixels = 0, clippedShadowPixels = 0; let leftWarm = 0, rightWarm = 0, topWarm = 0, bottomWarm = 0; let leftCool = 0, rightCool = 0, topCool = 0, bottomCool = 0; let leftLum = 0, rightLum = 0, topLum = 0, bottomLum = 0; let leftCount = 0, rightCount = 0, topCount = 0, bottomCount = 0; const histogram = new Array(256).fill(0); for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) { for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) { const idx = (y * w + x) * 4; const r = pixels[idx], g = pixels[idx+1], b = pixels[idx+2]; const max = Math.max(r, g, b); const min = Math.min(r, g, b); const sat = max > 0 ? (max - min) / max : 0; const lum = Math.round(r * 0.299 + g * 0.587 + b * 0.114); const isWarm = r > b + 12 && r >= g - 4; const isCool = b > r + 12; totalR += r; totalG += g; totalB += b; totalSat += sat; histogram[Math.min(lum, 255)]++; if (lum > 200) { highContrast++; highlightPixels++; } if (lum < 55) { lowContrast++; shadowPixels++; } if (isWarm) warmPixels++; if (isCool) coolPixels++; if (lum >= 245 || max >= 250) clippedHighlightPixels++; if (lum <= 12 && min <= 8) clippedShadowPixels++; if (x < w / 2) { leftLum += lum; leftCount++; if (isWarm) leftWarm++; if (isCool) leftCool++; } else { rightLum += lum; rightCount++; if (isWarm) rightWarm++; if (isCool) rightCool++; } if (y < h / 2) { topLum += lum; topCount++; if (isWarm) topWarm++; if (isCool) topCool++; } else { bottomLum += lum; bottomCount++; if (isWarm) bottomWarm++; if (isCool) bottomCool++; } } } const totalPixels = w * h; const contrastRatio = (highContrast + lowContrast) / totalPixels; const avgR = totalR / totalPixels, avgG = totalG / totalPixels, avgB = totalB / totalPixels; const avgSaturation = totalSat / totalPixels; const lumaStd = estimateHistogramContrast(histogram, totalPixels); // Vignetting detection (darker edges = possible lens characteristic) let edgeLum = 0, centerLum = 0, eCnt = 0, cCnt = 0; for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) { for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) { const idx = (y * w + x) * 4; const lum = pixels[idx] * 0.299 + pixels[idx+1] * 0.587 + pixels[idx+2] * 0.114; const dx = x / w - 0.5, dy = y / h - 0.5; if (Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy) > 0.4) { edgeLum += lum; eCnt++; } else { centerLum += lum; cCnt++; } } } const vignetting = cCnt > 0 && eCnt > 0 ? (centerLum / cCnt) / (edgeLum / eCnt) : 1; return { avgR, avgG, avgB, avgBrightness: (avgR + avgG + avgB) / (255 * 3), contrastRatio, vignetting, histogram, shadowRatio: shadowPixels / totalPixels, highlightRatio: highlightPixels / totalPixels, warmRatio: warmPixels / totalPixels, coolRatio: coolPixels / totalPixels, avgSaturation, lumaStd, clippedHighlightRatio: clippedHighlightPixels / totalPixels, clippedShadowRatio: clippedShadowPixels / totalPixels, leftBrightness: leftCount ? leftLum / (leftCount * 255) : 0, rightBrightness: rightCount ? rightLum / (rightCount * 255) : 0, topBrightness: topCount ? topLum / (topCount * 255) : 0, bottomBrightness: bottomCount ? bottomLum / (bottomCount * 255) : 0, leftWarmRatio: leftCount ? leftWarm / leftCount : 0, rightWarmRatio: rightCount ? rightWarm / rightCount : 0, topWarmRatio: topCount ? topWarm / topCount : 0, bottomWarmRatio: bottomCount ? bottomWarm / bottomCount : 0, leftCoolRatio: leftCount ? leftCool / leftCount : 0, rightCoolRatio: rightCount ? rightCool / rightCount : 0, topCoolRatio: topCount ? topCool / topCount : 0, bottomCoolRatio: bottomCount ? bottomCool / bottomCount : 0 }; } async function estimateMotion(scene) { if (!scene.multiFrames || scene.multiFrames.length < 2 || scene.duration < 0.25) { return { type: 'Static', confidence: 0.45, detail: 'Too few comparison frames were available, so the motion defaults to Static.' }; } try { const frames = []; const targetWidth = 96; for (const source of scene.multiFrames.slice(0, 3)) { const img = new Image(); img.src = source; await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { img.onload = resolve; img.onerror = reject; }); const w = targetWidth; const h = Math.max(1, Math.round(targetWidth * (img.height / img.width))); frameCanvas.width = w; frameCanvas.height = h; ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h); const pixels = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h).data; const gray = new Float32Array(w * h); for (let i = 0; i < w * h; i++) { const idx = i * 4; gray[i] = pixels[idx] * 0.299 + pixels[idx + 1] * 0.587 + pixels[idx + 2] * 0.114; } frames.push({ gray, w, h }); } const compareTransform = (gray1, gray2, w, h, dx, dy, scale = 1, step = 4) => { const centerX = (w - 1) / 2; const centerY = (h - 1) / 2; const invScale = 1 / scale; let total = 0; let count = 0; for (let y = 0; y < h; y += step) { for (let x = 0; x < w; x += step) { const sx = Math.round(((x - centerX - dx) * invScale) + centerX); const sy = Math.round(((y - centerY - dy) * invScale) + centerY); if (sx < 0 || sx >= w || sy < 0 || sy >= h) continue; const idx1 = y * w + x; const idx2 = sy * w + sx; total += Math.abs(gray1[idx1] - gray2[idx2]); count++; } } return count ? total / count : Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY; }; const estimateTransform = (gray1, gray2, w, h) => { const baseError = compareTransform(gray1, gray2, w, h, 0, 0, 1); let best = { dx: 0, dy: 0, scale: 1, error: baseError }; const scaleCandidates = [0.92, 0.96, 1, 1.04, 1.08]; for (const scale of scaleCandidates) { for (let dy = -4; dy <= 4; dy++) { for (let dx = -6; dx <= 6; dx++) { const error = compareTransform(gray1, gray2, w, h, dx, dy, scale); if (error < best.error) best = { dx, dy, scale, error }; } } } return { ...best, baseError, gain: baseError > 0 ? (baseError - best.error) / baseError : 0, scaleDelta: best.scale - 1, scaleGain: baseError > 0 && best.scale !== 1 ? (baseError - best.error) / baseError : 0, magnitude: Math.hypot(best.dx, best.dy) }; }; const pairs = []; for (let i = 0; i < frames.length - 1; i++) { pairs.push(estimateTransform(frames[i].gray, frames[i + 1].gray, frames[i].w, frames[i].h)); } const avgMagnitude = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.magnitude, 0) / pairs.length; const avgDx = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.dx, 0) / pairs.length; const avgDy = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.dy, 0) / pairs.length; const avgGain = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.gain, 0) / pairs.length; const avgResidual = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.error, 0) / (pairs.length * 255); const avgScaleDelta = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.scaleDelta, 0) / pairs.length; const avgScaleGain = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.scaleGain, 0) / pairs.length; const avgAbsScale = pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + Math.abs(pair.scaleDelta), 0) / pairs.length; const sameXDirection = Math.abs(pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + Math.sign(pair.dx || 0), 0)) / pairs.length; const sameYDirection = Math.abs(pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + Math.sign(pair.dy || 0), 0)) / pairs.length; const sameScaleDirection = Math.abs(pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + Math.sign(pair.scaleDelta || 0), 0)) / pairs.length; if (avgMagnitude < 0.8 && avgResidual < 0.08 && avgAbsScale < 0.02) { return { type: 'Static', confidence: 0.84, detail: 'Inter-frame alignment changes are minimal, which is most consistent with a locked-off camera.' }; } if (avgAbsScale > 0.03 && sameScaleDirection > 0.6 && avgScaleGain > 0.1) { const inward = avgScaleDelta > 0; if (avgMagnitude < 1.1 && avgResidual < 0.09) { return { type: inward ? 'Zoom-in' : 'Zoom-out', confidence: clamp(0.56 + avgScaleGain, 0.56, 0.88), detail: `Scale change dominates with ${Math.round(avgAbsScale * 100)}% frame expansion, closest to ${inward ? 'Zoom-in' : 'Zoom-out'}` }; } return { type: inward ? 'Push-in' : 'Pull-out', confidence: clamp(0.54 + avgScaleGain, 0.54, 0.84), detail: `Forward/backward camera travel is more likely than a pure pan/tilt because scale and translation both change (${Math.round(avgAbsScale * 100)}%)` }; } if (avgGain < 0.08 && avgResidual > 0.11) { return { type: 'Handheld', confidence: 0.58, detail: 'Residual jitter stays high without a clean directional transform, which reads as handheld motion.' }; } if (Math.abs(avgDx) > Math.abs(avgDy) * 1.65 && Math.abs(avgDx) >= 4.2 && sameXDirection > 0.8) { return { type: 'Whip-pan', confidence: clamp(0.58 + avgGain * 0.7, 0.58, 0.9), detail: `Very fast horizontal sweep (${avgDx.toFixed(1)}px average) is closer to a whip-pan than a standard pan` }; } if (Math.abs(avgDx) > Math.abs(avgDy) * 1.45 && Math.abs(avgDx) >= 1.2 && sameXDirection > 0.6) { const direction = avgDx > 0 ? 'right' : 'left'; return { type: 'Pan', confidence: clamp(0.55 + avgGain * 0.8, 0.55, 0.86), detail: `Horizontal motion vectors remain consistent toward the ${direction}, which is closest to a pan.` }; } if (Math.abs(avgDy) > Math.abs(avgDx) * 1.45 && Math.abs(avgDy) >= 1.0 && sameYDirection > 0.6) { const direction = avgDy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up'; return { type: 'Tilt', confidence: clamp(0.54 + avgGain * 0.8, 0.54, 0.84), detail: `Vertical motion vectors stay coherent toward the ${direction}, which is closest to a tilt.` }; } if (avgMagnitude > 1.1 && avgGain > 0.16 && avgResidual < 0.11) { return { type: 'Tracking', confidence: clamp(0.52 + avgGain, 0.52, 0.83), detail: 'The whole frame shifts in a coherent direction, which is closer to tracking camera movement.' }; } if (avgMagnitude > 0.9 && avgGain > 0.1) { return { type: 'Steadicam', confidence: 0.48, detail: 'Motion is present but smoother than handheld and less axis-locked than a pan or tilt.' }; } return { type: 'Handheld', confidence: 0.42, detail: 'Small unstable shifts remain without clear axis coherence, so this falls back to handheld.' }; } catch (err) { return { type: 'Static', confidence: 0.35, detail: 'Motion analysis failed, so the result falls back to Static.' }; } } // #5: 鍮꾩씤媛??쇱궗泥댁슜 ?섏쭅 ?ъ쁺 遺꾩꽍 function _estimateSubjectHeightByProjection(edgeMap, w, h) { const vertProj = new Float32Array(h); for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) { let s = 0; for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) s += edgeMap[y * w + x]; vertProj[y] = s / w; } const mean = vertProj.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / h; const thr = mean * 1.3; let top = h - 1, bot = 0, found = false; for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) { if (vertProj[y] > thr) { if (!found) { top = y; found = true; } bot = y; } } return found ? (bot - top) / h : 0.5; } function estimateShotSize(composition, edgeMap, w, h, focus, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis) { const skinRatio = composition.skinToneRatio; const centerW = composition.centerWeight; const edgeDensity = edgeMap.avgEdge; if (poseAnalysis?.primary) { const pose = poseAnalysis.primary; const subjectHeight = pose.heightRatio; const subjectArea = pose.areaRatio; const rawFaceH = Math.max(faceAnalysis?.maxHeightRatio || 0, pose.faceHeightRatio || 0); const isGroupShot = poseAnalysis.count > 1; // #3: headRoom 蹂댁젙 ???ㅻ뱶猷몄씠 ?댁닔濡??ㅼ쭏 ?쇱궗泥?鍮꾩쑉 異뺤냼 const headRoomAdj = pose.headRoom > 0.12 ? Math.min((pose.headRoom - 0.12) * 0.55, 0.10) : 0; const faceHeight = Math.max(0, rawFaceH - headRoomAdj); let type = 'MS'; if (faceHeight >= 0.72 || subjectArea > 0.58) { type = 'ECU'; } else if (faceHeight >= 0.55 || subjectArea > 0.34) { type = 'BCU'; } else if (pose.cropLevel === 'face' || pose.cropLevel === 'chin' || (pose.cropLevel === 'head' && faceHeight >= 0.3) || faceHeight >= 0.38) { type = 'CU'; } else if (pose.cropLevel === 'throat' || pose.cropLevel === 'shoulders' || pose.cropLevel === 'chest' || faceHeight >= 0.22) { type = 'MCU'; } else if (pose.cropLevel === 'waist') { type = 'MS'; } else if (pose.cropLevel === 'cowboy') { type = 'Cowboy'; } else if (pose.cropLevel === 'knee') { type = 'MLS'; } else if (pose.cropLevel === 'full-tight' || pose.cropLevel === 'full' || pose.cropLevel === 'fullish') { if (subjectHeight < 0.18) type = centerW < 0.16 ? 'Establishing' : 'ELS'; else if (pose.cropLevel === 'full-tight' || subjectHeight >= 0.62 || (pose.headRoom < 0.1 && pose.footRoom < 0.1)) type = 'FS'; else if (subjectHeight < 0.42) type = 'LS'; else type = 'FS'; } else if (subjectHeight < 0.18) { type = centerW < 0.16 ? 'Establishing' : 'ELS'; } else if (subjectHeight < 0.34) { type = 'LS'; } else if (subjectHeight < 0.55) { type = 'FS'; } else if (subjectHeight < 0.72) { type = pose.lowerBodyRatio > 0.65 ? 'Cowboy' : 'MS'; } else { type = faceHeight > 0.26 ? 'MCU' : 'MS'; } if (isGroupShot) { if (poseAnalysis.count >= 3 && subjectHeight < 0.22) type = centerW < 0.18 ? 'Establishing' : 'ELS'; else if (poseAnalysis.count >= 3 && subjectHeight < 0.42) type = 'LS'; else if (type === 'ECU') type = 'CU'; else if (type === 'BCU') type = 'MCU'; else if (poseAnalysis.count === 2 && type === 'CU' && subjectHeight < 0.52) type = 'MCU'; } // #4: face 遺꾩꽍怨?媛以??ы몴 ??遺덉씪移섏떆 ?좊ː??湲곕컲 以묒옱 let crossConf = 0; if (faceAnalysis?.count > 0 && !isGroupShot) { const fh2 = faceAnalysis.maxHeightRatio; const fa2 = faceAnalysis.largestAreaRatio; let fType = 'MS'; if (fh2 > 0.8 || fa2 > 0.5) fType = 'ECU'; else if (fh2 > 0.6 || fa2 > 0.3) fType = 'BCU'; else if (fh2 > 0.4 || fa2 > 0.17) fType = 'CU'; else if (fh2 > 0.26 || fa2 > 0.095) fType = 'MCU'; else if (fh2 > 0.17 || fa2 > 0.055) fType = 'MS'; else if (fh2 > 0.11 || fa2 > 0.028) fType = 'Cowboy'; else if (fh2 > 0.075 || fa2 > 0.016) fType = 'MLS'; else if (fh2 > 0.05 || fa2 > 0.008) fType = 'FS'; else if (fh2 > 0.03 || fa2 > 0.004) fType = 'LS'; else fType = 'ELS'; if (fType === type) { crossConf = 0.07; // ?쇱튂 蹂대꼫?? } else { const poseW = pose.confidence * 2.0; const faceW = faceAnalysis.confidence * 1.5; if (faceW > poseW * 1.35) { type = fType; crossConf = -0.04; } else { crossConf = -0.03; } // 遺덉씪移??⑤꼸?? } } const conf = clamp( 0.56 + Math.min(pose.confidence * 0.22, 0.2) + Math.min(Math.max(subjectHeight - 0.15, 0) * 0.18, 0.12) + (faceAnalysis?.count > 0 ? 0.04 : 0) + (pose.hasMask ? 0.04 : 0) + crossConf, 0.56, 0.96 ); return { type, confidence: conf, detail: `Pose-guided: subject ${Math.round(subjectHeight * 100)}% tall, face ${Math.round(rawFaceH * 100)}% (adj ${Math.round(faceHeight * 100)}%), crop ${pose.cropLevel}, group ${poseAnalysis.count} ??${type}`, metrics: { subjectHeight, subjectArea, faceHeight: rawFaceH, effectiveFaceHeight: faceHeight, cropLevel: pose.cropLevel, poseCount: poseAnalysis.count, headRoom: pose.headRoom, footRoom: pose.footRoom } }; } if (faceAnalysis?.count > 0) { const faceArea = faceAnalysis.largestAreaRatio; const faceHeight = faceAnalysis.maxHeightRatio; let type = 'MS'; if (faceHeight > 0.8 || faceArea > 0.5) type = 'ECU'; else if (faceHeight > 0.6 || faceArea > 0.3) type = 'BCU'; else if (faceHeight > 0.4 || faceArea > 0.17) type = 'CU'; else if (faceHeight > 0.26 || faceArea > 0.095) type = 'MCU'; else if (faceHeight > 0.17 || faceArea > 0.055) type = 'MS'; else if (faceHeight > 0.11 || faceArea > 0.028) type = 'Cowboy'; else if (faceHeight > 0.075 || faceArea > 0.016) type = 'MLS'; else if (faceHeight > 0.05 || faceArea > 0.008) type = 'FS'; else if (faceHeight > 0.03 || faceArea > 0.004) type = 'LS'; else type = 'ELS'; return { type, confidence: clamp(faceAnalysis.confidence + 0.04, 0.62, 0.94), detail: `媛먯???理쒕? ?쇨뎬???꾨젅???믪씠??${Math.round(faceHeight * 100)}%, 硫댁쟻??${Math.round(faceArea * 100)}%瑜?李⑥???${type}??媛源앹뒿?덈떎` }; } if (centerW > 0.42 && focus.sharpnessRatio > 1.7 && skinRatio < 0.02) { return { type: 'INSERT', confidence: 0.58, detail: 'The frame centers on a small detailed subject with little surrounding context, which fits an insert shot.' }; } if (skinRatio > 0.2 && centerW > 0.4) { return { type: 'CU', confidence: 0.48, detail: 'The face or subject fills a large portion of the frame, which fits a close-up.' }; } if (skinRatio > 0.08 && composition.hasFace) { return { type: 'MCU', confidence: 0.44, detail: 'The subject reads closer than medium shot but looser than a close-up, which fits MCU.' }; } // #5: 鍮꾩씤媛??쇱궗泥????섏쭅 ?먯? ?ъ쁺?쇰줈 ?쇱궗泥??믪씠 異붿젙 const projH = _estimateSubjectHeightByProjection(edgeMap, w, h); if (skinRatio < 0.01 && centerW < 0.18 && edgeDensity < 8) { return { type: 'ELS', confidence: 0.52, detail: 'Environmental information dominates over the subject, which fits an extreme long shot.' }; } if (skinRatio < 0.02 && centerW < 0.24) { const t = projH < 0.3 ? 'ELS' : 'LS'; return { type: t, confidence: 0.50, detail: `?쇱궗泥대낫??怨듦컙 鍮꾩쨷??而?${t} 怨꾩뿴濡?異붿젙?⑸땲??(?섏쭅?ъ쁺 ${Math.round(projH*100)}%)` }; } if (skinRatio < 0.04) { const t = projH < 0.5 ? 'LS' : projH < 0.75 ? 'FS' : 'MS'; return { type: t, confidence: 0.42, detail: `?섏쭅 ?먯? ?ъ쁺 湲곕컲 ${t} 異붿젙 (?ъ쁺 ${Math.round(projH*100)}%)` }; } return { type: 'MS', confidence: 0.36, detail: 'The framing reads as a middle-distance shot, so it falls back to MS.' }; } function estimateLens(focus, edgeMap, w, h, color, shotSize, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis) { const sharpnessRatio = focus.sharpnessRatio; const vignetting = color.vignetting; const overallSharpness = focus.overallSharpness; const shotType = shotSize?.type || shotSize || ''; const pose = poseAnalysis?.primary || null; const faceHeight = faceAnalysis?.maxHeightRatio || 0; const edgeFaceDistortion = faceAnalysis?.count > 0 && faceHeight > 0.22 && (faceAnalysis.subjectCenterX < 0.22 || faceAnalysis.subjectCenterX > 0.78); if ((shotType === 'ELS' || shotType === 'LS' || shotType === 'Establishing') && sharpnessRatio < 1.25 && overallSharpness > 10) { return { type: 'Wide(16-35mm)', confidence: 0.72, detail: `Wide framing with deep focus is most consistent with a wide lens (${shotType})` }; } if ((shotType === 'CU' || shotType === 'BCU' || shotType === 'ECU') && sharpnessRatio > 1.65 && faceHeight > 0.22) { return { type: 'Telephoto(60-135mm)', confidence: 0.74, detail: `Close framing plus background separation points toward a telephoto portrait lens (${shotType})` }; } if (edgeFaceDistortion || (pose && pose.widthRatio > 0.55 && pose.centerX < 0.28)) { return { type: 'Wide(16-35mm)', confidence: 0.62, detail: 'Strong edge placement with a large nearby subject suggests wide-angle perspective stretch' }; } if ((shotType === 'MCU' || shotType === 'MS' || shotType === 'Cowboy') && sharpnessRatio > 1.2 && sharpnessRatio < 1.9) { return { type: 'Normal(35-60mm)', confidence: 0.68, detail: `Mid shot coverage with moderate depth separation is closest to a normal lens (${shotType})` }; } // Strong vignetting + shallow focus = likely wide aperture / portrait lens if (sharpnessRatio > 2.0 && vignetting > 1.3) { return { type: 'Telephoto(60-135mm)', confidence: 0.7, detail: 'Strong vignetting with shallow focus is more consistent with a telephoto or portrait-oriented lens.' }; } if (sharpnessRatio > 1.8) { return { type: 'Normal(35-60mm)', confidence: 0.58, detail: 'Moderate depth separation without extreme compression is closest to a normal lens.' }; } // Very uniform sharpness = likely wide angle or deep focus if (sharpnessRatio < 1.2 && overallSharpness > 10) { return { type: 'Wide(16-35mm)', confidence: 0.66, detail: 'Uniform sharpness across the frame is more consistent with a wide lens or deep-focus setup.' }; } if (sharpnessRatio < 1.3) { return { type: 'Normal(35-60mm)', confidence: 0.6, detail: 'The image reads as balanced and moderate rather than clearly wide or telephoto.' }; } if (vignetting > 1.4) { return { type: 'Telephoto(60-135mm)', confidence: 0.46, detail: 'Strong vignetting still suggests a telephoto-leaning lens choice.' }; } return { type: 'Normal(35-60mm)', confidence: 0.42, detail: 'Lens cues are mixed, so the fallback stays in the normal range.' }; } function estimateAngle(composition, color, w, h, faceAnalysis) { const topBright = composition.regions[0].brightness + composition.regions[1].brightness + composition.regions[2].brightness; const bottomBright = composition.regions[6].brightness + composition.regions[7].brightness + composition.regions[8].brightness; const topAvg = topBright / 3; const bottomAvg = bottomBright / 3; // High angle: ground/floor visible (bottom brighter or more detail at bottom) // Low angle: sky visible (top brighter) const verticalBias = (topAvg - bottomAvg) / Math.max(topAvg, bottomAvg, 1); if (verticalBias > 0.3 && composition.topHeavy) { return { type: 'Low', confidence: 0.58, detail: 'Brighter upper regions and top-heavy framing suggest a low-angle view.' }; } if (verticalBias < -0.3 && composition.bottomHeavy) { return { type: 'High', confidence: 0.58, detail: 'Brighter lower regions and bottom-heavy framing suggest a high-angle view.' }; } // Check for extreme top brightness (bird's eye) if (topAvg > 200 && bottomAvg < 100) { return { type: 'Overhead', confidence: 0.52, detail: 'A strong top-vs-bottom brightness split suggests an overhead or bird-eye view.' }; } // Check for Dutch angle via edge distribution asymmetry const leftEdge = composition.regions[0].brightness + composition.regions[3].brightness + composition.regions[6].brightness; const rightEdge = composition.regions[2].brightness + composition.regions[5].brightness + composition.regions[8].brightness; const horizontalTilt = Math.abs(leftEdge - rightEdge) / Math.max(leftEdge, rightEdge, 1); if (horizontalTilt > 0.35) { return { type: 'Dutch', confidence: 0.46, detail: 'Left-right imbalance suggests a dutch angle or tilted framing.' }; } if (faceAnalysis.count > 0 && faceAnalysis.subjectCenterY > 0.58) { return { type: 'Shoulder-level', confidence: 0.4, detail: 'The subject sits slightly low in frame, which reads closer to shoulder-level coverage.' }; } return { type: 'Eye-level', confidence: 0.38, detail: 'There is no strong vertical bias, so the angle falls back to eye level.' }; } function estimateDOF(focus) { const ratio = focus.sharpnessRatio; if (ratio > 2.5) { return { type: 'Very-shallow', confidence: 0.78, detail: 'Center sharpness dominates strongly over the rest of the frame, indicating very shallow depth of field.' }; } if (ratio > 1.8) { return { type: 'Shallow', confidence: 0.7, detail: 'Subject sharpness separates clearly from the background, which fits shallow depth of field.' }; } if (ratio > 1.3) { return { type: 'Moderate', confidence: 0.56, detail: 'The subject is sharper than the background, but the separation is moderate.' }; } return { type: 'Deep', confidence: 0.62, detail: 'Sharpness stays relatively even across the frame, which fits deep depth of field.' }; } function generateLocalCamera() { return { shotSize: 'MS', shotSizeConf: 0, shotSizeDetail: '濡쒖뺄 fallback', framing: 'Empty', lensType: 'Normal(35-60mm)', lensConf: 0, lensDetail: '', movement: 'Static', movementConf: 0, movementDetail: 'fallback', angle: 'Eye-level', angleConf: 0, dof: 'Moderate', dofConf: 0, dofDetail: '' }; } // Research-guided overrides for the remaining camera attributes. async function estimateMotion(scene) { if (!scene.multiFrames || scene.multiFrames.length < 2 || scene.duration < 0.25) { return { type: 'Static', confidence: 0.45, detail: 'Not enough comparison frames were available, so motion defaults to Static.', direction: null, speed: 'none', smoothness: 1.0 }; } try { const COARSE_W = 64; const FINE_W = 128; const MAX_FRAMES = Math.min(5, scene.multiFrames.length); const coarseFrames = [], fineFrames = [], subjects = [], sharpnessVals = []; let motionBlurDir = null; for (let fi = 0; fi < MAX_FRAMES; fi++) { const src = scene.multiFrames[fi]; const img = new Image(); img.src = src; await new Promise((res, rej) => { img.onload = res; img.onerror = rej; }); // Coarse frame (64px) ??gray + subject detection const cw = COARSE_W; const cPx = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, cw, ch).data; const cGray = new Float32Array(cw * ch); for (let i = 0; i < cw * ch; i++) { const p = i * 4; cGray[i] = cPx[p] * 0.299 + cPx[p+1] * 0.587 + cPx[p+2] * 0.114; } coarseFrames.push({ gray: cGray, w: cw, h: ch }); // Fine frame (128px) ??transform estimation + center sharpness + motion blur const fw = FINE_W; const fh = Math.max(1, Math.round(fw * (img.height / img.width))); frameCanvas.width = fw; frameCanvas.height = fh; ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, fw, fh); const fPx = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, fw, fh).data; const fGray = new Float32Array(fw * fh); for (let i = 0; i < fw * fh; i++) { const p = i * 4; fGray[i] = fPx[p] * 0.299 + fPx[p+1] * 0.587 + fPx[p+2] * 0.114; } fineFrames.push({ gray: fGray, w: fw, h: fh }); // Center-region sharpness (Laplacian proxy) for rack-focus detection const cx0 = Math.floor(fw * 0.25), cx1 = Math.floor(fw * 0.75); const cy0 = Math.floor(fh * 0.25), cy1 = Math.floor(fh * 0.75); let sharpSum = 0, sharpCnt = 0; for (let y = cy0; y < cy1 - 1; y++) { for (let x = cx0; x < cx1 - 1; x++) { sharpSum += Math.abs(fGray[y * fw + x + 1] - fGray[y * fw + x]) + Math.abs(fGray[(y+1) * fw + x] - fGray[y * fw + x]); sharpCnt++; } } sharpnessVals.push(sharpCnt ? sharpSum / sharpCnt : 0); // Motion blur direction (horizontal vs vertical gradient energy, first frame only) if (fi === 0) { let hG = 0, vG = 0; for (let y = 1; y < fh - 1; y++) { for (let x = 1; x < fw - 1; x++) { hG += Math.abs(fGray[y * fw + x + 1] - fGray[y * fw + x - 1]); vG += Math.abs(fGray[(y+1) * fw + x] - fGray[(y-1) * fw + x]); } } const bRatio = hG > 0 ? vG / hG : 1; motionBlurDir = bRatio < 0.65 ? 'horizontal' : bRatio > 1.55 ? 'vertical' : null; } } // ?? Transform comparison (translation + scale + rotation) ???????????????? const cmpT = (g1, g2, w, h, dx, dy, sc, rot, step) => { const cx = (w - 1) / 2, cy = (h - 1) / 2, inv = 1 / sc; const cosR = rot !== 0 ? Math.cos(-rot) : 1; const sinR = rot !== 0 ? Math.sin(-rot) : 0; let total = 0, cnt = 0; for (let y = 0; y < h; y += step) { for (let x = 0; x < w; x += step) { let rx = x - cx - dx, ry = y - cy - dy; if (rot !== 0) { const t = rx * cosR - ry * sinR; ry = rx * sinR + ry * cosR; rx = t; } const sx = Math.round(rx * inv + cx), sy = Math.round(ry * inv + cy); if (sx < 0 || sx >= w || sy < 0 || sy >= h) continue; total += Math.abs(g1[y * w + x] - g2[sy * w + sx]); cnt++; } } return cnt ? total / cnt : Infinity; }; // Two-pass estimation: coarse (64px, wide search) ??fine (128px, refine) const estimatePair = (c1, c2, f1, f2) => { const { gray: g1c, w: wC, h: hC } = c1, { gray: g2c } = c2; const { gray: g1f, w: wF, h: hF } = f1, { gray: g2f } = f2; const scales = [0.88, 0.92, 0.96, 1.0, 1.04, 1.08, 1.12]; const rots = [-4, -2, 0, 2, 4].map(d => d * Math.PI / 180); let best = { dx: 0, dy: 0, sc: 1, rot: 0, err: cmpT(g1c, g2c, wC, hC, 0, 0, 1, 0, 4) }; for (const sc of scales) { for (const rot of rots) { for (let dy = -7; dy <= 7; dy++) { for (let dx = -10; dx <= 10; dx++) { const e = cmpT(g1c, g2c, wC, hC, dx, dy, sc, rot, 4); if (e < best.err) best = { dx, dy, sc, rot, err: e }; } } } } // Fine refinement at 128px const sf = FINE_W / COARSE_W; const bdxF = best.dx * sf, bdyF = best.dy * sf; let bF = { dx: bdxF, dy: bdyF, sc: best.sc, rot: best.rot, err: cmpT(g1f, g2f, wF, hF, bdxF, bdyF, best.sc, best.rot, 2) }; for (const sc of [best.sc - 0.02, best.sc, best.sc + 0.02]) { for (const rot of [best.rot - Math.PI/180, best.rot, best.rot + Math.PI/180]) { for (let ddy = -2; ddy <= 2; ddy++) { for (let ddx = -2; ddx <= 2; ddx++) { const e = cmpT(g1f, g2f, wF, hF, bdxF + ddx, bdyF + ddy, sc, rot, 2); if (e < bF.err) bF = { dx: bdxF + ddx, dy: bdyF + ddy, sc, rot, err: e }; } } } } const fBase = cmpT(g1f, g2f, wF, hF, 0, 0, 1, 0, 2); const gain = fBase > 0 ? (fBase - bF.err) / fBase : 0; return { dx: bF.dx / sf, dy: bF.dy / sf, scale: bF.sc, rot: bF.rot, error: bF.err / 255, gain, scaleDelta: bF.sc - 1, magnitude: Math.hypot(bF.dx / sf, bF.dy / sf) }; }; const pairs = []; for (let i = 0; i < coarseFrames.length - 1; i++) { pairs.push(estimatePair(coarseFrames[i], coarseFrames[i+1], fineFrames[i], fineFrames[i+1])); } // ?? Aggregate statistics ????????????????????????????????????????????????? const N = pairs.length; const avgOf = k => pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + p[k], 0) / N; const avgMagnitude = avgOf('magnitude'); const avgDx = avgOf('dx'); const avgDy = avgOf('dy'); const avgGain = avgOf('gain'); const avgResidual = avgOf('error'); const avgScaleDelta = avgOf('scaleDelta'); const avgAbsScale = pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.abs(p.scaleDelta), 0) / N; const avgAbsRot = pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.abs(p.rot), 0) / N; const avgScaleGain = (() => { const sp = pairs.filter(p => Math.abs(p.scaleDelta) > 0.005); return sp.length ? sp.reduce((s, p) => s + p.gain, 0) / sp.length : 0; })(); const dirConX = Math.abs(pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.sign(p.dx || 0), 0)) / N; const dirConY = Math.abs(pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.sign(p.dy || 0), 0)) / N; const dirConSc = Math.abs(pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.sign(p.scaleDelta || 0), 0)) / N; const dirConRot= Math.abs(pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.sign(p.rot || 0), 0)) / N; // Velocity profile: smoothness = 1 ??(?/關) of per-pair magnitudes const mags = pairs.map(p => p.magnitude); const magMean = mags.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / N; const magStd = Math.sqrt(mags.reduce((s, v) => s + (v - magMean) ** 2, 0) / N); const smoothness = magMean > 0 ? Math.max(0, 1 - magStd / magMean) : 1.0; const speed = avgMagnitude < 0.7 ? 'none' : avgMagnitude < 2.0 ? 'slow' : avgMagnitude < 4.5 ? 'medium' : avgMagnitude < 8.0 ? 'fast' : 'very-fast'; // ?? Subject tracking ????????????????????????????????????????????????????? const subjectPresent = subjects.some(s => s.size > 0.07); const subDX = subjectPresent ? subjects[subjects.length-1].centerX - subjects[0].centerX : 0; const subDY = subjectPresent ? subjects[subjects.length-1].centerY - subjects[0].centerY : 0; const subDS = subjectPresent ? subjects[subjects.length-1].size - subjects[0].size : 0; const subStableXY = Math.abs(subDX) < 0.07 && Math.abs(subDY) < 0.07; const subStableSize = Math.abs(subDS) < 0.06; // ?? Rack-focus: monotonic sharpness change, camera otherwise still ??????? let isRackFocus = false; if (sharpnessVals.length >= 3) { const sMax = Math.max(...sharpnessVals), sMin = Math.min(...sharpnessVals); const sRange = sMax > 0 ? (sMax - sMin) / sMax : 0; const sTrend = Math.abs(sharpnessVals[sharpnessVals.length-1] - sharpnessVals[0]) / Math.max(sMax, 1); isRackFocus = sRange > 0.22 && sTrend > 0.14 && avgMagnitude < 1.8; } // ?? Direction label ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????? const dirLabel = (dx, dy) => { const ax = Math.abs(dx), ay = Math.abs(dy); if (ax < 0.4 && ay < 0.4) return null; if (ax > ay * 1.6) return dx > 0 ? 'right' : 'left'; if (ay > ax * 1.6) return dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up'; return `${dy < 0 ? 'up' : 'down'}-${dx > 0 ? 'right' : 'left'}`; }; // ?? Classification cascade ???????????????????????????????????????????????? // Static if (avgMagnitude < 0.7 && avgResidual < 0.07 && avgAbsScale < 0.018) { return { type: 'Static', confidence: 0.88, detail: 'Inter-frame motion stays near zero, which is most consistent with a locked-off shot.', direction: null, speed: 'none', smoothness: 1.0 }; } // Rack-focus (focus plane shift, camera locked) if (isRackFocus) { const sMax = Math.max(...sharpnessVals), sMin = Math.min(...sharpnessVals); const conf = clamp(0.62 + (sMax > 0 ? (sMax - sMin) / sMax * 0.5 : 0), 0.62, 0.90); return { type: 'Rack-focus', confidence: conf, detail: 'Camera position stays stable while focus-plane sharpness shifts, which fits rack focus.', direction: null, speed: 'none', smoothness: 1.0 }; } // Dutch-tilt (rotational motion) if (avgAbsRot > 1.8 * Math.PI / 180 && dirConRot > 0.65 && avgGain > 0.07) { const rotDir = pairs.reduce((s, p) => s + Math.sign(p.rot || 0), 0) > 0 ? 'clockwise' : 'counter-clockwise'; return { type: 'Dutch-tilt', confidence: clamp(0.55 + avgGain * 0.55, 0.55, 0.82), detail: `Frame rotation trends ${rotDir}, which is closest to a dutch-tilt move.`, direction: rotDir, speed, smoothness }; } // Dolly-zoom (background scales, subject size/position stable) if (subjectPresent && avgAbsScale > 0.030 && dirConSc > 0.60 && subStableXY && subStableSize) { const inward = avgScaleDelta > 0; return { type: 'Dolly-zoom', confidence: clamp(0.64 + avgScaleGain * 0.75, 0.64, 0.92), detail: `Background scale ${inward ? 'expands' : 'compresses'} while the subject stays comparatively stable, which fits a dolly zoom.`, direction: inward ? 'in' : 'out', speed, smoothness }; } // Zoom (optical: pure scale, minimal translation, low residual) if (avgAbsScale > 0.028 && dirConSc > 0.60 && avgScaleGain > 0.07 && avgMagnitude < 1.3 && avgResidual < 0.09) { const inward = avgScaleDelta > 0; return { type: inward ? 'Zoom-in' : 'Zoom-out', confidence: clamp(0.58 + avgScaleGain * 0.85, 0.58, 0.91), detail: `Optical scale changes by ${(avgAbsScale * 100).toFixed(1)}% with limited translation, which fits a ${inward ? 'zoom-in' : 'zoom-out'}.`, direction: inward ? 'in' : 'out', speed, smoothness }; } // Push-in / Pull-out (scale + translation combined) if (avgAbsScale > 0.024 && dirConSc > 0.55 && avgScaleGain > 0.055) { const inward = avgScaleDelta > 0; return { type: inward ? 'Push-in' : 'Pull-out', confidence: clamp(0.55 + avgScaleGain * 0.75, 0.55, 0.86), detail: `Scale change (${(avgAbsScale * 100).toFixed(1)}%) combines with translation, which fits a ${inward ? 'push-in' : 'pull-out'}.`, direction: inward ? 'in' : 'out', speed, smoothness }; } // Handheld (high residual, low directional coherence) if (avgGain < 0.085 && avgResidual > 0.10) { return { type: 'Handheld', confidence: 0.63, detail: 'Residual shake stays high without clean directional consistency, which reads as handheld.', direction: dirLabel(avgDx, avgDy), speed, smoothness: Math.max(0, smoothness - 0.2) }; } // Whip-pan if (Math.abs(avgDx) > Math.abs(avgDy) * 1.65 && Math.abs(avgDx) >= 4.2 && dirConX > 0.78) { return { type: 'Whip-pan', confidence: clamp(0.60 + avgGain * 0.65, 0.60, 0.93), detail: `A very fast horizontal sweep (avg ${avgDx.toFixed(1)}px) is closer to a whip-pan than a normal pan.`, direction: avgDx > 0 ? 'right' : 'left', speed: 'very-fast', smoothness }; } // Crane / Jib (vertical + scale + smooth) if (Math.abs(avgDy) > Math.abs(avgDx) * 1.25 && avgAbsScale > 0.012 && dirConY > 0.60 && smoothness > 0.55 && avgGain > 0.09) { return { type: 'Crane', confidence: clamp(0.56 + avgGain * 0.65 + smoothness * 0.1, 0.56, 0.85), detail: 'Vertical travel combines with scale change and smooth motion, which is closer to a crane or jib move.', direction: avgDy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up', speed, smoothness }; } // Drone / Aerial (very smooth, multi-axis, no subject) if (smoothness > 0.68 && avgMagnitude > 1.0 && avgGain > 0.10 && !subjectPresent && avgResidual < 0.105) { return { type: 'Drone', confidence: clamp(0.56 + smoothness * 0.28, 0.56, 0.82), detail: 'The move is smooth, multi-axis, and lacks a stable foreground subject, which is closer to drone or aerial motion.', direction: dirLabel(avgDx, avgDy), speed, smoothness }; } // Pan / Trucking (horizontal dominant) if (Math.abs(avgDx) > Math.abs(avgDy) * 1.40 && Math.abs(avgDx) >= 1.1 && dirConX > 0.58) { const dir = avgDx > 0 ? 'right' : 'left'; if (subjectPresent && subStableXY && avgAbsScale < 0.022 && avgResidual > 0.068) { return { type: 'Trucking', confidence: clamp(0.55 + avgGain * 0.65, 0.55, 0.84), detail: `The subject stays comparatively stable while the background slides ${dir}, which fits trucking motion.`, direction: dir, speed, smoothness }; } return { type: 'Pan', confidence: clamp(0.56 + avgGain * 0.75, 0.56, 0.88), detail: `Horizontal movement trends ${dir}, which is closer to a pan.`, direction: dir, speed, smoothness }; } // Tilt / Pedestal (vertical dominant) if (Math.abs(avgDy) > Math.abs(avgDx) * 1.40 && Math.abs(avgDy) >= 0.9 && dirConY > 0.58) { const dir = avgDy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up'; if (subjectPresent && subStableXY && avgAbsScale < 0.022 && avgResidual > 0.068) { return { type: 'Pedestal', confidence: clamp(0.53 + avgGain * 0.65, 0.53, 0.83), detail: 'The camera shifts vertically while holding the subject, which fits a pedestal move.', direction: dir, speed, smoothness }; } return { type: 'Tilt', confidence: clamp(0.55 + avgGain * 0.75, 0.55, 0.87), detail: `Vertical movement trends ${dir}, which is closer to a tilt.`, direction: dir, speed, smoothness }; } // Arc (subject stable, both axes, no scale) if (subjectPresent && subStableXY && avgMagnitude > 1.0 && avgGain > 0.10 && avgResidual < 0.115 && avgAbsScale < 0.026 && Math.abs(avgDx) > 0.65 && Math.abs(avgDy) > 0.45) { return { type: 'Arc', confidence: clamp(0.52 + avgGain * 0.72, 0.52, 0.84), detail: 'The camera moves around a relatively stable subject on both axes, which fits an arc move.', direction: dirLabel(avgDx, avgDy), speed, smoothness }; } // Tracking (subject stays in frame, camera follows) if (subjectPresent && subStableXY && avgMagnitude > 0.85 && avgGain > 0.09 && avgAbsScale < 0.030) { return { type: 'Tracking', confidence: clamp(0.55 + avgGain * 0.85, 0.55, 0.87), detail: 'The camera follows a subject that stays in frame, which fits tracking motion.', direction: dirLabel(avgDx, avgDy), speed, smoothness }; } // Steadicam / gimbal (smooth but no clear single axis) if (avgMagnitude > 0.80 && avgGain > 0.085 && smoothness > 0.50) { return { type: 'Steadicam', confidence: clamp(0.48 + smoothness * 0.24, 0.48, 0.74), detail: 'The move is smooth and mobile without a single dominant axis, which fits steadicam or gimbal movement.', direction: dirLabel(avgDx, avgDy), speed, smoothness }; } // Fallback handheld return { type: 'Handheld', confidence: 0.43, detail: 'Motion remains unstable without a cleaner classification, so it falls back to handheld.', direction: dirLabel(avgDx, avgDy), speed, smoothness: Math.max(0, smoothness - 0.15) }; } catch (err) { return { type: 'Static', confidence: 0.35, detail: 'Motion analysis failed, so the result falls back to Static.', direction: null, speed: 'none', smoothness: 1.0 }; } } function estimateLens(focus, edgeMap, w, h, color, shotSize, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis) { const sharpnessRatio = focus.sharpnessRatio ?? 1; const overallSharpness = focus.overallSharpness ?? 5; // New rich fields from updated analyzeFocusRegions const bgCompression = focus.centerBgRatio ?? 1; // center vs background (top) sharpness const outerRS = focus.outerRingSharpness ?? 0; const centerS = focus.centerSharpness ?? 0; // Radial falloff: how steeply sharpness drops from center to extreme edges // Telephoto wide-open ??steep drop; wide stopped-down ??flat profile const radialFalloff = (outerRS > 0 && centerS > 0) ? centerS / outerRS : sharpnessRatio; const vignetting = color.vignetting ?? 1; const shotType = shotSize?.type || shotSize || ''; const pose = poseAnalysis?.primary || null; const faceH = Math.max(faceAnalysis?.maxHeightRatio ?? 0, pose?.faceHeightRatio ?? 0); const subjectWidth = pose?.widthRatio ?? faceAnalysis?.boxes?.[0]?.width ?? 0; const diagER = edgeMap.diagonalEnergyRatio ?? 0; // Subject at frame edge ??wide-angle perspective distortion / stretch const edgeDistortion = ( (faceAnalysis?.count > 0 && faceH > 0.20 && (faceAnalysis.subjectCenterX < 0.22 || faceAnalysis.subjectCenterX > 0.78)) || (!!pose && subjectWidth > 0.50 && (pose.centerX < 0.28 || pose.centerX > 0.72)) ); // H/V line concentration from 18-bin orientation histogram // Wide/fisheye: barrel distortion curves lines ??energy spreads across many bins // Telephoto/normal: straight parallel H/V lines dominate // H??째: bins 0,1,16,17 | V??0째: bins 8,9,10 const bins = Array.isArray(edgeMap.orientationBins) ? edgeMap.orientationBins : Array(18).fill(0); const totalBinE = bins.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0); const hvE = bins[0] + bins[1] + bins[8] + bins[9] + bins[10] + (bins[16] ?? 0) + (bins[17] ?? 0); const hvConc = totalBinE > 0 ? hvE / totalBinE : 0.50; // high ??straight H/V lines (normal/tele) // Shot type shorthands const isInsert = shotType === 'INSERT'; const isECU_BCU = ['ECU', 'BCU'].includes(shotType); const isCU_up = ['CU', 'BCU', 'ECU'].includes(shotType); const isMid = ['MCU', 'MS', 'Cowboy', 'MLS'].includes(shotType); const isWide = ['LS', 'ELS', 'Establishing'].includes(shotType); // ?? Macro ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // INSERT-level framing of tiny subject, extremely thin focal plane if (isInsert && sharpnessRatio > 2.5 && overallSharpness > 5.5) { return { type: 'Macro', confidence: clamp(0.64 + (sharpnessRatio - 2.5) * 0.07, 0.64, 0.90), detail: `Insert-scale framing with extreme focus separation (${Math.round(sharpnessRatio * 10) / 10}:1) is consistent with macro photography.`, focalRange: 'macro' }; } // ?? Ultra-wide (<16mm) ???????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Signatures: extreme diagonal energy (barrel convergence), very deep focus, // everything sharp, edge subject distortion, wide scene const uwScore = clamp((diagER - 0.20) / 0.14, 0, 1) * 0.30 + clamp((1.12 - sharpnessRatio) / 0.18, 0, 1) * 0.25 + clamp((overallSharpness - 10.0) / 3.0, 0, 1) * 0.20 + (edgeDistortion ? 0.15 : 0) + (isWide ? 0.10 : 0); if (uwScore > 0.55 || (isWide && diagER > 0.27 && sharpnessRatio < 1.09 && overallSharpness > 11)) { return { type: 'Ultra-wide(<16mm)', confidence: clamp(0.58 + uwScore * 0.30, 0.58, 0.86), detail: `Extreme diagonal energy, deep focus (${Math.round(sharpnessRatio * 100) / 100}), and ${(diagER * 100).toFixed(0)}% diagonal emphasis point to an ultra-wide lens.`, focalRange: '8-16mm' }; } // ?? Super-telephoto (>135mm) ??????????????????????????????????????????????? // Signatures: very large face in ECU/BCU, extreme background compression, // very high sharpness ratio, straight H/V lines (no distortion) const stScore = clamp((sharpnessRatio - 2.0) / 1.2, 0, 1) * 0.35 + clamp((bgCompression - 1.8) / 1.2, 0, 1) * 0.30 + (isECU_BCU ? 0.20 : 0) + (faceH > 0.38 ? clamp((faceH - 0.38) / 0.28, 0, 1) * 0.15 : 0); if (stScore > 0.45 || (isECU_BCU && sharpnessRatio > 2.2 && faceH > 0.36)) { return { type: 'Super-telephoto(>135mm)', confidence: clamp(0.60 + stScore * 0.28, 0.60, 0.88), detail: `The subject dominates the frame while the background compresses heavily (${Math.round(bgCompression * 10) / 10}:1), which fits a super-telephoto lens.`, focalRange: '135mm+' }; } // ?? Telephoto (60-135mm) ??portrait / medium tele ????????????????????????? // Signatures: background bokeh (centerBgRatio high), shallow DOF, face in CU/MCU, // steep radial sharpness falloff, H/V line dominance (no barrel distortion) const teleScore = clamp((sharpnessRatio - 1.55) / 0.75, 0, 1) * 0.28 + clamp((bgCompression - 1.30) / 0.80, 0, 1) * 0.24 + clamp((radialFalloff - 1.35) / 1.00, 0, 1) * 0.14 + ((isCU_up || isMid) ? 0.14 : 0) + (faceH > 0.14 ? clamp((faceH - 0.14) / 0.28, 0, 1) * 0.12 : 0) + (hvConc > 0.46 ? clamp((hvConc - 0.46) / 0.20, 0, 1) * 0.08 : 0); if (teleScore > 0.32 || (isCU_up && sharpnessRatio > 1.60 && faceH > 0.16)) { return { type: 'Telephoto(60-135mm)', confidence: clamp(0.55 + teleScore * 0.33, 0.55, 0.88), detail: faceH > 0.16 ? `Close subject framing with background separation ${Math.round(bgCompression * 10) / 10}:1 and sharpness ratio ${Math.round(sharpnessRatio * 10) / 10} fits a telephoto lens.` : `Background compression and isolation cues (${Math.round(sharpnessRatio * 10) / 10}) lean toward a telephoto lens.`, focalRange: '60-135mm' }; } // ?? Wide (16-35mm) ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Signatures: moderate diagonal energy (mild barrel), deep focus, wide scene, // edge distortion of subjects, lower H/V concentration const wideScore = clamp((diagER - 0.16) / 0.14, 0, 1) * 0.28 + clamp((1.25 - sharpnessRatio) / 0.20, 0, 1) * 0.26 + clamp((overallSharpness - 8.0) / 4.0, 0, 1) * 0.18 + (edgeDistortion ? 0.14 : 0) + (isWide ? 0.10 : 0) + (hvConc < 0.46 ? clamp((0.46 - hvConc) / 0.15, 0, 1) * 0.04 : 0); if (wideScore > 0.30 || edgeDistortion) { return { type: 'Wide(16-35mm)', confidence: clamp(0.52 + wideScore * 0.30, 0.52, 0.82), detail: edgeDistortion ? 'Edge subject stretch and perspective expansion suggest a wide lens.' : `Open spatial coverage, deep focus, and ${(diagER * 100).toFixed(0)}% diagonal energy suggest a wide lens.`, focalRange: '16-35mm' }; } // ?? Normal (35-60mm) ??default ???????????????????????????????????????????? // Natural perspective, no strong distortion, balanced H/V vs diagonal, mid shots const normalConf = clamp( 0.46 + (isMid ? 0.14 : 0) + clamp(1 - Math.abs(sharpnessRatio - 1.35) / 0.45, 0, 1) * 0.12 + clamp(1 - Math.abs(diagER - 0.20) / 0.12, 0, 1) * 0.08, 0.46, 0.74 ); return { type: 'Normal(35-60mm)', confidence: normalConf, detail: isMid ? `${shotType} framing with balanced perspective and moderate depth cues fits a normal lens.` : 'Wide and telephoto cues are mixed, so the fallback stays in the normal lens range.', focalRange: '35-60mm' }; } function estimateAngle(composition, color, w, h, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis, edgeMap, shotSize) { const shotType = shotSize?.type || shotSize || ''; const subject = getPrimarySubject(faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis); const pose = poseAnalysis?.primary || null; // ?? 1. Brightness / weight signals ?????????????????????????????????????? const topAvg = (composition.regions[0].brightness + composition.regions[1].brightness + composition.regions[2].brightness) / 3; const midAvg = (composition.regions[3].brightness + composition.regions[4].brightness + composition.regions[5].brightness) / 3; const bottomAvg = (composition.regions[6].brightness + composition.regions[7].brightness + composition.regions[8].brightness) / 3; // vertBias: +1 = top much brighter (low angle toward sky), ?? = bottom much brighter (high angle) const vertBias = (topAvg - bottomAvg) / Math.max(topAvg, bottomAvg, 1); // Row visual weight distribution [top, mid, bottom] (normalized) const [rowTop, rowMid, rowBot] = composition.rowWeights || [0.333, 0.334, 0.333]; const centroidY = composition.visualCentroidY ?? 0.5; // ?? 2. Environment proxies ???????????????????????????????????????????????? // Edge density per row (sky = low detail; ground = often low detail but darker) const topEdge = (composition.regions[0].edgeDensity + composition.regions[1].edgeDensity + composition.regions[2].edgeDensity) / 3; const botEdge = (composition.regions[6].edgeDensity + composition.regions[7].edgeDensity + composition.regions[8].edgeDensity) / 3; const edgeRatio = topEdge / Math.max(botEdge, 0.001); // < 0.65 ??open/plain top region // Sky: bright top + structurally open + cool/neutral tones const skyLikely = topAvg > 152 && composition.topOpenness > 0.48 && edgeRatio < 0.72 && (color.coolRatio > 0.12 || topAvg > 185 || color.avgBrightness > 0.60); // Ground/floor: uniform low-detail bottom (flat surface texture) const groundLikely = botEdge < topEdge * 0.60 && composition.bottomOpenness > 0.46 && bottomAvg < topAvg * 1.20; // ?? 3. Subject geometry ??????????????????????????????????????????????????? const subjectY = subject?.centerY ?? 0.5; const subjectSize = subject?.size ?? 0; // heightRatio (0-1) const faceH = subject?.faceHeight ?? 0; // face height as fraction of frame // Foreshortening proxy: faceToBody = face height / total subject height // Low angle ??see under-chin ??small face relative to body (< 0.25) // High angle ??see top-of-head ??large face relative to body (> 0.55) const faceToBody = subjectSize > 0.06 ? faceH / subjectSize : 0.35; // ?? 4. Dutch angle ??multi-signal score ?????????????????????????????????? const lrLeft = composition.regions[0].brightness + composition.regions[3].brightness + composition.regions[6].brightness; const lrRight = composition.regions[2].brightness + composition.regions[5].brightness + composition.regions[8].brightness; const lrAsym = Math.abs(lrLeft - lrRight) / Math.max(lrLeft + lrRight, 1); const dutchScore = clamp((edgeMap.axisTilt - 8) / 20, 0, 1) * 0.50 + clamp((edgeMap.diagonalEnergyRatio - 0.18) / 0.14, 0, 1) * 0.30 + clamp((lrAsym - 0.14) / 0.18, 0, 1) * 0.20; if (dutchScore > 0.40 || (edgeMap.axisTilt > 18 && edgeMap.diagonalEnergyRatio > 0.20)) { const tiltDeg = Math.round(edgeMap.axisTilt); return { type: 'Dutch', confidence: clamp(0.54 + dutchScore * 0.38, 0.54, 0.85), detail: `The dominant frame axis tilts by about ${tiltDeg} degrees, which fits dutch-angle framing.`, tilt: tiltDeg }; } // ?? 5. Bird's-eye (camera straight down, 85-90째) ???????????????????????? // Flat perspective + no strong subject + visual centroid near center + even brightness const flatPerspective = edgeMap.diagonalEnergyRatio < 0.15 && (edgeMap.axisEnergyRatio ?? 1) > 0.65; if ( (!subject || subjectSize < 0.10) && (shotType === 'ELS' || shotType === 'Establishing' || shotType === 'LS') && flatPerspective && Math.abs(centroidY - 0.50) < 0.18 && composition.centerWeight < 0.22 && Math.abs(vertBias) < 0.12 ) { return { type: "Bird's-eye", confidence: 0.66, detail: 'Flat top-down geometry with minimal subject prominence suggests a bird-eye view.', tilt: 90 }; } // ?? 6. Aerial (steep downward, ~50-80째) ?????????????????????????????????? if ( (!subject || subjectSize < 0.14) && (shotType === 'ELS' || shotType === 'Establishing' || shotType === 'LS') && vertBias < -0.20 && composition.bottomHeavy ) { return { type: 'Aerial', confidence: clamp(0.54 + Math.abs(vertBias) * 0.35, 0.54, 0.74), detail: 'A steep downward view over space and layout suggests an aerial angle.', tilt: 65 }; } // ?? 7. Subject-present: score-based classification ??????????????????????? if (subject) { // WORM'S-EYE: extreme low angle, camera near ground pointing straight up // ??face/head at very top of frame, tall body fill, sky/ceiling visible, under-chin view const wormsScore = clamp((0.30 - subjectY) / 0.22, 0, 1) * 0.40 + (skyLikely ? 0.22 : 0) + clamp((vertBias - 0.15) / 0.35, 0, 1) * 0.18 + clamp((subjectSize - 0.55) / 0.30, 0, 1) * 0.12 + (faceToBody < 0.22 && subjectSize > 0.45 ? 0.08 : 0); // LOW: camera below subject eye level, looking up 15-45째 // ??subject in upper frame, sky often visible, top brighter const lowScore = clamp((0.44 - subjectY) / 0.28, 0, 1) * 0.38 + (skyLikely ? 0.18 : 0) + clamp((vertBias - 0.08) / 0.35, 0, 1) * 0.20 + (composition.topOpenness > 0.50 ? 0.10 : 0) + (rowTop > 0.38 ? clamp((rowTop - 0.38) / 0.20, 0, 1) * 0.10 : 0) + (faceToBody < 0.28 && subjectSize > 0.22 ? 0.04 : 0); // HIGH: camera above subject, looking down 15-45째 // ??subject in lower frame, floor/ground visible, top brighter or darker const highScore = clamp((subjectY - 0.55) / 0.28, 0, 1) * 0.38 + clamp((-vertBias - 0.08) / 0.28, 0, 1) * 0.22 + (composition.bottomHeavy ? 0.12 : 0) + (groundLikely ? 0.14 : 0) + (rowBot > 0.38 ? clamp((rowBot - 0.38) / 0.20, 0, 1) * 0.10 : 0) + (faceToBody > 0.52 && subjectSize > 0.15 ? 0.04 : 0); // EYE-LEVEL: camera at subject eye height, ~0째 tilt // ??subject centered vertically, balanced brightness, centroid near middle const eyeScore = clamp(1 - Math.abs(subjectY - 0.50) / 0.17, 0, 1) * 0.40 + clamp(1 - Math.abs(vertBias) / 0.15, 0, 1) * 0.28 + clamp(1 - Math.abs(centroidY - 0.50) / 0.16, 0, 1) * 0.18 + (Math.abs(rowTop - rowBot) < 0.08 ? 0.14 : 0); // SHOULDER-LEVEL: slightly below eye, ~5-15째 downward, common dialogue/interview // ??subject in upper-center, MCU/CU shots, minimal vertical bias const shoulderScore = clamp(1 - Math.abs(subjectY - 0.56) / 0.14, 0, 1) * 0.40 + clamp(1 - Math.abs(vertBias - 0.04) / 0.12, 0, 1) * 0.22 + (['MCU', 'CU', 'BCU', 'MS', 'Cowboy'].includes(shotType) ? 0.24 : 0) + (faceH > 0.12 && faceH < 0.40 ? 0.14 : 0); // Pick winner ??require a minimum confidence threshold const candidates = { "Worm's-eye": { score: wormsScore, minThresh: 0.46, tilt: -65 }, 'Low': { score: lowScore, minThresh: 0.30, tilt: -25 }, 'High': { score: highScore, minThresh: 0.30, tilt: 28 }, 'Eye-level': { score: eyeScore, minThresh: 0.38, tilt: 0 }, 'Shoulder-level': { score: shoulderScore, minThresh: 0.36, tilt: 8 } }; let bestType = null, bestScore = 0; for (const [type, { score, minThresh, tilt }] of Object.entries(candidates)) { if (score > bestScore && score >= minThresh) { bestType = type; bestScore = score; } } if (bestType) { const tilts = { "Worm's-eye": -65, 'Low': -25, 'High': 28, 'Eye-level': 0, 'Shoulder-level': 8 }; const details = { "Worm's-eye": 'The subject rises from near the top edge with strong upward perspective, which fits a worm-eye angle.', 'Low': 'The subject sits high in frame and the camera appears to look upward, which fits a low angle.', 'High': 'The subject sits lower in frame and the camera appears to look downward, which fits a high angle.', 'Shoulder-level': 'The frame sits slightly below eye height, which reads closer to shoulder-level coverage.', 'Eye-level': 'The subject aligns near camera height without a strong vertical bias, which fits eye level.' }; return { type: bestType, confidence: clamp(0.48 + bestScore * 0.52, 0.48, 0.88), detail: details[bestType], tilt: tilts[bestType] }; } } // ?? 8. Subject-absent fallbacks ???????????????????????????????????????? if (!subject) { if (composition.centerWeight < 0.16 && composition.bottomHeavy && vertBias < -0.14) { return { type: 'Overhead', confidence: 0.50, detail: 'A centered top-down layout with little subject prominence suggests an overhead angle.', tilt: 60 }; } if (skyLikely && vertBias > 0.14) { return { type: 'Low', confidence: 0.48, detail: 'An open upper frame and upward bias suggest a low angle.', tilt: -20 }; } if (vertBias < -0.20 && composition.bottomHeavy) { return { type: 'High', confidence: 0.47, detail: 'Downward framing without a dominant subject suggests a high angle.', tilt: 28 }; } } return { type: 'Eye-level', confidence: 0.44, detail: 'Vertical angle cues are weak, so the fallback stays at eye level.', tilt: 0 }; } function estimateDOF(focus, shotSize, faceAnalysis, poseAnalysis) { const { centerSharpness, avgPeriphery, sharpnessRatio, overallSharpness, topSharpness, bottomSharpness, leftSharpness, rightSharpness, midBandSharpness, outerRingSharpness, centerBgRatio, centerFgRatio, midVsEdgeRatio, zoneVariance } = focus; const shotType = shotSize?.type || shotSize || ''; const hasFace = (faceAnalysis?.count ?? 0) > 0; const faceArea = faceAnalysis?.largestAreaRatio ?? 0; const isMacroShot = ['ECU', 'BCU', 'INSERT'].includes(shotType); const isCloseUp = ['CU', 'BCU', 'ECU', 'INSERT', 'MCU'].includes(shotType); const isWide = ['LS', 'ELS', 'Establishing'].includes(shotType); // ?? 1. Soft-focus / diffusion (everything uniformly low sharpness) ???????? // All zones are soft and sharpness is evenly distributed ??optical filter, fog, or haze if (overallSharpness < 3.8 && sharpnessRatio < 1.28 && zoneVariance < 2.5) { return { type: 'Soft-focus', confidence: clamp(0.58 + (3.8 - overallSharpness) * 0.07, 0.58, 0.82), detail: 'The whole frame is uniformly soft, which is more consistent with diffusion, haze, or soft-focus treatment.', focusPlane: 'pan-focus', separation: 0 }; } // ?? 2. Tilt-shift / Miniature effect ????????????????????????????????????? // Top AND bottom thirds are soft; full-width horizontal mid-band is the sharp plane const topSoft = topSharpness < centerSharpness * 0.60; const bottomSoft = bottomSharpness < centerSharpness * 0.60; const tiltScore = (topSoft ? 0.44 : 0) + (bottomSoft ? 0.44 : 0) + (midVsEdgeRatio > 1.5 ? 0.12 : 0); if (tiltScore >= 0.80 && sharpnessRatio > 1.28) { return { type: 'Tilt-shift', confidence: clamp(0.58 + tiltScore * 0.24, 0.58, 0.84), detail: 'A narrow horizontal sharp band with soft top and bottom regions fits a tilt-shift or miniature effect.', focusPlane: 'midground', separation: clamp((sharpnessRatio - 1) / 2, 0, 1) }; } // ?? 3. Macro (extreme close focus) ??????????????????????????????????????? // ECU/INSERT shot + extreme center/periphery difference + almost no periphery detail if (isMacroShot && sharpnessRatio > 2.7 && avgPeriphery < centerSharpness * 0.32) { return { type: 'Macro', confidence: clamp(0.62 + (sharpnessRatio - 2.7) * 0.07, 0.62, 0.90), detail: `Extreme close framing (${shotType}) with almost all sharpness concentrated at the center fits macro focus.`, focusPlane: 'foreground', separation: clamp((sharpnessRatio - 1) / 4, 0, 1) }; } // ?? 4. Focus plane determination ????????????????????????????????????????? // background-focused: top (BG region) is sharper than center // foreground-focused: center sharper than background // pan-focus: all equally sharp let focusPlane; if (topSharpness > centerSharpness * 1.18) { focusPlane = 'background'; } else if (sharpnessRatio < 1.14 && overallSharpness > 7.5) { focusPlane = 'pan-focus'; } else if (centerBgRatio > 1.30) { focusPlane = 'midground'; } else { focusPlane = 'foreground'; } // Separation: 0 = flat, 1 = maximum subject isolation const separation = clamp((sharpnessRatio - 1) / 2.6, 0, 1); // Portrait DOF: face present AND background is distinctly blurrier const portraitDOF = hasFace && centerBgRatio > 1.45; // ?? 5. Very-shallow ??????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Extreme center vs periphery gap, especially with a face (portrait bokeh) if ( sharpnessRatio > 2.1 && overallSharpness > 5.5 && (portraitDOF || isCloseUp || centerBgRatio > 1.9) ) { const conf = clamp(0.68 + (sharpnessRatio - 2.1) * 0.05 + (portraitDOF ? 0.06 : 0), 0.68, 0.93); return { type: 'Very-shallow', confidence: conf, detail: hasFace ? `The face is sharply isolated from the background by about ${Math.round(centerBgRatio * 10) / 10}:1, which fits very shallow portrait depth of field.` : `Center sharpness exceeds the periphery by about ${Math.round(sharpnessRatio * 10) / 10}:1, which fits very shallow depth of field.`, focusPlane, separation: clamp(separation + 0.08, 0, 1) }; } // ?? 6. Shallow ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Clear subject-background separation, noticeable background blur if (sharpnessRatio > 1.60 || (portraitDOF && sharpnessRatio > 1.30)) { const conf = clamp(0.60 + (sharpnessRatio - 1.60) * 0.09 + (portraitDOF ? 0.05 : 0), 0.60, 0.86); return { type: 'Shallow', confidence: conf, detail: hasFace ? 'The subject is clearly separated from the background, which fits shallow depth of field.' : `Noticeable sharpness separation (${Math.round(sharpnessRatio * 10) / 10}:1) indicates shallow depth of field.`, focusPlane, separation }; } // ?? 7. Deep focus ????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? // Uniform sharpness, high overall detail, wide or landscape shot if (sharpnessRatio < 1.14 && overallSharpness > 8.0) { const conf = clamp(0.64 + (overallSharpness - 8.0) * 0.025, 0.64, 0.84); return { type: 'Deep', confidence: conf, detail: `Sharpness stays broadly even across the frame (overall ${Math.round(overallSharpness * 10) / 10}), which fits deep focus.`, focusPlane: 'pan-focus', separation: 0 }; } // ?? 8. Soft overall (low detail but not uniform) ??????????????????????????? if (overallSharpness < 5.0 && sharpnessRatio < 1.35) { return { type: 'Soft-focus', confidence: 0.54, detail: 'Overall detail is low across the frame, which reads closer to a soft-focus look.', focusPlane: 'pan-focus', separation: 0 }; } // ?? 9. Moderate ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? if (sharpnessRatio > 1.18 || isCloseUp) { const conf = clamp(0.52 + (sharpnessRatio - 1.0) * 0.12, 0.52, 0.74); return { type: 'Moderate', confidence: conf, detail: 'The subject is somewhat sharper than the background, which fits moderate depth of field.', focusPlane, separation }; } // Default return { type: overallSharpness > 7 ? 'Deep' : 'Moderate', confidence: 0.50, detail: overallSharpness > 7 ? 'Overall sharpness stays fairly even, so the fallback leans toward deep focus.' : 'Depth cues are mixed, so the fallback stays at moderate depth of field.', focusPlane: overallSharpness > 7 ? 'pan-focus' : focusPlane, separation }; } function generateLocalCamera() { return { shotSize: 'MS', shotSizeConf: 0, shotSizeDetail: 'Local fallback', shotSizeMetrics: null, framing: 'Empty', lensType: 'Normal(35-60mm)', lensConf: 0, lensDetail: '', movement: 'Static', movementConf: 0, movementDetail: 'Fallback', angle: 'Eye-level', angleConf: 0, dof: 'Moderate', dofConf: 0, dofDetail: '', lightingType: 'Mixed', lightingCondition: 'Flat', lightingDirection: 'Front', lightingHardness: 'Mixed', lightingContrast: 'Medium', lightingMotivation: 'Studio', lightingSubtype: '', lightingColorTemp: 'Neutral', lightingColorTempK: 5500, lightingKeyFillRatio: 1.8, lightingRimStrength: 0, lightingMixedColorContrast: 0, lightingConf: 0, lightingDetail: 'Local fallback', lightingMetrics: null, composition: 'Rule-of-thirds', compositionConf: 0, compositionDetail: 'Local fallback', compositionMetrics: null }; } async function generateAIDescriptionsLegacy() { if (!isAIAvailable()) { showToast('API ?ㅺ? ?놁뼱 濡쒖뺄 ?대━?ㅽ떛 遺꾩꽍?쇰줈 ?꾪솚?⑸땲??'); for (let i = 0; i < scenes.length; i++) { const s = scenes[i]; try { s.camera = await analyzeFrameAdvanced(s); } catch(e) { s.camera = generateLocalCamera(); } s.description = generateLocalDescription(s); updateProgress(`濡쒖뺄 移대찓??遺꾩꽍 以?.. (${i+1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (i / scenes.length) * 15); } return; } for (let i = 0; i < scenes.length; i++) { const scene = scenes[i]; try { debugLog(`Scene ${i + 1}/${scenes.length} AI analysis requested (${scene.multiFrames ? '3-frame set' : 'single frame'})`); const headers = getApiHeaders(); debugLog(`API ?ㅻ뜑: ${Object.keys(headers).join(', ')} | claude.ai ?섍꼍: ${isClaudeAI}`); // Build image content ??send up to 3 frames for movement analysis const imageContents = []; if (scene.multiFrames && scene.multiFrames.length === 3) { const labels = ['Start frame', 'Middle frame', 'End frame']; scene.multiFrames.forEach((f, idx) => { imageContents.push({ type: 'text', text: labels[idx] }); imageContents.push({ type: 'image', source: { type: 'base64', media_type: 'image/jpeg', data: f.split(',')[1] } }); }); } else { imageContents.push({ type: 'text', text: 'Representative frame' }); imageContents.push({ type: 'image', source: { type: 'base64', media_type: 'image/jpeg', data: scene.image.split(',')[1] } }); } const systemPrompt = `?뱀떊? 20??寃쎈젰???쒕꽕留덊넗洹몃옒?쇱씠???곹솕 遺꾩꽍 ?꾨Ц媛?낅땲?? ShotBench ?숈닠 踰ㅼ튂留덊겕??8? ?쒕꽕留덊넗洹몃옒??遺꾨쪟 泥닿퀎瑜?湲곕컲?쇰줈 ?뺣? 遺꾩꽍?⑸땲?? 諛섎뱶???쒖닔 JSON留?異쒕젰?섏꽭?? 留덊겕?ㅼ슫 諛깊떛, ?ㅻ챸, 異붽? ?띿뒪???놁씠 JSON 媛앹껜留??묐떟?⑸땲??`; const analysisPrompt = `${scene.multiFrames ? '???λ㈃???쒖옉/以묎컙/??3媛??꾨젅?꾩엯?덈떎.' : '???λ㈃???ㅽ봽?덉엫?낅땲??'} ?λ㈃ 湲몄씠: ${scene.duration.toFixed(1)}珥? ?꾨옒 泥댄겕由ъ뒪?몃? ?쒖꽌?濡?遺꾩꽍?섍퀬, JSON?쇰줈留??묐떟?섏꽭?? ## STEP 1: SHOT SIZE (StudioBinder 遺꾨쪟) ???꾨젅?꾩뿉???몃Ъ/?쇱궗泥닿?
