(${j+1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (j / scenes.length) * 15); } return; } debugLog(`?λ㈃ ${i+1} AI 遺꾩꽍 ?ㅽ뙣: ${err.message}`, 'error'); debugLog('濡쒖뺄 ?대━?ㅽ떛 遺꾩꽍?쇰줈 ?泥댄빀?덈떎...', 'warn'); console.warn('AI description failed for scene', i, err); try { scene.camera = await analyzeFrameAdvanced(scene); } catch(e) { scene.camera = generateLocalCamera(); } scene.description = generateLocalDescription(scene); } updateProgress(`AI 移대찓??遺꾩꽍 以?.. (${i+1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (i / scenes.length) * 15); } } function buildSceneAIPrompts(scene) { const systemPrompt = [ 'You are an expert cinematography analyst.', 'Internally reason like a panel of specialists in cinematography: director of photography, gaffer, portrait-lighting photographer, colorist, composition coach, and camera operator.', 'Use standard film-language definitions.', 'Reply with exactly one JSON object and no markdown.' ].join(' '); const frameScope = scene.multiFrames && scene.multiFrames.length === 3 ? 'You are given three frames from the same scene in temporal order: start, middle, end.' : 'You are given one representative frame from the scene.'; const localEvidence = buildLocalEvidenceBlock(scene.localCameraAnalysis); const analysisPrompt = `${frameScope} Scene duration: ${scene.duration.toFixed(1)} seconds. Classify the scene with these rules: - Shot size: ECU, BCU, CU, MCU, MS, Cowboy, MLS, FS, LS, ELS, Establishing, INSERT. - Framing: Single, Two-shot, Three-shot, OTS, POV, Crowd, Empty. - Camera angle: Overhead, High, Eye-level, Shoulder-level, Low, Worms-eye, Dutch, Aerial. - Lens type: Ultra-wide(<16mm), Wide(16-35mm), Normal(35-60mm), Telephoto(60-135mm), Super-telephoto(>135mm), Macro. - Camera movement: Static, Pan, Whip-pan, Tilt, Push-in, Pull-out, Tracking, Trucking, Arc, Crane, Pedestal, Handheld, Steadicam, Zoom-in, Zoom-out, Dolly-zoom, Rack-focus, Drone. - Depth of field: Deep, Moderate, Shallow, Very-shallow. - Lighting type: Natural, Artificial, Mixed, Practical. - Lighting condition: High-key, Low-key, Silhouette, Chiaroscuro, Flat, Rembrandt. - Composition: Rule-of-thirds, Center-framed, Symmetrical, Leading-lines, Frame-within-frame, Negative-space, Golden-ratio. Decision guidance: - Shot size depends on how much of the subject or body is visible and where the frame crops the body. - Lens depends on field of view, perspective stretch or compression, and depth separation. - Movement should use the sequence of frames: distinguish pan/tilt from physical travel and zoom. - Camera angle depends on whether the viewpoint looks up, down, level, or intentionally tilted. - For lighting, internally cross-check source motivation, key direction on the subject, hardness/contrast, color temperature, and rim/backlight cues before deciding. - Use Rembrandt only when directional facial modeling is present; use Silhouette only when the subject reads substantially darker than the background or rim. - For composition, internally cross-check subject placement, balance/symmetry, geometric lines, enclosing frames, and negative space before choosing one label. - If composition is ambiguous, pick the strongest primary pattern and explain the evidence in composition_detail. - If the local heuristic evidence conflicts with your read, trust the images and explain the decisive cue. - Describe the narrative purpose in one short sentence. ${localEvidence} Return JSON only with this schema: { "description": "3-4 sentences describing subject, environment, mood, lighting, and dramatic purpose", "shot_size": "ECU|BCU|CU|MCU|MS|Cowboy|MLS|FS|LS|ELS|Establishing|INSERT", "shot_size_confidence": 0.0, "shot_size_detail": "brief evidence", "framing": "Single|Two-shot|Three-shot|OTS|POV|Crowd|Empty", "camera_angle": "Overhead|High|Eye-level|Shoulder-level|Low|Worms-eye|Dutch|Aerial", "angle_confidence": 0.0, "lens_type": "Ultra-wide(<16mm)|Wide(16-35mm)|Normal(35-60mm)|Telephoto(60-135mm)|Super-telephoto(>135mm)|Macro", "lens_confidence": 0.0, "lens_detail": "brief evidence", "camera_movement": "Static|Pan|Whip-pan|Tilt|Push-in|Pull-out|Tracking|Trucking|Arc|Crane|Pedestal|Handheld|Steadicam|Zoom-in|Zoom-out|Dolly-zoom|Rack-focus|Drone", "movement_confidence": 0.0, "movement_detail": "brief evidence", "camera_mechanism": "Tripod|Dolly|Steadicam|Gimbal|Handheld|Crane|Jib|Drone|Slider|Snorricam", "depth_of_field": "Deep|Moderate|Shallow|Very-shallow", "dof_confidence": 0.0, "dof_detail": "brief evidence", "lighting_type": "Natural|Artificial|Mixed|Practical", "lighting_condition": "High-key|Low-key|Silhouette|Chiaroscuro|Flat|Rembrandt", "lighting_confidence": 0.0, "lighting_direction": "Back|Top-left|Top|Top-right|Left|Right|Front|Bottom", "lighting_hardness": "Soft|Mixed|Hard", "lighting_contrast": "Low|Medium|High|Extreme", "lighting_color_temp": "Very-warm|Warm|Neutral|Cool|Very-cool", "lighting_motivation": "Window|Practical|Ambient|Sunlight|Studio|Mixed-source", "lighting_subtype": "|Split|Butterfly|Golden-hour|Blue-hour|Overcast|Rim-lit|Window-lit|Neon-mixed", "lighting_detail": "brief evidence", "composition": "Rule-of-thirds|Center-framed|Symmetrical|Leading-lines|Frame-within-frame|Negative-space|Golden-ratio", "composition_confidence": 0.0, "composition_detail": "brief evidence", "narrative_purpose": "one short sentence" }`; return { systemPrompt, analysisPrompt }; } async function generateAIDescriptions() { if (!isAIAvailable()) { showToast('API key is unavailable. Falling back to local analysis.'); for (let i = 0; i < scenes.length; i++) { const scene = scenes[i]; scene.camera = await getSceneLocalCamera(scene); scene.description = generateLocalDescription(scene); updateProgress(`Local camera analysis... (${i + 1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (i / scenes.length) * 15); } return; } for (let i = 0; i < scenes.length; i++) { const scene = scenes[i]; try { const localCamera = await getSceneLocalCamera(scene); debugLog(`Scene ${i + 1}/${scenes.length}: requesting AI analysis`, 'info'); const imageContents = []; if (scene.multiFrames && scene.multiFrames.length === 3) { const labels = ['Start frame', 'Middle frame', 'End frame']; scene.multiFrames.forEach((frame, index) => { imageContents.push({ type: 'text', text: labels[index] }); imageContents.push({ type: 'image', source: { type: 'base64', media_type: 'image/jpeg', data: frame.split(',')[1] } }); }); } else { imageContents.push({ type: 'text', text: 'Representative frame' }); imageContents.push({ type: 'image', source: { type: 'base64', media_type: 'image/jpeg', data: scene.image.split(',')[1] } }); } const { systemPrompt, analysisPrompt } = buildSceneAIPrompts(scene); const rawText = await callAI( systemPrompt, [...imageContents, { type: 'text', text: analysisPrompt }], 1500 ); debugLog(`Scene ${i + 1}: AI response received`, 'success'); try { const cleaned = rawText.replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim(); const parsed = JSON.parse(cleaned); scene.description = parsed.description || ''; const aiCamera = buildAICameraFromParsed(parsed); scene.camera = mergeCameraWithLocalEvidence(aiCamera, localCamera); debugLog(`Scene ${i + 1} analyzed: ${parsed.shot_size} / ${parsed.lens_type} / ${parsed.camera_movement}`, 'success'); } catch (parseErr) { scene.description = rawText; scene.camera = localCamera; } } catch (err) { const isNetworkError = err.message === 'Failed to fetch' || err.name === 'TypeError'; if (isNetworkError && i === 0) { showToast('AI request failed. Falling back to local analysis.'); for (let j = i; j < scenes.length; j++) { scenes[j].camera = await getSceneLocalCamera(scenes[j]); scenes[j].description = generateLocalDescription(scenes[j]); updateProgress(`Local camera analysis... (${j + 1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (j / scenes.length) * 15); } return; } debugLog(`Scene ${i + 1} AI analysis failed: ${err.message}`, 'error'); scene.camera = await getSceneLocalCamera(scene); scene.description = generateLocalDescription(scene); } updateProgress(`AI camera analysis... (${i + 1}/${scenes.length})`, 80 + (i / scenes.length) * 15); } } // Confidence indicator helper function confDot(conf) { if (conf === undefined || conf === null || conf === 0) return ''; const pct = Math.round(conf * 100); if (conf >= 0.8) return `<span style="color:#4dff88;font-size:9px;margin-left:4px;" title="?좊ː??${pct}%">??/span>`; if (conf >= 0.5) return `<span style="color:#ffd644;font-size:9px;margin-left:4px;" title="?좊ː??${pct}%">??/span>`; return `<span style="color:#ff6b6b;font-size:9px;margin-left:4px;" title="?좊ː??${pct}%">??/span>`; } function renderStoryboard() { const section = document.getElementById('storyboardSection'); section.classList.add('active'); // Stats document.getElementById('totalScenes').textContent = scenes.length; document.getElementById('totalDuration').textContent = currentMediaType === 'photo' ? 'PHOTO' : formatTime(videoDuration); const avgDur = scenes.length > 0 ? videoDuration / scenes.length : 0; document.getElementById('avgScene').textContent = currentMediaType === 'photo' ? 'STILL' : avgDur.toFixed(1) + 's'; // Timeline const timelineStrip = document.querySelector('.timeline-strip'); const timelineBar = document.getElementById('timelineBar'); if (timelineStrip) timelineStrip.style.display = currentMediaType === 'photo' ? '' : scenes.map((s, i) => { const widthPercent = (s.duration / timelineDuration) * 100; const color = colors[i % colors.length]; const handle = i < scenes.length - 1 ? `<div class="timeline-handle" data-index="${i}" title="寃쎄퀎 ?쒕옒洹몃줈 ?대룞"> <div class="tl-merge-btn" onclick="handleMergeBtnClick(event,${i})">???⑹튂湲?/div> </div>` : ''; return `<div class="timeline-segment" data-scene-index="${i}" style="width:${widthPercent}%;background:${color}" onclick="timelineSegmentClick(event,${i})" title="?λ㈃ ${s.index}: ${formatTimecode(s.startTime)}"> ${s.index}${handle} </div>`; }).join(''); initTimelineDrag(); initPlayhead(); // 鍮꾨뵒??timeupdate ???뚮젅?댄뿤???먮룞 ?대룞 const _vp = getVideoPlayer(); if (_vp && !_vp._tlListenerAdded) { _vp.addEventListener('timeupdate', () => { if (!_tlPhDrag) updatePlayhead(_vp.currentTime); }); _vp._tlListenerAdded = true; } // Scene cards const grid = document.getElementById('scenesGrid'); grid.innerHTML = scenes.map((s, i) => { const cam = s.camera || {}; return ` <div class="scene-card" style="animation-delay: ${i * 0.05}s"> <div class="scene-thumbnail" onclick="seekTo(${s.startTime})"> <img src="${s.image}" alt="?λ㈃ ${s.index}"> <div class="scene-number">SCENE ${s.index}</div> <div class="scene-timecode">${formatTimecode(s.startTime)}</div> ${i > 0 || (s.transition && s.transition !== 'cut') ? // 寃쎄퀎 ?쒕옒洹??곹깭 let _tlPhDrag = null; // ?뚮젅?댄뿤???쒕옒洹??곹깭 // ?? 寃쎄퀎 ?쒕옒洹??????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? function initTimelineDrag() { const bar = document.getElementById('timelineBar'); if (!bar) return; const startBoundaryDrag = (clientX, idx) => { const handle = bar.querySelector(`.timeline-handle[data-index="${idx}"]`); if (handle) handle.classList.add('dragging'); _tlDrag = { idx, handle, startX: clientX, barRect: document.getElementById('timelineBarWrap').getBoundingClientRect(), origEnd: scenes[idx].endTime }; const tooltip = document.getElementById('tlDragTooltip'); if (tooltip) tooltip.style.display = 'block'; }; bar.addEventListener('mousedown', e => { const handle = e.target.closest('.timeline-handle'); if (!handle) return; e.preventDefault(); startBoundaryDrag(e.touches[0].clientX, parseInt(handle.dataset.index)); }, { passive: false }); } function _tlApplyDrag(clientX) { if (!_tlDrag) return; const { idx, barRect, origEnd } = _tlDrag; const dx = clientX - _tlDrag.startX; const dt = (dx / barRect.width) * videoDuration; const MIN_LEN = 0.3; const newBoundary = Math.max( scenes[idx].startTime + MIN_LEN, Math.min(scenes[idx + 1].endTime - MIN_LEN, origEnd + dt) ); scenes[idx].endTime = newBoundary; scenes[idx].duration = newBoundary - scenes[idx].startTime; scenes[idx + 1].startTime = newBoundary; scenes[idx + 1].duration = scenes[idx + 1].endTime - newBoundary; // ?멸렇癒쇳듃 ?덈퉬 ?ㅼ떆媛??낅뜲?댄듃 const segs = document.querySelectorAll('.timeline-segment'); const totalDur = Math.max(videoDuration, 1); segs.forEach((seg, i) => { if (scenes[i]) seg.style.width = `${(scenes[i].duration / totalDur) * 100}%`; }); // 寃쎄퀎 ?쒓컙 ?댄똻 const tooltip = document.getElementById('tlDragTooltip'); if (tooltip) { const pct = (newBoundary / totalDur) * 100; tooltip.style.left = `${pct}%`; tooltip.style.display = 'block'; tooltip.textContent = formatTimecode(newBoundary); } } // ?? ?뚮젅?댄뿤????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? function updatePlayhead(time) { const ph = document.getElementById('tlPlayhead'); const wrap = document.getElementById('timelineBarWrap'); if (!ph || !wrap || !videoDuration) return; ph.classList.add('active'); const pct = Math.min(time / videoDuration, 1) * 100; ph.style.left = `${pct}%`; document.getElementById('tlPlayheadTime').textContent = formatTimecode(time); } function initPlayhead() { const ph = document.getElementById('tlPlayhead'); const wrap = document.getElementById('timelineBarWrap'); e.stopPropagation(); startPhDrag(e.clientX); }); ph.addEventListener('touchstart', e => { e.stopPropagation(); startPhDrag(e.touches[0].clientX); }, { passive: true }); // 鍮?怨듦컙 ?대┃?쇰줈???대룞 (遺꾪븷 紐⑤뱶?먯꽌??鍮꾪솢?? wrap.addEventListener('mousedown', e => { if (_tlSplitMode) return; const t = pct * videoDuration; seekTo(t); updatePlayhead(t); _tlPhDrag = { wrapRect: rect }; }); } function _phApplyDrag(clientX) { if (!_tlPhDrag || !videoDuration) return; const { wrapRect } = _tlPhDrag; const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, (clientX - wrapRect.left) / wrapRect.width)); const t = pct * videoDuration; updatePlayhead(t); const vp = getVideoPlayer(); if (vp) vp.currentTime = t; } // ?? 怨듯넻 ?대깽???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????? document.addEventListener('mousemove', e => { if (_tlDrag) _tlApplyDrag(e.clientX); if (_tlPhDrag) _phApplyDrag(e.clientX); }); document.addEventListener('touchmove', e => { if (_tlDrag) _tlApplyDrag(e.touches[0].clientX); if (_tlPhDrag) _phApplyDrag(e.touches[0].clientX); }, { passive: true }); document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { if (_tlDrag) { if (_tlDrag.handle) _tlDrag.handle.classList.remove('dragging'); const tooltip = document.getElementById('tlDragTooltip'); if (tooltip) tooltip.style.display = 'none'; _tlDrag = null; renderStoryboard(); } _tlPhDrag = null; }); document.addEventListener('touchend', () => { if (_tlDrag) { if (_tlDrag.handle) _tlDrag.handle.classList.remove('dragging'); const tooltip = document.getElementById('tlDragTooltip'); if (tooltip) tooltip.style.display = 'none'; _tlDrag = null; renderStoryboard(); } _tlPhDrag = null; }); function timelineSegmentClick(e, sceneIndex) { if (e.target.closest('.timeline-handle') || e.target.closest('#tlPlayhead') || e.target.closest('.tl-merge-btn')) return; } // ?? ?λ㈃ ?몄쭛: ?⑹튂湲?/ ?섎늻湲???????????????????????????????????????????? let _splitSceneIdx = -1; let _tlSplitMode = false; function _reindexScenes() { scenes.forEach((s, i) => { s.index = i + 1; }); } // 鍮꾨뵒?ㅼ뿉???뱀젙 ?쒓컙???꾨젅?꾩쓣 罹≪쿂 (dataURL 諛섑솚) async function captureFrameAtTime(time) { const vp = getVideoPlayer(); if (!vp || !vp.videoWidth) return null; const wasPaused = vp.paused; const prevTime = vp.currentTime; if (!wasPaused) vp.pause(); return new Promise((resolve) => { const onSeeked = () => { try { const c = document.createElement('canvas'); c.width = 320; c.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(320 * vp.videoHeight / vp.videoWidth)); c.getContext('2d').drawImage(vp, 0, 0, c.width, c.height); resolve(c.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.82)); } catch (_) { resolve(null); } // ?먮옒 ?꾩튂濡?蹂듭썝 vp.currentTime = prevTime; if (!wasPaused) vp.play().catch(() => {}); }; vp.addEventListener('seeked', onSeeked, { once: true }); vp.currentTime = Math.max(0, Math.min(time, (vp.duration || time) - 0.01)); }); } // ?λ㈃ i ? i+1 ?⑹튂湲?function mergeScenes(i) { if (i < 0 || i >= scenes.length - 1) return; const a = scenes[i]; const b = scenes[i + 1]; a.endTime = b.endTime; a.duration = a.endTime - a.startTime; if (!a.camera && b.camera) a.camera = b.camera; if (b.multiFrames?.length) { a.multiFrames = [...(a.multiFrames || []), ...b.multiFrames]; } scenes.splice(i + 1, 1); _reindexScenes(); renderStoryboard(); showToast(`?λ㈃ ${i + 1}怨?${i + 2}瑜??⑹낀?듬땲??`); } // ?λ㈃ i 瑜?splitTime ?꾩튂?먯꽌 遺꾪븷 async function splitSceneAtTime(i, splitTime) { if (i < 0 || i >= scenes.length) return; const s = scenes[i]; const MIN_DUR = 0.5; if (splitTime <= s.startTime + MIN_DUR || splitTime >= s.endTime - MIN_DUR) { showToast(`遺꾪븷 ?꾩튂媛 ?덈Т 媛?μ옄由ъ뿉 ?덉뒿?덈떎 (?묐걹 ${MIN_DUR}珥??댁긽 ?꾩슂)`); return; } closeSplitDialog(); // 遺꾪븷 吏??吏곹썑 ?꾨젅??罹≪쿂 ?쒕룄 let newImage = s.image; try { const captured = await captureFrameAtTime(splitTime + Math.min((s.endTime - splitTime) * 0.08, 0.5)); if (captured) newImage = captured; } catch (_) {} const newScene = { index: s.index + 1, startTime: splitTime, endTime: s.endTime, duration: s.endTime - splitTime, keyframeTime: splitTime, image: newImage, multiFrames: [], transition: 'cut', score: s.score, description: s.description, brightness: s.brightness, colorDominant: s.colorDominant, camera: s.camera ? { ...s.camera } : null, }; s.endTime = splitTime; s.duration = splitTime - s.startTime; scenes.splice(i + 1, 0, newScene); _reindexScenes(); renderStoryboard(); showToast(`?λ㈃ ${i + 1}??${formatTimecode(splitTime)}?먯꽌 遺꾪븷?덉뒿?덈떎.`); } function splitSceneAtMidpoint(i) { if (i < 0 || i >= scenes.length) return; const s = scenes[i]; splitSceneAtTime(i, (s.startTime + s.endTime) / 2); } function splitSceneAtPlayhead(i) { const vp = getVideoPlayer();
